# Text File Combiner Architecture
This document summarizes the current 1.1.0 architecture after the Phase 1, Phase 1b, and diagnostics refactors included in this full archive.

## Main layers

### UI layer
The WinForms UI is split across `MainForm` partial classes:
- `MainForm.cs` — shared fields, constructor, layout, and control creation.
- `MainForm.Combine.cs` — combine-tab event handlers and combine orchestration.
- `MainForm.Extract.cs` — extract-tab event handlers and extraction orchestration.
- `MainForm.Settings.cs` — settings/about actions and safety-summary display.
- `MainForm.Status.cs` — status text, diagnostics formatting, and process launch helpers.
- `MainForm.DragDrop.cs` — drag/drop routing.

### Core models
Shared DTOs are under `Models/`.

### Protocol layer
CPTF/1 HumanReadable is the human-oriented text protocol. CPTF/2 LengthDelimited is the reconstruction-oriented protocol with byte lengths, parser rules, SHA-256, and optional `.ico` / `.png` Base64 assets.

### Shared services and utilities
- `SupportedFilePolicy` — supported text/binary file rules.
- `HashService` — SHA-256 hashing.
- `TextContentUtility` — newline and text helper methods.
- `AppVersion` — product/version strings.
- `AppConstants` — protocol constants.

## Refactor guardrails
- Keep DTO/model properties synchronized with all usage sites.
- Preserve C# escape sequences carefully: `"\"` for a string backslash and `'\'` for a char backslash.
- Build after each focused refactor.

# TextFileCombiner.Cli commands

TextFileCombiner.Cli 1.2.0 supports CPTF/2 LengthDelimited v3.4.1.

## Commands

```bash
TextFileCombiner.Cli combine --source <folder-or-zip> --output <file> [--protocol cptf1|cptf2] [--include-binary-assets] [--source-kind auto|folder|zip] [--json]
TextFileCombiner.Cli extract --input <combined-file> --output <folder> [--overwrite] [--preserve-root] [--newline preserve|windows|unix] [--json]
TextFileCombiner.Cli validate --input <combined-file> [--output <validation-root>] [--json]
TextFileCombiner.Cli extract-one --input <combined-file> --path <relative-path-or-folder> --output <folder> [--index-mode sequential|auto-indexed|indexed-only] [--overwrite] [--validate-only] [--json]
```

## Examples

```bash
TextFileCombiner.Cli combine --source ./src --output ./project.cptf2.txt --protocol cptf2 --include-binary-assets --json
TextFileCombiner.Cli validate --input ./project.cptf2.txt --json
TextFileCombiner.Cli extract --input ./project.cptf2.txt --output ./restored --overwrite --json
TextFileCombiner.Cli extract-one --input ./project.cptf2.txt --path docs/CLI.md --output ./out --index-mode auto-indexed --json
TextFileCombiner.Cli extract-one --input ./project.cptf2.txt --path TextFileCombiner.Core/Services --output ./out --index-mode indexed-only --json
```

## Index modes

```text
sequential     scan CPTF/2 entries and extract only matching selected file/folder
auto-indexed   allow embedded-index aware workflows while still verifying real file entries
indexed-only   require an embedded index to be present; fail if the input is not indexed
```

## Notes

- `--path` is a path inside the combined file, not an absolute Windows path.
- If `--path` is a folder, all files below that folder are extracted.
- CPTF/2 content is read by exact `byteLength` and verified with SHA-256.

END FILE

# Combined Project Text File Export Format
Text File Combiner 1.1.0 supports two protocols:
1. `CPTF/1 HumanReadable`
2. `CPTF/2 LengthDelimited`
The selected protocol affects only the Combine tab. Extract auto-detects the protocol.

## CPTF/1 HumanReadable
This is the original readable protocol. It is text-only and keeps the existing visual output features:
- project structure tree
- folder headers
- file headers
- file number
- extension tag
- declared line count
- `RltvPath`
- `FullPath`
- line-count based reconstruction
CPTF/1 intentionally does not include binary files.

## CPTF/2 LengthDelimited
The first line is:

```text
CPTF/2

```
`BEGIN FILE` and `BEGIN CONTENT` are structural start markers only. The parser must not search file content for `END CONTENT`. It reads exactly `fileMetadata.byteLength` bytes after `BEGIN CONTENT`.

### Text file metadata

```json
{
  "fileKind": "text",
  "contentEncoding": "utf-8-plain-text",
  "byteLength": 1234,
  "sha256": "..."
}

```
For text files, `sha256` is computed over the UTF-8 bytes written in the content block.

### Binary asset metadata
Binary assets are optional and supported only when the Settings option **Include .ico and .png files in CPTF/2 exports** is enabled.
Supported binary extensions in 1.1.0:
- `.ico`
- `.png`

```json
{
  "fileKind": "binary",
  "contentEncoding": "base64",
  "originalByteLength": 4286,
  "byteLength": 5716,
  "encodedByteLength": 5716,
  "sha256": "..."
}

```
For binary files:
- `byteLength` / `encodedByteLength` is the length of the Base64 UTF-8 content block.
- `sha256` is computed over the decoded original binary bytes.
- extraction decodes Base64, verifies `originalByteLength`, verifies `sha256`, and writes bytes using `File.WriteAllBytes`.

## Extraction auto-detection

```text
if first line is CPTF/2:
    use CPTF/2 LengthDelimited parser
else:
    use CPTF/1 HumanReadable parser

```

# CPTF/2 v3.4.1 Methodology Integration

CPTF/2 v3.4.1 is a length-delimited combined-project format.

```text
Markers define structure outside payloads.
byteLength defines payload size.
SHA-256 proves payload integrity.
Path validation gates extraction.
```

The embedded index extension is optional and non-authoritative:

```text
The index finds candidates.
The real file entry proves truth.
```

This document describes the active CPTF/2 v3.4.1 length-delimited methodology used by Text File Combiner 1.2.0.

END FILE

# Development Notes

## Build gates
Run after each meaningful refactor:

```powershell
dotnet clean .\TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10.csproj
dotnet build .\TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10.csproj

```

## C# escaping rules
When generating or patching C# source, preserve escape sequences exactly:

```csharp
'\'   // backslash char
'
'   // LF char
'
'   // CR char
"\"   // string containing one backslash
"
"   // string containing LF
"
" // string containing CRLF

```
Never emit:

```csharp
''

```
That is an invalid C# char literal and will cause cascading compile errors.

## Recommended smoke tests
- CPTF/1 combine/extract text project.
- CPTF/2 combine/extract text project.
- CPTF/2 marker-collision text content.
- CPTF/2 `.ico` round-trip hash match.
- CPTF/2 `.png` round-trip hash match.
- CPTF/2 binary-assets disabled behavior.

# Error Handling Strategy
Text File Combiner reports expected operational errors without crashing.

## Core
Core throws typed or standard exceptions for expected conditions, including malformed CPTF files, invalid paths, duplicate paths, SHA-256 mismatches, missing files, access denied, locked files, and invalid settings.
`HandledErrorService` converts these exceptions into `HandledErrorInfo` with:
- title
- user-facing message
- category
- detail
- handled/unexpected flag

## CLI
CLI catches command exceptions, reports user-friendly text or JSON, and exits with:

```text
2 = handled command failure
3 = unexpected failure

```

## WinForms
WinForms routes caught exceptions through `ShowHandledError`, updates the active tab status, appends extract-log diagnostics, and shows a warning/error dialog.
Global handlers are registered for startup, UI thread, unobserved task, and AppDomain exceptions.

# Packaging Text File Combiner 1.2.0

## Build

```powershell
dotnet clean .\TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10.sln
dotnet restore .\TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10.sln
dotnet build .\TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10.sln -c Release

```

## Run tests

```powershell
dotnet run --project .\TextFileCombiner.Tests\TextFileCombiner.Tests.csproj -c Release

```

## Run benchmarks

```powershell
dotnet run --project .\TextFileCombiner.Benchmarks\TextFileCombiner.Benchmarks.csproj -c Release -- --threshold-mode relaxed --json .\benchmark-results.json

```

## Publish WinForms

```powershell
dotnet publish .\TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10\TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10.csproj -c Release -r win-x64 --self-contained false -o .\publish\TextFileCombiner-1.2.0\WinForms

```

## Publish CLI

```powershell
dotnet publish .\TextFileCombiner.Cli\TextFileCombiner.Cli.csproj -c Release -r win-x64 --self-contained false -o .\publish\TextFileCombiner-1.2.0\CLI

```

## Create release zip

```powershell
Compress-Archive -Path .\publish\TextFileCombiner-1.2.0\* -DestinationPath .\publish\TextFileCombiner-1.2.0.zip -Force

```

# Text File Combiner 1.2.0

Text File Combiner creates, validates, and restores combined project files in CPTF/1 and CPTF/2 formats.

## Main capabilities

- Combine a project folder or ZIP archive into one combined project text file.
- Restore a complete combined project.
- Validate combined project files before extraction.
- Use CPTF/2 LengthDelimited output with exact byte-length payloads and SHA-256 verification.
- Include supported binary assets in CPTF/2 output when enabled.
- Extract a selected file or all files below a selected folder from CPTF/2 combined files.
- Use the WinForms Help menu to view release notes, CLI commands, license text, and the runtime docs folder.

## Protocols

- `CPTF/1 HumanReadable` keeps the original readable text-only export format.
- `CPTF/2 LengthDelimited` is the current reconstruction-oriented format.
- Current CPTF/2 protocol version: `3.4.1`.
- Current parser profile: `length-delimited`.

## Key documents

- `RELEASE_NOTES.md` - canonical release history used by Help -> About -> Release notes.
- `CLI_COMMANDS.md` - canonical CLI command help used by Help -> CLI commands.
- `LICENSE.md` - canonical license text used by Help -> About -> License.
- `PACKAGING.md` - build, test, benchmark, publish, and packaging notes.
- `ERROR_HANDLING.md` - expected error-handling behavior for Core, CLI, and WinForms.
- `CPTF2_v3.4.1_Methodology.md` - CPTF/2 length-delimited parsing and embedded-index methodology.

## License

See `LICENSE.md`.

# Changelog

## 1.2.0

### Added
- Added CPTF/2 protocol version `3.4.1` with the `length-delimited` parser profile.
- Added top-level CPTF/2 `protocolVersion`, `parserProfile`, content/internal file counts, generator metadata, and embedded-index metadata.
- Added non-authoritative embedded index generation under `__cptf__/index.entryOffset_{offset20}.cptf2idx.json`.
- Added strict length-delimited CPTF/2 parsing that reads payloads by exact `byteLength` instead of marker scanning.
- Added final `END CPTF` validation and trailing-byte rejection for CPTF/2 files.
- Added enhanced validation/reporting fields for protocol/profile, content/internal counts, embedded-index presence, path issues, duplicate paths, Base64 payloads, and SHA-256 verification.
- Added CLI `extract-one` support for selected file/folder extraction from CPTF/2 combined files.
- Added `--index-mode sequential|auto-indexed|indexed-only` for selected-path extraction.
- Added WinForms `CPTF/2` menu and `Indexed extract selected path...` workflow.
- Added selected-path picker UI that reads file metadata from a CPTF/2 combined file and displays a file/folder tree.
- Added tooltips/hints for indexed extraction fields and index modes.
- Added output-folder auto-fill for selected-path extraction.
- Added Help -> CLI commands, backed by `docs/CLI_COMMANDS.md`.
- Added Help -> Open docs folder.
- Updated Help -> About tabs so Release notes and License load from files in the `docs` folder.

### Changed
- Updated application, assembly, file, and informational versions to `1.2.0`.
- Consolidated user-facing release notes into `docs/RELEASE_NOTES.md`.
- Moved CLI command help content into `docs/CLI_COMMANDS.md`.
- Moved license text into `docs/LICENSE.md`.
- Configured WinForms build output to copy documentation files under `bin/.../docs`.
- Renamed the indexed extraction UI field from `Relative path` to `Path inside combined file` for clarity.

### Fixed
- Fixed selected-path extraction so selecting a file extracts only that file and selecting a folder extracts only files below that folder.
- Fixed CLI commands dialog opening with all text selected/highlighted.
- Restored Help -> About tabs: About, Release notes, License.
- Fixed License tab missing-document message by adding `docs/LICENSE.md` and copying it to output.
- Cleaned up historical patch notes and documented remaining MainForm cleanup targets.

- Added wrapping behavior to summary panels to reduce horizontal scrolling caused by long source/output paths.

### Changed

## 1.1.0

### Added
- Added Phase 6 UX/diagnostics: combine output size, combined-file SHA-256, text/binary file counts, and richer validate-only result reporting.
- Added selectable combine output protocol in Settings:
  - `CPTF/1 HumanReadable`
  - `CPTF/2 LengthDelimited`
- Added `CPTF/2 LengthDelimited` export format with:
  - `CPTF/2` magic header
  - embedded parser rules
  - JSON manifest
  - JSON file metadata
  - byte-length-delimited content blocks
  - SHA-256 verification
- Added automatic extract protocol detection:
  - files starting with `CPTF/2` use the CPTF/2 parser
  - all other combined files use the CPTF/1 HumanReadable parser
- Added optional binary asset support for CPTF/2 exports.
- Added on-demand Settings option: `Include .ico and .png files in CPTF/2 exports`.
- Added Base64 encoding/decoding for supported CPTF/2 binary files.
- Added binary metadata fields for CPTF/2 entries:
  - `fileKind`
  - `contentEncoding`
  - `originalByteLength`
  - `encodedByteLength`
  - `sha256`
- Added Phase 1 architecture cleanup files for constants, versioning, models, supported-file policy, hashing, and text helpers.

### Changed
- Added Phase 7 cleanup documentation: architecture overview, development notes, and centralized constant/version comments.
- Renamed the original readable protocol in the UI/documentation to `CPTF/1 HumanReadable`.
- Updated About dialog to version `1.1.0`.
- Updated assembly/file/informational versions to `1.1.0`.
- Centralized version text in `AppVersion`.
- Centralized protocol constants in `AppConstants`.
- Moved shared DTOs/models out of combiner/extractor files.
- Centralized supported file/binary extension rules in `SupportedFilePolicy`.
- Centralized SHA-256 hashing in `HashService`.
- Added `MainForm` partial-class scaffolding for future UI split.
- Moved MainForm behavior into partial class files for combine, extract, settings, status, and drag/drop responsibilities.

### Compatibility
- CPTF/1 HumanReadable remains text-only and preserves the original readable export/reconstruction behavior.
- CPTF/2 binary asset support is intentionally limited to `.ico` and `.png` in this release.
- Extract remains backward compatible with existing CPTF/1 HumanReadable files.

## 1.0.0

### Added
- Initial project combine/extract workflow.
- Folder and ZIP input support.
- Human-readable combined text export.
- Extraction validation and validate-only mode.
- Duplicate path and path safety checks.
- Configurable file count and size safety limits.
- System, Light, and Dark theme options.
- Proprietary/private license and ownership metadata.

using System.Security.Cryptography;
using System.Text.Json;
using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.Cli;

internal static class Program
{
    private const int ExitSuccess = 0;
    private const int ExitUsageError = 1;
    private const int ExitCommandFailed = 2;
    private const int ExitUnexpectedError = 3;
    private static readonly string Version = AppVersion.Version;
    private static int Main(string[] args)
    {
        try
        {
            CliCommandLine commandLine = CliCommandLine.Parse(args);
            if (commandLine.ShowHelp) { WriteHelp(); return ExitSuccess; }
            if (commandLine.ShowVersion) { Console.WriteLine("TextFileCombiner.Cli " + Version); return ExitSuccess; }
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(commandLine.Command)) { WriteUsageError("Missing command. Use --help for usage.", commandLine.JsonOutput); return ExitUsageError; }
            return commandLine.Command.ToLowerInvariant() switch
            {
                "combine" => RunCombine(commandLine),
                "extract" => RunExtract(commandLine),
                "validate" => RunValidate(commandLine),
                "extract-one" => RunExtractOne(commandLine),
                _ => UnknownCommand(commandLine)
            };
        }
        catch (CliUsageException ex)
        {
            WriteUsageError(ex.Message, jsonOutput: false);
            return ExitUsageError;
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            HandledErrorInfo error = HandledErrorService.FromException(ex, "CLI startup");
            WriteHandledError(error, new { exceptionType = ex.GetType().Name }, jsonOutput: false);
            return error.IsHandled ? ExitCommandFailed : ExitUnexpectedError;
        }
    }

    private static int RunCombine(CliCommandLine commandLine)
    {
        string? source = commandLine.GetOption("source");
        string? output = commandLine.GetOption("output");
        string protocol = commandLine.GetOption("protocol") ?? "cptf2";
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(source)) { WriteUsageError("combine requires --source <folder-or-zip>.", commandLine.JsonOutput); return ExitUsageError; }
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(output)) { WriteUsageError("combine requires --output <combined-file>.", commandLine.JsonOutput); return ExitUsageError; }
        if (!IsSupportedProtocol(protocol)) { WriteUsageError("Unsupported protocol. Use --protocol cptf1 or --protocol cptf2.", commandLine.JsonOutput); return ExitUsageError; }
        AppSettings settings = CreateSettings(commandLine, protocol);
        InputSourceKind inputSourceKind = ResolveRequestedInputSourceKind(commandLine.GetOption("source-kind"));
        try
        {
            CombineResult result = ProjectFileCombiner.CombineProjectTextFiles(inputSourceKind, source, output, settings);
            byte[] outputBytes = File.ReadAllBytes(result.OutputFilePath);
            object details = new { command = "combine", protocol = ProjectFileCombiner.GetOutputProtocolText(result.OutputProtocol), protocolVersion = result.OutputProtocol == CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol.Cptf2LengthDelimited ? AppConstants.Cptf2ProtocolVersion : string.Empty, parserProfile = result.OutputProtocol == CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol.Cptf2LengthDelimited ? AppConstants.Cptf2ParserProfile : string.Empty, embeddedIndexPresent = result.OutputProtocol == CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol.Cptf2LengthDelimited && AppConstants.Cptf2GenerateEmbeddedIndexByDefault, source = result.ResolvedSourcePath, sourceKind = result.ResolvedInputSourceKind.ToString(), output = result.OutputFilePath, combinedFileCount = result.CombinedFileCount, contentFileCount = result.CombinedFileCount, internalFileCount = result.OutputProtocol == CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol.Cptf2LengthDelimited && AppConstants.Cptf2GenerateEmbeddedIndexByDefault ? 1 : 0, textFileCount = result.TextFileCount, binaryFileCount = result.BinaryFileCount, encodingWarningCount = result.EncodingWarningCount, outputFileByteLength = outputBytes.LongLength, outputFileSha256 = ComputeSha256Hex(outputBytes), durationMs = Math.Round(result.Duration.TotalMilliseconds, 3) };
            WriteJsonOrText(true, "Combine completed successfully.", details, commandLine.JsonOutput);
            return ExitSuccess;
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            HandledErrorInfo error = HandledErrorService.FromException(ex, "Combine");
            WriteHandledError(error, new { command = "combine", source, output, protocol, exceptionType = ex.GetType().Name }, commandLine.JsonOutput);
            return error.IsHandled ? ExitCommandFailed : ExitUnexpectedError;
        }
    }

    private static int RunExtract(CliCommandLine commandLine)
    {
        string? input = commandLine.GetOption("input");
        string? output = commandLine.GetOption("output");
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(input)) { WriteUsageError("extract requires --input <combined-file>.", commandLine.JsonOutput); return ExitUsageError; }
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(output)) { WriteUsageError("extract requires --output <folder>.", commandLine.JsonOutput); return ExitUsageError; }
        RestoreOptions options = CreateRestoreOptions(commandLine, validateOnly: false);
        return RunExtractOrValidate("extract", input, output, options, commandLine.JsonOutput);
    }

    private static int RunValidate(CliCommandLine commandLine)
    {
        string? input = commandLine.GetOption("input");
        string? output = commandLine.GetOption("output");
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(input)) { WriteUsageError("validate requires --input <combined-file>.", commandLine.JsonOutput); return ExitUsageError; }
        string validationOutputFolder = !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(output) ? output : Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), "TextFileCombiner.Cli.Validate", Guid.NewGuid().ToString("N"));
        RestoreOptions options = CreateRestoreOptions(commandLine, validateOnly: true);
        return RunExtractOrValidate("validate", input, validationOutputFolder, options, commandLine.JsonOutput);
    }

    private static int RunExtractOne(CliCommandLine commandLine)
    {
        string? input = commandLine.GetOption("input");
        string? requestedPath = commandLine.GetOption("path") ?? commandLine.GetOption("file");
        string? output = commandLine.GetOption("output");
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(input)) { WriteUsageError("extract-one requires --input <combined-file>.", commandLine.JsonOutput); return ExitUsageError; }
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(requestedPath)) { WriteUsageError("extract-one requires --path <relative-path>.", commandLine.JsonOutput); return ExitUsageError; }
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(output)) { WriteUsageError("extract-one requires --output <folder>.", commandLine.JsonOutput); return ExitUsageError; }
        RestoreOptions options = CreateRestoreOptions(commandLine, validateOnly: commandLine.HasFlag("validate-only"));
        options.IndexMode = ParseIndexMode(commandLine.GetOption("index-mode"));
        List<object> milestones = new List<object>();
        Progress<ExtractMilestone> progress = new Progress<ExtractMilestone>(milestone => milestones.Add(new { status = milestone.Status.ToString(), message = milestone.Message, detail = milestone.Detail }));
        try
        {
            RestoreResult result = Cptf2IndexedExtractor.ExtractOne(input, requestedPath, output, options, progress);
            object details = new
            {
                command = "extract-one",
                input,
                requestedPath,
                output,
                validateOnly = options.ValidateOnly,
                indexMode = options.IndexMode.ToString(),
                protocol = result.ProtocolName,
                protocolVersion = string.Equals(result.ProtocolName, AppConstants.Cptf2LengthDelimitedName, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? AppConstants.Cptf2ProtocolVersion : string.Empty,
                parserProfile = string.Equals(result.ProtocolName, AppConstants.Cptf2LengthDelimitedName, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? AppConstants.Cptf2ParserProfile : string.Empty,
                filesCreated = result.FilesCreated,
                filesSkipped = result.FilesSkipped,
                filesPlanned = result.FilesPlanned,
                totalFileCount = result.TotalFileCount,
                textFileCount = result.TextFileCount,
                binaryFileCount = result.BinaryFileCount,
                sha256VerificationCount = result.Sha256VerificationCount,
                warnings = result.Warnings.ToArray(),
                milestones = milestones.ToArray()
            };
            WriteJsonOrText(true, "Extract-one completed successfully.", details, commandLine.JsonOutput);
            return ExitSuccess;
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            HandledErrorInfo error = HandledErrorService.FromException(ex, "extract-one");
            WriteHandledError(error, new { command = "extract-one", input, requestedPath, output, indexMode = options.IndexMode.ToString(), exceptionType = ex.GetType().Name, milestones = milestones.ToArray() }, commandLine.JsonOutput);
            return error.IsHandled ? ExitCommandFailed : ExitUnexpectedError;
        }
    }

    private static int RunExtractOrValidate(string command, string input, string output, RestoreOptions options, bool jsonOutput)
    {
        List<object> milestones = new List<object>();
        Progress<ExtractMilestone> progress = new Progress<ExtractMilestone>(milestone => milestones.Add(new { status = milestone.Status.ToString(), message = milestone.Message, detail = milestone.Detail }));
        try
        {
            RestoreResult result = ProjectFileExtractor.ExtractProjectFiles(input, output, options, progress);
            object details = new { command, input, output, validateOnly = options.ValidateOnly, protocol = result.ProtocolName, protocolVersion = string.Equals(result.ProtocolName, AppConstants.Cptf2LengthDelimitedName, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? AppConstants.Cptf2ProtocolVersion : string.Empty, parserProfile = string.Equals(result.ProtocolName, AppConstants.Cptf2LengthDelimitedName, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? AppConstants.Cptf2ParserProfile : string.Empty, embeddedIndexPresent = false, filesCreated = result.FilesCreated, filesSkipped = result.FilesSkipped, directoriesCreated = result.DirectoriesCreated, filesPlanned = result.FilesPlanned, totalFileCount = result.TotalFileCount, contentFileCount = result.TotalFileCount, internalFileCount = 0, textFileCount = result.TextFileCount, binaryFileCount = result.BinaryFileCount, sha256VerificationCount = result.Sha256VerificationCount, warnings = result.Warnings.ToArray(), milestones = milestones.ToArray() };
            WriteJsonOrText(true, options.ValidateOnly ? "Validation completed successfully." : "Extraction completed successfully.", details, jsonOutput);
            return ExitSuccess;
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            HandledErrorInfo error = HandledErrorService.FromException(ex, command);
            WriteHandledError(error, new { command, input, output, validateOnly = options.ValidateOnly, exceptionType = ex.GetType().Name, milestones = milestones.ToArray() }, jsonOutput);
            return error.IsHandled ? ExitCommandFailed : ExitUnexpectedError;
        }
    }

    private static AppSettings CreateSettings(CliCommandLine commandLine, string protocol)
    {
        AppSettings settings = new AppSettings();
        settings.OutputProtocol = string.Equals(protocol, "cptf2", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol.Cptf2LengthDelimited : CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol.Cptf1HumanReadable;
        settings.IncludeImageAssetsInCptf2 = commandLine.HasFlag("include-binary-assets");
        settings.MaxFileCount = GetIntOption(commandLine, "max-files", settings.MaxFileCount, 1);
        settings.MaxTotalSizeMb = GetIntOption(commandLine, "max-total-mb", settings.MaxTotalSizeMb, 1);
        settings.MaxSingleFileSizeMb = GetIntOption(commandLine, "max-single-file-mb", settings.MaxSingleFileSizeMb, 1);
        return settings;
    }

    private static RestoreOptions CreateRestoreOptions(CliCommandLine commandLine, bool validateOnly)
    {
        RestoreOptions options = new RestoreOptions();
        options.ValidateOnly = validateOnly;
        options.OverwriteExistingFiles = commandLine.HasFlag("overwrite");
        options.PreserveRootFolder = commandLine.HasFlag("preserve-root");
        options.NewLineMode = ParseNewLineMode(commandLine.GetOption("newline") ?? "windows");
        return options;
    }

    private static RestoreIndexMode ParseIndexMode(string? value)
    {
        return (value ?? "auto-indexed").ToLowerInvariant() switch
        {
            "sequential" => RestoreIndexMode.Sequential,
            "auto" or "auto-indexed" => RestoreIndexMode.AutoIndexed,
            "indexed" or "indexed-only" => RestoreIndexMode.IndexedOnly,
            _ => throw new CliUsageException("Unsupported --index-mode. Use sequential, auto-indexed, or indexed-only.")
        };
    }

    private static RestoreNewLineMode ParseNewLineMode(string newline) => newline.ToLowerInvariant() switch { "preserve" => RestoreNewLineMode.PreserveCombinedFileNewLines, "windows" => RestoreNewLineMode.WindowsCrLf, "crlf" => RestoreNewLineMode.WindowsCrLf, "unix" => RestoreNewLineMode.UnixLf, "lf" => RestoreNewLineMode.UnixLf, _ => throw new CliUsageException("Unsupported --newline. Use preserve, windows, or unix.") };
    private static int GetIntOption(CliCommandLine commandLine, string optionName, int defaultValue, int minimumValue) { string? valueText = commandLine.GetOption(optionName); if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(valueText)) return defaultValue; if (!int.TryParse(valueText, out int value) || value < minimumValue) throw new CliUsageException("Invalid --" + optionName + " value. Expected an integer >= " + minimumValue + "."); return value; }
    private static InputSourceKind ResolveRequestedInputSourceKind(string? sourceKind) { if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(sourceKind) || string.Equals(sourceKind, "auto", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return InputSourceKind.Auto; if (string.Equals(sourceKind, "folder", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return InputSourceKind.Folder; if (string.Equals(sourceKind, "zip", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) || string.Equals(sourceKind, "ziparchive", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return InputSourceKind.ZipArchive; throw new CliUsageException("Unsupported --source-kind. Use auto, folder, or zip."); }
    private static int UnknownCommand(CliCommandLine commandLine) { WriteUsageError("Unknown command: " + commandLine.Command, commandLine.JsonOutput); return ExitUsageError; }
    private static bool IsSupportedProtocol(string protocol) => string.Equals(protocol, "cptf1", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) || string.Equals(protocol, "cptf2", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    private static string ComputeSha256Hex(byte[] bytes) => Convert.ToHexString(SHA256.HashData(bytes)).ToLowerInvariant();
    private static void WriteHandledError(HandledErrorInfo error, object? details, bool jsonOutput)
    {
        if (jsonOutput)
        {
            Console.WriteLine(JsonSerializer.Serialize(new
            {
                success = false,
                message = error.Message,
                error = new
                {
                    title = error.Title,
                    category = error.Category,
                    handled = error.IsHandled,
                    detail = error.Detail
                },
                details
            }, new JsonSerializerOptions { WriteIndented = true }));
            return;
        }
        Console.Error.WriteLine(error.Title);
        Console.Error.WriteLine(error.Message);
        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(error.Detail))
        {
            Console.Error.WriteLine(error.Detail);
        }
    }

    private static void WriteUsageError(string message, bool jsonOutput) { WriteJsonOrText(false, message, new { kind = "usage" }, jsonOutput); if (!jsonOutput) { Console.Error.WriteLine(); WriteHelp(); } }
    private static void WriteJsonOrText(bool success, string message, object? details, bool jsonOutput) { if (jsonOutput) { Console.WriteLine(JsonSerializer.Serialize(new { success, message, details }, new JsonSerializerOptions { WriteIndented = true })); return; } TextWriter writer = success ? Console.Out : Console.Error; writer.WriteLine(message); if (details is not null) writer.WriteLine(JsonSerializer.Serialize(details, new JsonSerializerOptions { WriteIndented = true })); }
    private static void WriteHelp()
    {
        Console.WriteLine("TextFileCombiner.Cli " + Version);
        Console.WriteLine();
        Console.WriteLine("Usage:");
        Console.WriteLine("  TextFileCombiner.Cli combine  --source <folder-or-zip> --output <file> [--protocol cptf1|cptf2] [--include-binary-assets] [--source-kind auto|folder|zip] [--json]");
        Console.WriteLine("  TextFileCombiner.Cli extract  --input <combined-file> --output <folder> [--overwrite] [--preserve-root] [--newline preserve|windows|unix] [--json]");
        Console.WriteLine("  TextFileCombiner.Cli validate --input <combined-file> [--output <validation-root>] [--json]");
        Console.WriteLine("  TextFileCombiner.Cli extract-one --input <combined-file> --path <relative-path> --output <folder> [--index-mode sequential|auto-indexed|indexed-only] [--overwrite] [--json]");
        Console.WriteLine();
        Console.WriteLine("CPTF/2 profile:");
        Console.WriteLine($"  Protocol version: {AppConstants.Cptf2ProtocolVersion}");
        Console.WriteLine($"  Parser profile:   {AppConstants.Cptf2ParserProfile}");
        Console.WriteLine("  Embedded index:   optional, non-authoritative, generated by default in CPTF/2 v3.4.1 output");
    }
}

internal sealed class CliCommandLine
{
    private readonly Dictionary<string, string> options = new Dictionary<string, string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    private readonly HashSet<string> flags = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    internal string Command { get; private set; } = string.Empty;
    internal bool ShowHelp { get; private set; }
    internal bool ShowVersion { get; private set; }
    internal bool JsonOutput => HasFlag("json");
    internal static CliCommandLine Parse(string[] args) { CliCommandLine result = new CliCommandLine(); int index = 0; if (args.Length == 0) { result.ShowHelp = true; return result; } while (index < args.Length) { string token = args[index]; if (token == "--help" || token == "-h") { result.ShowHelp = true; index++; continue; } if (token == "--version") { result.ShowVersion = true; index++; continue; } if (token.StartsWith("--", StringComparison.Ordinal)) { string name = token.Substring(2); if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(name)) throw new CliUsageException("Invalid empty option name."); if (index + 1 < args.Length && !args[index + 1].StartsWith("--", StringComparison.Ordinal)) { result.options[name] = args[index + 1]; index += 2; } else { result.flags.Add(name); index++; } continue; } if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(result.Command)) { result.Command = token; index++; continue; } throw new CliUsageException("Unexpected argument: " + token); } return result; }
    internal string? GetOption(string name) => options.TryGetValue(name, out string? value) ? value : null;
    internal bool HasFlag(string name) => flags.Contains(name);
}

internal sealed class CliUsageException : Exception { internal CliUsageException(string message) : base(message) { } }

namespace TextFileCombiner.Core;

internal sealed class CombinedFileValidationOptions
{
    internal string? IntendedOutputRoot { get; set; }
    internal bool ValidateSafePaths { get; set; } = true;
    internal bool ValidateHashes { get; set; } = true;
    internal bool ValidateBinaryBase64 { get; set; } = true;
    internal bool DetectDuplicatePaths { get; set; } = true;
    internal bool ValidateWindowsFileNameChars { get; set; } = true;
    internal bool RejectEmptyPathSegments { get; set; } = true;
    internal bool RejectTrailingSpacesOrDots { get; set; } = true;
    internal bool PreflightTargetContainment { get; set; } = true;

    internal RestoreOptions ToRestoreOptions()
    {
        return new RestoreOptions
        {
            ValidateOnly = true,
            EnableValidationChecks = ValidateHashes || ValidateBinaryBase64 || ValidateSafePaths || DetectDuplicatePaths,
            DetectDuplicatePaths = DetectDuplicatePaths,
            ValidatePathSafety = ValidateSafePaths,
            ValidateWindowsFileNameChars = ValidateWindowsFileNameChars,
            RejectEmptyPathSegments = RejectEmptyPathSegments,
            RejectTrailingSpacesOrDots = RejectTrailingSpacesOrDots,
            ValidateBlockBoundaries = false,
            PreflightBeforeWriting = true
        };
    }
}

namespace TextFileCombiner.Core;

internal sealed class CombinedFileValidationResult
{
    internal bool IsValid { get; set; }
    internal string CombinedTextFilePath { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    internal string Protocol { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    internal string ProtocolVersion { get; set; } = string.Empty;

    internal int ParsedFileCount { get; set; }
    internal int ContentFileCount { get; set; }
    internal int InternalFileCount { get; set; }
    internal int TextFileCount { get; set; }
    internal int BinaryFileCount { get; set; }
    internal int MetadataFailureCount { get; set; }
    internal int PayloadFailureCount { get; set; }
    internal int Sha256VerificationCount { get; set; }
    internal int Sha256FailureCount { get; set; }
    internal int Base64DecodeCount { get; set; }
    internal int Base64FailureCount { get; set; }
    internal int PathValidationCount { get; set; }

namespace TextFileCombiner.Core;

internal static class CombinedProjectProtocolRegistry
{
    private static readonly ICombinedProjectWriter[] Writers =
    {
        new Cptf1HumanReadableWriter(),
        new Cptf2LengthDelimitedWriter()
    };
    private static readonly ICombinedProjectReader[] Readers =
    {
        new Cptf2LengthDelimitedReader(),
        new Cptf1HumanReadableReader()
    };
    internal static ICombinedProjectWriter CreateWriter(CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol protocol)
    {
        ICombinedProjectWriter? writer = Writers.FirstOrDefault(x => x.Protocol == protocol);
        if (writer is null)
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException($"No writer is registered for protocol {protocol}.");
        }
        return writer;
    }

    internal static ICombinedProjectReader SelectReader(byte[] combinedFileBytes)
    {
        foreach (ICombinedProjectReader reader in Readers)
        {
            if (reader.CanRead(combinedFileBytes))
            {
                return reader;
            }
        }
        throw new ExtractValidationException("Protocol detection", "The combined file protocol could not be detected.");
    }
}

namespace TextFileCombiner.Core;

internal sealed class Cptf1HumanReadableReader : ICombinedProjectReader
{
    public string ProtocolName => AppConstants.Cptf1HumanReadableName;
    public bool CanRead(byte[] combinedFileBytes) => true;
    public IReadOnlyList<CombinedFileEntry> Read(byte[] combinedFileBytes, RestoreOptions options, IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones, out string detectedNewLine)
    {

        return ProjectFileExtractor.ParseCombinedText(decodedText.Text, options, milestones);
    }

using System.Text;

namespace TextFileCombiner.Core;

internal sealed class Cptf2LengthDelimitedReader : ICombinedProjectReader
{
    public string ProtocolName => AppConstants.Cptf2LengthDelimitedName;
    public bool CanRead(byte[] combinedFileBytes)
    {
        byte[] magic = Encoding.ASCII.GetBytes(AppConstants.Cptf2MagicHeader);
        if (combinedFileBytes.Length < magic.Length)
        {
            return false;
        }
        for (int index = 0; index < magic.Length; index++)
        {
            if (combinedFileBytes[index] != magic[index])
            {
                return false;
            }
        }
        return true;
    }

    public IReadOnlyList<CombinedFileEntry> Read(byte[] combinedFileBytes, RestoreOptions options, IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones, out string detectedNewLine)
    {
        detectedNewLine = Environment.NewLine;
        return ProjectFileExtractor.ParseCptf2LengthDelimited(combinedFileBytes, options, milestones);
    }
}

using System.Text.RegularExpressions;

namespace TextFileCombiner.Core;

internal static class CombinedProjectValidator
{
    private static readonly char[] WindowsInvalidFileNameChars = Enumerable
        .Range(0, 32)
        .Select(value => (char)value)
        .Concat(new[] { '<', '>', ':', '"', '|', '?', '*' })
        .ToArray();

    internal static CombinedFileValidationResult ValidateCombinedFile(string combinedTextFilePath, CombinedFileValidationOptions options)
    {
        return ValidateCombinedFile(combinedTextFilePath, options, null);
    }

    internal static CombinedFileValidationResult ValidateCombinedFile(string combinedTextFilePath, CombinedFileValidationOptions options, IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones)
    {
        CombinedFileValidationResult result = new CombinedFileValidationResult
        {
            CombinedTextFilePath = Path.GetFullPath(combinedTextFilePath),
            MarkerBasedContentParsingUsed = false
        };
        try
        {
            if (!File.Exists(combinedTextFilePath))
            {
                AddIssue(result, CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity.Error, "InputFileNotFound", "Combined text file was not found.");
                return Finish(result);
            }
            milestones?.Report(new ExtractMilestone { Status = ExtractMilestoneStatus.Started, Message = "Reading combined text file", Detail = combinedTextFilePath });
            byte[] combinedBytes = File.ReadAllBytes(combinedTextFilePath);
            ICombinedProjectReader reader = CombinedProjectProtocolRegistry.SelectReader(combinedBytes);
            result.Protocol = reader.ProtocolName;
            result.ParserCompliantLengthDelimited = string.Equals(reader.ProtocolName, AppConstants.Cptf2LengthDelimitedName, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
            if (result.ParserCompliantLengthDelimited)
            {
                result.ProtocolVersion = AppConstants.Cptf2ProtocolVersion;
                result.ParserProfile = AppConstants.Cptf2ParserProfile;
            }
            RestoreOptions restoreOptions = options.ToRestoreOptions();
            IReadOnlyList<CombinedFileEntry> entries = reader.Read(combinedBytes, restoreOptions, milestones, out _);
            result.ManifestFileCount = entries.Count;
            result.ParsedFileCount = entries.Count;
            result.InternalFileCount = entries.Count(IsInternalCptfEntry);
            result.ContentFileCount = entries.Count - result.InternalFileCount;
            result.TextFileCount = entries.Count(entry => !IsBinaryEntry(entry));
            result.BinaryFileCount = entries.Count(IsBinaryEntry);
            result.Sha256VerificationCount = entries.Count(entry => entry.IsByteContent);
            result.Base64DecodeCount = entries.Count(entry => IsBinaryEntry(entry) && entry.IsBinaryContent);
            result.EmbeddedIndexPresent = entries.Any(IsEmbeddedIndexEntry);
            result.EmbeddedIndexPath = entries.FirstOrDefault(IsEmbeddedIndexEntry)?.RelativePath;
            ValidateEntries(entries, options, result);
            milestones?.Report(new ExtractMilestone { Status = ExtractMilestoneStatus.Done, Message = "Validation completed", Detail = result.IsValid ? "No files were written." : "Validation issues were detected." });
        }
        catch (ExtractValidationException ex)
        {
            AddIssue(result, CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity.Error, ex.CheckName, ex.Message, ex.RelativePath);
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            AddIssue(result, CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity.Error, "Validation", ex.Message);
        }
        return Finish(result);
    }

    internal static RestoreResult ToRestoreResult(CombinedFileValidationResult validationResult)
    {
        RestoreResult restoreResult = new RestoreResult();
        restoreResult.ProtocolName = validationResult.Protocol;
        restoreResult.TotalFileCount = validationResult.ParsedFileCount;
        restoreResult.TextFileCount = validationResult.TextFileCount;
        restoreResult.BinaryFileCount = validationResult.BinaryFileCount;
        restoreResult.Sha256VerificationCount = validationResult.Sha256VerificationCount;
        restoreResult.FilesPlanned = validationResult.ParsedFileCount;
        foreach (CombinedFileValidationIssue issue in validationResult.Issues.Where(issue => issue.Severity == CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity.Warning))
        {
            restoreResult.Warnings.Add(issue.Message);
        }
        return restoreResult;
    }

    private static void ValidateEntries(IReadOnlyList<CombinedFileEntry> entries, CombinedFileValidationOptions options, CombinedFileValidationResult result)
    {
        HashSet<string> seenRelativePaths = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        HashSet<string> seenTargetPaths = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        string outputRoot = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(options.IntendedOutputRoot)
            ? Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), "TextFileCombinerValidationRoot")
            : Path.GetFullPath(options.IntendedOutputRoot);
        foreach (CombinedFileEntry entry in entries)
        {
            CombinedFileValidationFileResult fileResult = new CombinedFileValidationFileResult
            {
                Index = entry.Index,
                RelativePath = entry.RelativePath,
                FileKind = entry.FileKind,
                ContentEncoding = entry.ContentEncoding,
                DeclaredByteLength = entry.ByteLength,
                ActualPayloadByteLength = entry.IsBinaryContent ? entry.EncodedByteLength : entry.ContentBytes.LongLength,
                OutputByteLength = entry.ContentBytes.LongLength,
                ExpectedSha256 = entry.Sha256,
                ActualSha256 = entry.IsByteContent ? HashService.ComputeSha256Hex(entry.ContentBytes) : string.Empty,
                Base64Decoded = !IsBinaryEntry(entry) || entry.IsBinaryContent
            };
            fileResult.Sha256Ok = !options.ValidateHashes || !entry.IsByteContent || string.Equals(fileResult.ActualSha256, entry.Sha256, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
            if (options.ValidateHashes && entry.IsByteContent && !fileResult.Sha256Ok)
            {
                result.Sha256FailureCount++;
                AddIssue(result, CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity.Error, "Sha256Mismatch", $"SHA-256 mismatch for {entry.RelativePath}.", entry.RelativePath);
            }
            if (options.ValidateBinaryBase64 && IsBinaryEntry(entry) && !fileResult.Base64Decoded)
            {
                result.Base64FailureCount++;
                AddIssue(result, CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity.Error, "Base64Decode", $"Base64 decode failed for {entry.RelativePath}.", entry.RelativePath);
            }
            if (options.DetectDuplicatePaths)
            {
                string relativeKey = entry.RelativePath.Replace('/', '\\').Trim();
                if (!seenRelativePaths.Add(relativeKey))
                {
                    fileResult.DuplicateRelativePath = true;
                    result.DuplicateRelativePathCount++;
                    AddIssue(result, CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity.Error, "DuplicateRelativePath", $"Duplicate relative path detected: {entry.RelativePath}", entry.RelativePath);
                }
            }
            if (options.ValidateSafePaths)
            {
                result.PathValidationCount++;
                if (TryGetSafeTargetPath(outputRoot, entry.RelativePath, options, out string? targetPath, out string? error))
                {
                    fileResult.PathSafe = true;
                    if (options.DetectDuplicatePaths && targetPath is not null && !seenTargetPaths.Add(targetPath))
                    {
                        fileResult.DuplicateTargetPath = true;
                        result.DuplicateTargetPathCount++;
                        AddIssue(result, CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity.Error, "DuplicateTargetPath", $"Duplicate target path detected: {entry.RelativePath}", entry.RelativePath);
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    result.PathFailureCount++;
                    fileResult.ErrorMessage = error;
                    AddIssue(result, CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity.Error, "UnsafePath", error ?? $"Unsafe relative path: {entry.RelativePath}", entry.RelativePath);
                }
            }
            else
            {
                fileResult.PathSafe = true;
            }
            result.Files.Add(fileResult);
        }
    }

    private static bool TryGetSafeTargetPath(string outputRoot, string relativePath, CombinedFileValidationOptions options, out string? targetPath, out string? error)
    {
        targetPath = null;
        error = null;
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(relativePath))
        {
            error = "Relative path is empty.";
            return false;
        }
        string windowsPath = relativePath.Replace('/', '\\');
        if (Path.IsPathRooted(relativePath) || Regex.IsMatch(windowsPath, @"^[A-Za-z]:\\") || windowsPath.StartsWith(@"\\", StringComparison.Ordinal))
        {
            error = $"Unsafe rooted path: {relativePath}";
            return false;
        }
        string[] segments = relativePath.Replace('\\', '/').Split('/');
        foreach (string segment in segments)
        {
            if (options.RejectEmptyPathSegments && string.IsNullOrEmpty(segment))
            {
                error = $"Unsafe path contains an empty segment: {relativePath}";
                return false;
            }
            if (segment == "." || segment == "..")
            {
                error = $"Unsafe path contains traversal or current-directory segment: {relativePath}";
                return false;
            }
            if (options.RejectTrailingSpacesOrDots && (segment.EndsWith(' ') || segment.EndsWith('.')))
            {
                error = $"Unsafe path contains a segment with trailing space or dot: {relativePath}";
                return false;
            }
            if (options.ValidateWindowsFileNameChars && segment.IndexOfAny(WindowsInvalidFileNameChars) >= 0)
            {
                error = $"Unsafe path contains an invalid Windows filename character: {relativePath}";
                return false;
            }
        }
        string fullRoot = Path.GetFullPath(outputRoot);
        string fullTarget = Path.GetFullPath(Path.Combine(new[] { fullRoot }.Concat(segments).ToArray()));
        if (options.PreflightTargetContainment)
        {
            string rootWithSeparator = fullRoot.EndsWith(Path.DirectorySeparatorChar) ? fullRoot : fullRoot + Path.DirectorySeparatorChar;
            if (!fullTarget.StartsWith(rootWithSeparator, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) && !string.Equals(fullTarget, fullRoot, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                error = $"Unsafe path escapes the output folder: {relativePath}";
                return false;
            }
        }
        targetPath = fullTarget;
        return true;
    }

    private static bool IsBinaryEntry(CombinedFileEntry entry)
    {
        return string.Equals(entry.FileKind, "binary", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) || entry.IsBinaryContent;
    }

    private static bool IsInternalCptfEntry(CombinedFileEntry entry)
    {
        return NormalizeRelativePath(entry.RelativePath).StartsWith(AppConstants.Cptf2InternalRoot, StringComparison.Ordinal);
    }

    private static bool IsEmbeddedIndexEntry(CombinedFileEntry entry)
    {
        string normalizedPath = NormalizeRelativePath(entry.RelativePath);
        return normalizedPath.StartsWith(AppConstants.Cptf2InternalRoot, StringComparison.Ordinal)
            && normalizedPath.EndsWith(".cptf2idx.json", StringComparison.Ordinal);
    }

    private static string NormalizeRelativePath(string relativePath)
    {
        return relativePath.Replace('\\', '/').Trim().ToLowerInvariant();
    }

    private static CombinedFileValidationResult Finish(CombinedFileValidationResult result)
    {
        result.IsValid = result.Issues.All(issue => issue.Severity != CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity.Error);
        return result;
    }

    private static void AddIssue(CombinedFileValidationResult result, CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity severity, string code, string message, string? relativePath = null)
    {
        result.Issues.Add(new CombinedFileValidationIssue { Severity = severity, Code = code, Message = message, RelativePath = relativePath });
    }
}

using System.Security.Cryptography;
using System.Text;
using System.Text.Json;
using System.Text.RegularExpressions;

namespace TextFileCombiner.Core;

/// <summary>
/// CPTF/2 v3.4.1 selected-path extraction surface.
/// Supports extracting one file or all files under a selected folder path.
/// </summary>
internal static class Cptf2IndexedExtractor
{
    private static readonly Regex EmbeddedIndexPathRegex = new Regex(
        @"^__cptf__/index\.entryOffset_(\d{20})\.cptf2idx\.json$",
        RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant);

    internal static RestoreResult ExtractOne(
        string combinedTextFilePath,
        string requestedRelativePath,
        string outputDirectory,
        RestoreOptions options,
        IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones = null)
    {
        if (options is null)
        {
            throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(options));
        }
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(combinedTextFilePath))
        {
            throw new ArgumentException("Combined text file path is required.", nameof(combinedTextFilePath));
        }
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(requestedRelativePath))
        {
            throw new ArgumentException("Selected file/folder path is required.", nameof(requestedRelativePath));
        }
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(outputDirectory))
        {
            throw new ArgumentException("Output directory is required.", nameof(outputDirectory));
        }
        if (!File.Exists(combinedTextFilePath))
        {
            throw new FileNotFoundException("Combined text file was not found.", combinedTextFilePath);
        }

        byte[] bytes = File.ReadAllBytes(combinedTextFilePath);
        bool embeddedIndexPresent = HasEmbeddedIndexHint(bytes);
        if (options.IndexMode == RestoreIndexMode.IndexedOnly && !embeddedIndexPresent)
        {
            throw new ExtractValidationException(
                "CPTF/2 embedded index",
                "indexed-only mode requires a valid embedded index.",
                requestedRelativePath);
        }

        string requestedNormalizedPath = NormalizeRelativePath(requestedRelativePath);
        ReaderState state = new ReaderState(bytes);
        RestoreResult result = new RestoreResult
        {
            ProtocolName = AppConstants.Cptf2LengthDelimitedName
        };
        HashSet<string> createdDirectories = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        int matchedCount = 0;

        RequireLine(state, AppConstants.Cptf2MagicHeader);
        SkipBlankLines(state);
        RequireSection(state, "BEGIN PARSER RULES", "END PARSER RULES");
        SkipBlankLines(state);
        RequireSection(state, "BEGIN MANIFEST", "END MANIFEST");
        SkipBlankLines(state);
        RequireSection(state, "BEGIN PROJECT STRUCTURE", "END PROJECT STRUCTURE");
        SkipBlankLines(state);
        RequireLine(state, "BEGIN FILES");

        while (true)
        {
            SkipBlankLines(state);
            string marker = ReadLine(state);
            if (string.Equals(marker, "END FILES", StringComparison.Ordinal))
            {
                break;
            }
            if (!string.Equals(marker, "BEGIN FILE", StringComparison.Ordinal))
            {
                throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 parsing", "Expected BEGIN FILE or END FILES.");
            }

            RequireLine(state, "BEGIN FILE METADATA");
            string metadataJson = ReadBlock(state, "END FILE METADATA");
            using JsonDocument metadataDocument = JsonDocument.Parse(metadataJson);
            JsonElement metadata = metadataDocument.RootElement;
            string relativePath = GetString(metadata, "relativePath");
            string normalizedPath = NormalizeRelativePath(relativePath);
            string fileKind = GetString(metadata, "fileKind");
            string contentEncoding = GetString(metadata, "contentEncoding");
            string cptfRole = GetString(metadata, "cptfRole");
            bool isInternal = GetBoolean(metadata, "internal")
                || normalizedPath.StartsWith(AppConstants.Cptf2InternalRoot, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                || string.Equals(cptfRole, AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexRole, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
            long byteLengthLong = GetInt64(metadata, "byteLength");
            if (byteLengthLong < 0 || byteLengthLong > int.MaxValue)
            {
                throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 metadata", "Invalid byteLength.", relativePath);
            }
            int byteLength = (int)byteLengthLong;
            string expectedSha256 = GetString(metadata, "sha256");

            RequireLine(state, "BEGIN CONTENT");
            byte[] payload = state.ReadBytes(byteLength);
            ConsumeOptionalNewLine(state);
            RequireLine(state, "END FILE");

            if (isInternal || !IsRequestedPathMatch(normalizedPath, requestedNormalizedPath))
            {
                continue;
            }

            matchedCount++;
            bool isBinary = string.Equals(fileKind, "binary", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                || string.Equals(contentEncoding, "base64", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
            byte[] outputBytes = isBinary ? Convert.FromBase64String(Encoding.UTF8.GetString(payload)) : payload;
            string actualSha256 = Convert.ToHexString(SHA256.HashData(outputBytes)).ToLowerInvariant();
            if (!string.Equals(expectedSha256, actualSha256, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                throw new ExtractValidationException("SHA-256 verification", "Payload SHA-256 verification failed.", relativePath);
            }

            result.Sha256VerificationCount++;
            if (isBinary)
            {
                result.BinaryFileCount++;
            }
            else
            {
                result.TextFileCount++;
            }

            if (options.ValidateOnly)
            {
                result.FilesSkipped++;
                continue;
            }

            string targetPath = ResolveTargetPath(outputDirectory, relativePath);
            string? targetDirectory = Path.GetDirectoryName(targetPath);
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(targetDirectory) && !Directory.Exists(targetDirectory))
            {
                Directory.CreateDirectory(targetDirectory);
                createdDirectories.Add(targetDirectory);
            }

            if (File.Exists(targetPath) && !options.OverwriteExistingFiles)
            {
                result.FilesSkipped++;
                result.Warnings.Add("Output file already exists and overwrite was not enabled: " + targetPath);
                continue;
            }

            File.WriteAllBytes(targetPath, outputBytes);
            result.FilesCreated++;
        }

        SkipBlankLines(state);
        RequireLine(state, "END CPTF");
        SkipBlankLines(state);
        if (!state.EndOfFile)
        {
            throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 parsing", "Unexpected trailing bytes after END CPTF.");
        }

        if (matchedCount == 0)
        {
            throw new ExtractValidationException(
                "CPTF/2 selected path",
                "Selected file/folder path was not found in the combined file.",
                requestedRelativePath);
        }

        result.FilesPlanned = matchedCount;
        result.TotalFileCount = matchedCount;
        result.DirectoriesCreated = createdDirectories.Count;
        if (options.IndexMode == RestoreIndexMode.AutoIndexed && embeddedIndexPresent)
        {
            result.Warnings.Add("Embedded index was detected. This selected-path extraction still verifies real file entries before writing.");
        }
        return result;
    }

    private static bool IsRequestedPathMatch(string normalizedPath, string requestedNormalizedPath)
    {
        return string.Equals(normalizedPath, requestedNormalizedPath, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            || normalizedPath.StartsWith(requestedNormalizedPath + "/", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    }

    private static bool HasEmbeddedIndexHint(byte[] bytes)
    {
        string text = Encoding.UTF8.GetString(bytes);
        foreach (string line in text.Split(new[] { "\r\n", "\n" }, StringSplitOptions.None))
        {
            if (EmbeddedIndexPathRegex.IsMatch(line.Trim()))
            {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    private static string ResolveTargetPath(string outputDirectory, string relativePath)
    {
        string normalized = relativePath.Replace('\\', '/').Trim('/');
        if (Path.IsPathRooted(normalized) || normalized.Contains("../", StringComparison.Ordinal) || normalized.StartsWith("../", StringComparison.Ordinal))
        {
            throw new ExtractValidationException("Path safety", "Unsafe relative path.", relativePath);
        }
        string[] segments = normalized.Split('/', StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);
        if (segments.Any(segment => string.Equals(segment, ".", StringComparison.Ordinal) || string.Equals(segment, "..", StringComparison.Ordinal)))
        {
            throw new ExtractValidationException("Path safety", "Unsafe relative path segment.", relativePath);
        }
        string outputRoot = Path.GetFullPath(outputDirectory);
        string targetPath = Path.GetFullPath(Path.Combine(new[] { outputRoot }.Concat(segments).ToArray()));
        if (!targetPath.StartsWith(outputRoot, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            throw new ExtractValidationException("Path safety", "Target path escapes output directory.", relativePath);
        }
        return targetPath;
    }

    private static string NormalizeRelativePath(string relativePath)
    {
        return relativePath.Replace('\\', '/').Trim().Trim('/').ToLowerInvariant();
    }

    private static string GetString(JsonElement metadata, string name)
    {
        return metadata.TryGetProperty(name, out JsonElement value) ? value.GetString() ?? string.Empty : string.Empty;
    }

    private static long GetInt64(JsonElement metadata, string name)
    {
        return metadata.TryGetProperty(name, out JsonElement value) && value.TryGetInt64(out long result) ? result : -1;
    }

    private static bool GetBoolean(JsonElement metadata, string name)
    {
        return metadata.TryGetProperty(name, out JsonElement value) && value.ValueKind == JsonValueKind.True;
    }

    private static void RequireSection(ReaderState state, string begin, string end)
    {
        RequireLine(state, begin);
        ReadBlock(state, end);
    }

    private static void RequireLine(ReaderState state, string expected)
    {
        string actual = ReadLine(state);
        if (!string.Equals(actual, expected, StringComparison.Ordinal))
        {
            throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 parsing", $"Expected '{expected}', got '{actual}'.");
        }
    }

    private static string ReadBlock(ReaderState state, string endMarker)
    {
        StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
        while (!state.EndOfFile)
        {
            string line = ReadLine(state);
            if (string.Equals(line, endMarker, StringComparison.Ordinal))
            {
                return builder.ToString();
            }
            builder.AppendLine(line);
        }
        throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 parsing", "Unexpected end of file while reading block.");
    }

    private static void SkipBlankLines(ReaderState state)
    {
        while (!state.EndOfFile)
        {
            int saved = state.Position;
            string line = ReadLine(state);
            if (line.Length != 0)
            {
                state.Position = saved;
                return;
            }
        }
    }

    private static string ReadLine(ReaderState state)
    {
        int start = state.Position;
        while (state.Position < state.Bytes.Length && state.Bytes[state.Position] != (byte)'\n')
        {
            state.Position++;
        }
        int length = state.Position - start;
        if (state.Position < state.Bytes.Length && state.Bytes[state.Position] == (byte)'\n')
        {
            state.Position++;
        }
        if (length > 0 && state.Bytes[start + length - 1] == (byte)'\r')
        {
            length--;
        }
        return Encoding.UTF8.GetString(state.Bytes, start, length);
    }

    private static void ConsumeOptionalNewLine(ReaderState state)
    {
        if (state.Position < state.Bytes.Length && state.Bytes[state.Position] == (byte)'\r')
        {
            state.Position++;
        }
        if (state.Position < state.Bytes.Length && state.Bytes[state.Position] == (byte)'\n')
        {
            state.Position++;
        }
    }

    private sealed class ReaderState
    {
        internal ReaderState(byte[] bytes)
        {
            Bytes = bytes;
        }
        internal byte[] Bytes { get; }
        internal int Position { get; set; }
        internal bool EndOfFile => Position >= Bytes.Length;
        internal byte[] ReadBytes(int length)
        {
            if (Position + length > Bytes.Length)
            {
                throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 parsing", "Content payload is shorter than declared byteLength.");
            }
            byte[] result = new byte[length];
            Buffer.BlockCopy(Bytes, Position, result, 0, length);
            Position += length;
            return result;
        }
    }
}
