using System.Globalization;
using System.IO.Compression;
using System.Security.Cryptography;
using System.Text;
using System.Text.Json;

namespace TextFileCombiner.Core;

internal static class ProjectFileCombiner
{
    internal const int LineWidth = AppConstants.LineWidth;
    private const string Cptf2MagicHeader = AppConstants.Cptf2MagicHeader;
    private static readonly Encoding OutputEncoding = new UTF8Encoding(false);
    private static readonly JsonSerializerOptions JsonOptions = new JsonSerializerOptions
    {
        WriteIndented = true,
        PropertyNamingPolicy = JsonNamingPolicy.CamelCase
    };
    private static readonly HashSet<string> ProjectFileExtensions = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
    {
        ".csproj", ".sln", ".slnf", ".props", ".targets", ".nuspec", ".pubxml", ".ruleset"
    };
    private static readonly HashSet<string> ConfigFileExtensions = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
    {
        ".config", ".json", ".xml", ".editorconfig"
    };
    private static readonly HashSet<string> ConfigSpecialFileNames = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
    {
        "global.json", "nuget.config", "Directory.Build.props", "Directory.Build.targets", "Directory.Packages.props"
    };
    internal static CombineResult CombineProjectTextFiles(InputSourceKind requestedInputSourceKind, string sourcePath, string outputFilePath, AppSettings settings)
    {
        DateTime startUtc = DateTime.UtcNow;
        InputSourceKind sourceKind = ResolveInputSourceKind(requestedInputSourceKind, sourcePath);
        CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol outputProtocol = settings.OutputProtocol;
        string fullOutputPath = Path.GetFullPath(outputFilePath);
        string? outputDirectory = Path.GetDirectoryName(fullOutputPath);
        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(outputDirectory))
        {
            Directory.CreateDirectory(outputDirectory);
        }
        List<SourceFileEntry> entries = sourceKind == InputSourceKind.ZipArchive
            ? LoadFromZip(sourcePath, settings)
            : LoadFromFolder(sourcePath, fullOutputPath, settings);
        entries = entries.OrderBy(x => x.RelativePath, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase).ToList();
        string output = BuildCombinedOutput(sourceKind, sourcePath, entries, outputProtocol);
        File.WriteAllText(fullOutputPath, output, OutputEncoding);
        byte[] outputBytes = File.ReadAllBytes(fullOutputPath);
        CombineResult result = new CombineResult();
        result.ResolvedInputSourceKind = sourceKind;
        result.ResolvedSourcePath = sourcePath;
        result.OutputFilePath = fullOutputPath;
        result.CombinedFileCount = entries.Count;
        result.TextFileCount = entries.Count(x => !x.IsBinary);
        result.BinaryFileCount = entries.Count(x => x.IsBinary);
        result.EncodingWarningCount = entries.Count(x => x.UsedFallbackEncoding);
        result.OutputProtocol = outputProtocol;
        result.OutputFileByteLength = outputBytes.LongLength;
        result.OutputFileSha256 = HashService.ComputeSha256Hex(outputBytes);
        result.Duration = DateTime.UtcNow - startUtc;
        return result;
    }

    internal static string GetSupportedFileSummary()
    {
        return SupportedFilePolicy.GetSupportedTextFileSummary();
    }

    internal static string GetSpecialFileSummary()
    {
        return SupportedFilePolicy.GetSpecialFileSummary();
    }

    internal static string GetExcludedFolderSummary()
    {
        return SupportedFilePolicy.GetExcludedFolderSummary();
    }

    internal static string GetBinaryFileSummary()
    {
        return SupportedFilePolicy.GetBinaryFileSummary();
    }

    internal static string GetSourceTypeText(InputSourceKind inputSourceKind)
    {
        return inputSourceKind switch
        {
            InputSourceKind.Folder => "Folder",
            InputSourceKind.ZipArchive => "ZIP archive",
            _ => "Auto"
        };
    }

    internal static string GetOutputProtocolText(CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol outputProtocol)
    {
        return outputProtocol switch
        {
            CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol.Cptf2LengthDelimited => AppConstants.Cptf2LengthDelimitedName,
            _ => AppConstants.Cptf1HumanReadableName
        };
    }

    private static InputSourceKind ResolveInputSourceKind(InputSourceKind requestedInputSourceKind, string sourcePath)
    {
        if (requestedInputSourceKind != InputSourceKind.Auto)
        {
            return requestedInputSourceKind;
        }
        if (Directory.Exists(sourcePath))
        {
            return InputSourceKind.Folder;
        }
        if (File.Exists(sourcePath) && string.Equals(Path.GetExtension(sourcePath), ".zip", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            return InputSourceKind.ZipArchive;
        }
        throw new InvalidOperationException("Auto mode could not determine whether the source is a folder or ZIP archive.");
    }

    private static List<SourceFileEntry> LoadFromFolder(string folderPath, string outputFilePath, AppSettings settings)
    {
        if (!Directory.Exists(folderPath))
        {
            throw new DirectoryNotFoundException("Source folder was not found: " + folderPath);
        }
        string rootPath = Path.GetFullPath(folderPath);
        List<string> files = Directory.EnumerateFiles(rootPath, "*", SearchOption.AllDirectories)
            .Where(path => !IsInExcludedFolder(rootPath, path))
            .Where(path => IsSupportedFile(path) || SupportedFilePolicy.ShouldIncludeBinaryAsset(Path.GetFileName(path), settings))
            .Where(path => !string.Equals(Path.GetFullPath(path), outputFilePath, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .OrderBy(path => Path.GetRelativePath(rootPath, path), StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();
        ValidateFileCount(files.Count, settings);
        List<SourceFileEntry> entries = new List<SourceFileEntry>();
        long totalBytes = 0;
        foreach (string path in files)
        {
            FileInfo fileInfo = new FileInfo(path);
            ValidateSingleFileSize(fileInfo.Length, path, settings);
            totalBytes += fileInfo.Length;
            ValidateTotalSize(totalBytes, settings);
            byte[] bytes = File.ReadAllBytes(path);
            string relativePath = Path.GetRelativePath(rootPath, path).Replace('/', '\\');
            SourceFileEntry entry = SupportedFilePolicy.ShouldIncludeBinaryAsset(
                Path.GetFileName(path),
                settings)
                ? CreateBinaryEntry(relativePath, path, bytes)
                : CreateTextEntry(relativePath, path, bytes, DecodeTextWithFallback(bytes));
            entries.Add(entry);
        }
        return entries;
    }

    private static List<SourceFileEntry> LoadFromZip(string zipPath, AppSettings settings)
    {
        if (!File.Exists(zipPath))
        {
            throw new FileNotFoundException("ZIP archive was not found.", zipPath);
        }
        List<SourceFileEntry> entries = new List<SourceFileEntry>();
        long totalBytes = 0;
        using ZipArchive archive = ZipFile.OpenRead(zipPath);
        List<ZipArchiveEntry> zipEntries = archive.Entries
            .Where(entry => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(entry.Name))
            .Where(entry => !IsZipEntryInExcludedFolder(entry.FullName))
            .Where(entry => IsSupportedFileName(entry.Name) || SupportedFilePolicy.ShouldIncludeBinaryAsset(entry.Name, settings))
            .OrderBy(entry => entry.FullName, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();
        ValidateFileCount(zipEntries.Count, settings);
        foreach (ZipArchiveEntry zipEntry in zipEntries)
        {
            ValidateSingleFileSize(zipEntry.Length, zipEntry.FullName, settings);
            totalBytes += zipEntry.Length;
            ValidateTotalSize(totalBytes, settings);
            using Stream stream = zipEntry.Open();
            using MemoryStream memoryStream = new MemoryStream();
            stream.CopyTo(memoryStream);
            byte[] bytes = memoryStream.ToArray();
            string relativePath = zipEntry.FullName.Replace('/', '\\');
            string fullPath = Path.GetFullPath(zipPath) + "::" + relativePath;
            SourceFileEntry entry = SupportedFilePolicy.ShouldIncludeBinaryAsset(
                zipEntry.Name,
                settings)
                ? CreateBinaryEntry(relativePath, fullPath, bytes)
                : CreateTextEntry(relativePath, fullPath, bytes, DecodeTextWithFallback(bytes));
            entries.Add(entry);
        }
        return entries;
    }

    private static SourceFileEntry CreateTextEntry(string relativePath, string fullPath, byte[] bytes, DecodedTextResult decodedText)
    {
        SourceFileEntry entry = new SourceFileEntry();
        entry.RelativePath = relativePath;
        entry.FullPath = fullPath;
        entry.FileName = Path.GetFileName(relativePath);
        entry.ExtensionText = GetExtensionText(entry.FileName);
        entry.Content = NormalizeNewLines(decodedText.Text);
        byte[] contentBytes = OutputEncoding.GetBytes(entry.Content);
        entry.LineCount = CountLines(entry.Content);
        entry.ByteSize = bytes.LongLength;
        entry.ByteLengthAsWritten = contentBytes.LongLength;
        entry.Sha256 = HashService.ComputeSha256Hex(contentBytes);
        entry.NewLineStyle = DetectNewLineStyle(entry.Content);
        entry.HadUtf8Bom = decodedText.HadUtf8Bom;
        entry.ContentEncoding = "utf-8-plain-text";
        entry.UsedFallbackEncoding = decodedText.UsedFallbackEncoding;
        return entry;
    }

    private static SourceFileEntry CreateBinaryEntry(string relativePath, string fullPath, byte[] bytes)
    {
        string base64Content = Convert.ToBase64String(bytes);
        byte[] encodedBytes = OutputEncoding.GetBytes(base64Content);
        SourceFileEntry entry = new SourceFileEntry();
        entry.RelativePath = relativePath;
        entry.FullPath = fullPath;
        entry.FileName = Path.GetFileName(relativePath);
        entry.ExtensionText = GetExtensionText(entry.FileName);
        entry.Content = base64Content;
        entry.LineCount = 1;
        entry.ByteSize = bytes.LongLength;
        entry.ByteLengthAsWritten = encodedBytes.LongLength;
        entry.Sha256 = HashService.ComputeSha256Hex(bytes);
        entry.NewLineStyle = "none";
        entry.HadUtf8Bom = false;
        entry.IsBinary = true;
        entry.ContentEncoding = "base64";
        return entry;
    }

    private static string BuildCombinedOutput(InputSourceKind sourceKind, string sourcePath, IReadOnlyList<SourceFileEntry> entries, CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol outputProtocol)
    {
        ICombinedProjectWriter writer = CombinedProjectProtocolRegistry.CreateWriter(outputProtocol);
        return writer.Write(sourceKind, sourcePath, entries);
    }

    internal static string BuildCptf1HumanReadableOutput(InputSourceKind sourceKind, string sourcePath, IReadOnlyList<SourceFileEntry> entries)
    {
        StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
        string sourceType = GetSourceTypeText(sourceKind);
        int csharpCount = entries.Count(x => string.Equals(x.ExtensionText, ".cs", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
        int projectCount = entries.Count(x => ProjectFileExtensions.Contains(x.ExtensionText));
        int configCount = entries.Count(x => ConfigFileExtensions.Contains(x.ExtensionText) || ConfigSpecialFileNames.Contains(x.FileName));
        IReadOnlyList<string> folders = GetIncludedFolders(entries);
        int encodingWarningCount = entries.Count(x => x.UsedFallbackEncoding);
        builder.AppendLine("' COMBINED TEXT FILES " + new string('=', Math.Max(3, LineWidth - 22)));
        builder.AppendLine("' Source Type        : " + sourceType);
        builder.AppendLine("' Source Path        : " + Path.GetFullPath(sourcePath));
        builder.AppendLine("' Created On         : " + DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"));
        builder.AppendLine("' Total Folders      : " + folders.Count);
        builder.AppendLine("' Total Files        : " + entries.Count);
        builder.AppendLine("' Total C# Files     : " + csharpCount);
        builder.AppendLine("' Total Project Files: " + projectCount);
        builder.AppendLine("' Total Config Files : " + configCount);
        builder.AppendLine();
        builder.AppendLine("' PROJECT STRUCTURE " + new string('=', Math.Max(3, LineWidth - 20)));
        builder.AppendLine("'");
        foreach (string line in BuildTreeLines(entries))
        {
            builder.AppendLine("' " + line);
        }
        builder.AppendLine();
        builder.AppendLine("' BEGIN FILE CONTENT " + new string('=', Math.Max(3, LineWidth - 21)));
        builder.AppendLine();
        int index = 1;
        foreach (string folder in folders)
        {
            string folderDisplay = string.IsNullOrEmpty(folder) ? "Root Folder" : folder;
            string folderTreePrefix = string.IsNullOrEmpty(folder) ? "[Root Folder]" : GetTreePrefixForFolder(folder) + folder;
            builder.AppendLine(CreateFolderHeader(folderTreePrefix, folderDisplay));
            builder.AppendLine();
            foreach (SourceFileEntry entry in entries
                .Where(x => string.Equals(GetFolderPath(x.RelativePath), folder, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                .OrderBy(x => x.FileName, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                builder.AppendLine(CreateFileHeader(entry, index));
                builder.AppendLine("' RltvPath: " + entry.RelativePath + ", FullPath: " + entry.FullPath);
                builder.AppendLine();
                builder.AppendLine(entry.Content);
                builder.AppendLine();
                index++;
            }
        }
        return builder.ToString();
    }

    internal static string BuildCptf2LengthDelimitedOutput(InputSourceKind sourceKind, string sourcePath, IReadOnlyList<SourceFileEntry> entries)
    {
        string indexOffset20 = new string('0', AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexOffsetWidth);
        string indexRelativePath = FormatEmbeddedIndexPath(indexOffset20);
        string output = string.Empty;
        for (int attempt = 0; attempt < 4; attempt++)
        {
            output = BuildCptf2LengthDelimitedOutputCore(sourceKind, sourcePath, entries, indexOffset20, indexRelativePath, out int indexEntryOffset);
            string finalOffset20 = FormatOffset20(indexEntryOffset);
            string finalIndexRelativePath = FormatEmbeddedIndexPath(finalOffset20);
            if (string.Equals(finalOffset20, indexOffset20, StringComparison.Ordinal) && string.Equals(finalIndexRelativePath, indexRelativePath, StringComparison.Ordinal))
            {
                return output;
            }
            indexOffset20 = finalOffset20;
            indexRelativePath = finalIndexRelativePath;
        }
        output = BuildCptf2LengthDelimitedOutputCore(sourceKind, sourcePath, entries, indexOffset20, indexRelativePath, out int finalIndexEntryOffset);
        if (!string.Equals(FormatOffset20(finalIndexEntryOffset), indexOffset20, StringComparison.Ordinal))
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException("CPTF/2 embedded-index offset did not stabilize.");
        }
        return output;
    }

    private static string BuildCptf2LengthDelimitedOutputCore(InputSourceKind sourceKind, string sourcePath, IReadOnlyList<SourceFileEntry> entries, string indexOffset20, string indexRelativePath, out int indexEntryOffset)
    {
        StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
        string sourceType = GetSourceTypeText(sourceKind);
        IReadOnlyList<string> folders = GetIncludedFolders(entries);
        int contentFileCount = entries.Count;
        int internalFileCount = AppConstants.Cptf2GenerateEmbeddedIndexByDefault ? 1 : 0;
        int fileCount = contentFileCount + internalFileCount;
        builder.AppendLine(Cptf2MagicHeader);
        builder.AppendLine("BEGIN PARSER RULES");
        builder.AppendLine(JsonSerializer.Serialize(CreateCptf2ParserRules(), JsonOptions));
        builder.AppendLine("END PARSER RULES");
        builder.AppendLine();
        builder.AppendLine("BEGIN MANIFEST");
        builder.AppendLine(JsonSerializer.Serialize(new
        {
            format = AppConstants.FormatName,
            formatVersion = AppConstants.Cptf2FormatVersion,
            protocol = AppConstants.Cptf2LengthDelimitedName,
            protocolVersion = AppConstants.Cptf2ProtocolVersion,
            parserProfile = AppConstants.Cptf2ParserProfile,
            createdOn = DateTime.Now.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"),
            sourceType,
            sourcePath = Path.GetFullPath(sourcePath),
            rootFolderName = GetRootName(sourcePath, sourceKind),
            fileCount,
            contentFileCount,
            internalFileCount,
            folderCount = folders.Count,
            textFileCount = entries.Count(x => !x.IsBinary),
            binaryFileCount = entries.Count(x => x.IsBinary),
            contentTransferEncoding = AppConstants.Cptf2ContentTransferEncoding,
            contentLengthUnit = AppConstants.Cptf2ContentLengthUnit,
            hashAlgorithm = AppConstants.Cptf2HashAlgorithm,
            embeddedIndex = new
            {
                present = AppConstants.Cptf2GenerateEmbeddedIndexByDefault,
                relativePath = indexRelativePath,
                offset20 = indexOffset20,
                offsetWidth = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexOffsetWidth,
                offsetBase = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexOffsetBase,
                offsetTarget = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexOffsetTarget,
                cptfRole = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexRole,
                authoritative = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexAuthoritative
            },
            generator = new { name = AppVersion.ProductName, version = AppVersion.Version }
        }, JsonOptions));
        builder.AppendLine("END MANIFEST");
        builder.AppendLine();
        builder.AppendLine("BEGIN PROJECT STRUCTURE");
        foreach (string line in BuildTreeLines(entries)) builder.AppendLine(line);
        if (AppConstants.Cptf2GenerateEmbeddedIndexByDefault) builder.AppendLine(indexRelativePath);
        builder.AppendLine("END PROJECT STRUCTURE");
        builder.AppendLine();
        builder.AppendLine("BEGIN FILES");
        int index = 1;
        List<Cptf2IndexEntryInfo> indexEntries = new List<Cptf2IndexEntryInfo>();
        foreach (SourceFileEntry entry in entries.OrderBy(x => x.RelativePath, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            int entryStartOffset = GetUtf8ByteCount(builder);
            string fileEntryText = BuildCptf2FileEntry(entry, index, entryStartOffset, out Cptf2IndexEntryInfo indexEntryInfo);
            builder.Append(fileEntryText);
            indexEntries.Add(indexEntryInfo);
            index++;
        }
        indexEntryOffset = GetUtf8ByteCount(builder);
        if (AppConstants.Cptf2GenerateEmbeddedIndexByDefault) builder.Append(BuildCptf2EmbeddedIndexFileEntry(index, indexRelativePath, indexEntryOffset, indexEntries));
        builder.AppendLine("END FILES");
        builder.AppendLine("END CPTF");
        return builder.ToString();
    }

    

    private static object CreateCptf2ParserRules()
    {
        return new
        {
            format = AppConstants.FormatName,
            formatVersion = AppConstants.Cptf2FormatVersion,
            protocol = AppConstants.Cptf2LengthDelimitedName,
            protocolVersion = AppConstants.Cptf2ProtocolVersion,
            parserProfile = AppConstants.Cptf2ParserProfile,
            parserRulesVersion = AppConstants.Cptf2ParserRulesVersion,
            contentReadMode = AppConstants.Cptf2ContentReadMode,
            contentLengthUnit = AppConstants.Cptf2ContentLengthUnit,
            hashAlgorithm = AppConstants.Cptf2HashAlgorithm,
            pathSeparator = AppConstants.Cptf2PathSeparator,
            contentTerminator = AppConstants.Cptf2ContentTerminator,
            extensions = new[] { new { name = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexExtensionName, version = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexExtensionVersion, required = false } },
            embeddedIndex = new { reservedRoot = AppConstants.Cptf2InternalRoot, pathPattern = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexPathPattern, offsetWidth = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexOffsetWidth, offsetBase = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexOffsetBase, offsetTarget = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexOffsetTarget, placement = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexPlacement, authoritative = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexAuthoritative },
            rules = new[] { "Read exactly byteLength payload bytes.", "Do not marker-scan payloads.", "Verify SHA-256.", "The embedded index is optional and non-authoritative." }
        };
    }

    

    private static IReadOnlyList<string> GetIncludedFolders(IReadOnlyList<SourceFileEntry> entries)
    {
        SortedSet<string> folders = new SortedSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        folders.Add(string.Empty);
        foreach (SourceFileEntry entry in entries)
        {
            string folder = GetFolderPath(entry.RelativePath);
            while (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(folder))
            {
                folders.Add(folder);
                int separatorIndex = folder.LastIndexOf('\\');
                folder = separatorIndex < 0 ? string.Empty : folder.Substring(0, separatorIndex);
            }
        }
        return folders.ToList();
    }

    private static IEnumerable<string> BuildTreeLines(IReadOnlyList<SourceFileEntry> entries)
    {
        TreeNode root = new TreeNode("[Root Folder]");
        foreach (SourceFileEntry entry in entries)
        {
            TreeNode current = root;
            string[] parts = entry.RelativePath.Split('\\', StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);
            for (int partIndex = 0; partIndex < parts.Length; partIndex++)
            {
                bool isFile = partIndex == parts.Length - 1;
                current = isFile ? current.GetOrAddFile(parts[partIndex]) : current.GetOrAddFolder(parts[partIndex]);
            }
        }
        yield return root.Name;
        foreach (string childLine in BuildTreeChildLines(root, string.Empty))
        {
            yield return childLine;
        }
    }

    private static IEnumerable<string> BuildTreeChildLines(TreeNode node, string prefix)
    {
        List<TreeNode> children = node.Folders
            .OrderBy(x => x.Name, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .Concat(node.Files.OrderBy(x => x.Name, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .ToList();
        for (int index = 0; index < children.Count; index++)
        {
            TreeNode child = children[index];
            bool isLast = index == children.Count - 1;
            yield return prefix + (isLast ? "└── " : "├── ") + child.Name;
            string childPrefix = prefix + (isLast ? "    " : "│   ");
            foreach (string childLine in BuildTreeChildLines(child, childPrefix))
            {
                yield return childLine;
            }
        }
    }

    private static string CreateFolderHeader(string folderTreePrefix, string displayFolderPath)
    {
        string text = "' " + folderTreePrefix + " ";
        string suffix = " FOLDER: [" + displayFolderPath + "]";
        int fillCount = Math.Max(3, LineWidth - text.Length - suffix.Length);
        return text + new string('#', fillCount) + suffix;
    }

    private static string CreateFileHeader(SourceFileEntry entry, int index)
    {
        string treePrefix = GetTreePrefixForFile(entry.RelativePath);
        string text = "' " + treePrefix + entry.FileName + " ";
        string suffix = " [" + index.ToString("000") + "][" + entry.ExtensionText + "][Lines: " + entry.LineCount + "]";
        int fillCount = Math.Max(3, LineWidth - text.Length - suffix.Length);
        return text + new string('-', fillCount) + suffix;
    }

    private static string GetTreePrefixForFile(string relativePath)
    {
        int depth = relativePath.Count(character => character == '\\');
        return new string(' ', depth * 4) + "├── ";
    }

    private static string GetTreePrefixForFolder(string relativeFolderPath)
    {
        int depth = relativeFolderPath.Count(character => character == '\\');
        return new string(' ', depth * 4) + "├── ";
    }

    private static string GetFolderPath(string relativePath)
    {
        string normalizedPath = relativePath.Replace('/', '\\');
        int separatorIndex = normalizedPath.LastIndexOf('\\');
        return separatorIndex < 0 ? string.Empty : normalizedPath.Substring(0, separatorIndex);
    }

    private static string BuildCptf2FileEntry(SourceFileEntry entry, int index, int entryStartOffset, out Cptf2IndexEntryInfo indexEntryInfo)
    {
        StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
        builder.AppendLine("BEGIN FILE");
        builder.AppendLine("BEGIN FILE METADATA");
        object metadata = CreateCptf2FileMetadata(entry, index);
        string metadataJson = JsonSerializer.Serialize(metadata, JsonOptions);
        int metadataOffset = entryStartOffset + Encoding.UTF8.GetByteCount("BEGIN FILE\nBEGIN FILE METADATA\n");
        int metadataByteLength = Encoding.UTF8.GetByteCount(metadataJson + "\n");
        builder.AppendLine(metadataJson);
        builder.AppendLine("END FILE METADATA");
        builder.AppendLine("BEGIN CONTENT");
        int payloadOffset = entryStartOffset + Encoding.UTF8.GetByteCount(builder.ToString());
        builder.Append(entry.Content);
        if (!entry.Content.EndsWith("\n", StringComparison.Ordinal)) builder.AppendLine();
        builder.AppendLine("END FILE");
        int entryEndOffset = entryStartOffset + Encoding.UTF8.GetByteCount(builder.ToString());
        indexEntryInfo = new Cptf2IndexEntryInfo(index, entry.RelativePath, NormalizeCptf2Path(entry.RelativePath), entry.IsBinary ? "binary" : "text", entry.ContentEncoding, entryStartOffset, metadataOffset, metadataByteLength, payloadOffset, entry.ByteLengthAsWritten, entryEndOffset, entry.Sha256);
        return builder.ToString();
    }

    private static object CreateCptf2FileMetadata(SourceFileEntry entry, int index)
    {
        return new { index, relativePath = entry.RelativePath, fullPath = entry.FullPath, fileName = entry.FileName, extension = entry.ExtensionText, fileKind = entry.IsBinary ? "binary" : "text", contentEncoding = entry.ContentEncoding, encoding = entry.IsBinary ? "binary" : entry.UsedFallbackEncoding ? "system-default-fallback" : "utf-8", hadBom = entry.HadUtf8Bom, newline = entry.NewLineStyle, lineCount = entry.LineCount, originalByteLength = entry.ByteSize, byteLength = entry.ByteLengthAsWritten, encodedByteLength = entry.IsBinary ? entry.ByteLengthAsWritten : 0, sha256 = entry.Sha256 };
    }

    private static string BuildCptf2EmbeddedIndexFileEntry(int index, string indexRelativePath, int indexEntryOffset, IReadOnlyList<Cptf2IndexEntryInfo> indexEntries)
    {
        object indexDocument = new { format = "CPTF/2-EMBEDDED-INDEX", version = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexExtensionVersion, offsetBase = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexOffsetBase, offsetTarget = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexOffsetTarget, offsetWidth = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexOffsetWidth, indexEntryRelativePath = indexRelativePath, indexEntryOffset, coversIndexEntry = false, counts = new { indexedEntries = indexEntries.Count, contentFiles = indexEntries.Count, internalFilesExcluded = 1 }, entries = indexEntries.Select(x => new { entryId = x.EntryId, index = x.Index, relativePath = x.RelativePath, normalizedPath = x.NormalizedPath, fileKind = x.FileKind, contentEncoding = x.ContentEncoding, entryStartOffset = x.EntryStartOffset, metadataOffset = x.MetadataOffset, metadataByteLength = x.MetadataByteLength, payloadOffset = x.PayloadOffset, byteLength = x.ByteLength, entryEndOffset = x.EntryEndOffset, sha256 = x.Sha256 }).ToArray(), pathIndex = indexEntries.ToDictionary(x => x.NormalizedPath, x => x.EntryId, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase), duplicateNormalizedPaths = new Dictionary<string, int[]>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase) };
        string indexPayload = "BEGIN CPTF INDEX\n" + JsonSerializer.Serialize(indexDocument, JsonOptions) + "\nEND CPTF INDEX\n";
        byte[] indexPayloadBytes = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(indexPayload);
        string indexPayloadSha256 = Convert.ToHexString(SHA256.HashData(indexPayloadBytes)).ToLowerInvariant();
        object metadata = new { index, relativePath = indexRelativePath, fileName = Path.GetFileName(indexRelativePath), extension = ".json", fileKind = "text", contentEncoding = "utf-8", encoding = "utf-8", hadBom = false, newline = "LF", lineCount = indexPayload.Count(character => character == '\n'), originalByteLength = indexPayloadBytes.LongLength, byteLength = indexPayloadBytes.LongLength, encodedByteLength = 0, sha256 = indexPayloadSha256, cptfRole = AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexRole, @internal = true };
        StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
        builder.AppendLine("BEGIN FILE");
        builder.AppendLine("BEGIN FILE METADATA");
        builder.AppendLine(JsonSerializer.Serialize(metadata, JsonOptions));
        builder.AppendLine("END FILE METADATA");
        builder.AppendLine("BEGIN CONTENT");
        builder.Append(indexPayload);
        builder.AppendLine("END FILE");
        return builder.ToString();
    }

    private static string FormatOffset20(int offset) => offset.ToString("D20", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);
    private static string FormatEmbeddedIndexPath(string offset20) => AppConstants.Cptf2EmbeddedIndexPathPattern.Replace("{offset20}", offset20, StringComparison.Ordinal);
    private static int GetUtf8ByteCount(StringBuilder builder) => Encoding.UTF8.GetByteCount(builder.ToString());
    private static string NormalizeCptf2Path(string relativePath) => relativePath.Replace('\\', '/').ToLowerInvariant();

    private sealed class Cptf2IndexEntryInfo
    {
        internal Cptf2IndexEntryInfo(int index, string relativePath, string normalizedPath, string fileKind, string contentEncoding, int entryStartOffset, int metadataOffset, int metadataByteLength, int payloadOffset, long byteLength, int entryEndOffset, string sha256)
        {
            EntryId = index; Index = index; RelativePath = relativePath; NormalizedPath = normalizedPath; FileKind = fileKind; ContentEncoding = contentEncoding; EntryStartOffset = entryStartOffset; MetadataOffset = metadataOffset; MetadataByteLength = metadataByteLength; PayloadOffset = payloadOffset; ByteLength = byteLength; EntryEndOffset = entryEndOffset; Sha256 = sha256;
        }
        internal int EntryId { get; }
        internal int Index { get; }
        internal string RelativePath { get; }
        internal string NormalizedPath { get; }
        internal string FileKind { get; }
        internal string ContentEncoding { get; }
        internal int EntryStartOffset { get; }
        internal int MetadataOffset { get; }
        internal int MetadataByteLength { get; }
        internal int PayloadOffset { get; }
        internal long ByteLength { get; }
        internal int EntryEndOffset { get; }
        internal string Sha256 { get; }
    }

    private sealed class TreeNode
    {
        internal TreeNode(string name)
        {
            Name = name;
        }

        internal string Name { get; }
        internal List<TreeNode> Folders { get; } = new List<TreeNode>();
        internal List<TreeNode> Files { get; } = new List<TreeNode>();
        internal TreeNode GetOrAddFolder(string name) => GetOrAdd(Folders, name);
        internal TreeNode GetOrAddFile(string name) => GetOrAdd(Files, name);
        private static TreeNode GetOrAdd(List<TreeNode> nodes, string name)
        {
            TreeNode? node = nodes.FirstOrDefault(x => string.Equals(x.Name, name, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
            if (node is null)
            {
                node = new TreeNode(name);
                nodes.Add(node);
            }
            return node;
        }
    }

    private static void ValidateFileCount(int fileCount, AppSettings settings)
    {
        if (fileCount > settings.MaxFileCount)
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException($"File count {fileCount} exceeds the configured limit of {settings.MaxFileCount} files.");
        }
    }

    private static void ValidateSingleFileSize(long bytes, string path, AppSettings settings)
    {
        long limitBytes = settings.MaxSingleFileSizeMb * 1024L * 1024L;
        if (bytes > limitBytes)
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException($"File exceeds the configured single-file limit.\r\n\r\nFile:\r\n{path}\r\n\r\nSize:\r\n{FormatBytes(bytes)}\r\n\r\nLimit:\r\n{settings.MaxSingleFileSizeMb} MB");
        }
    }

    private static void ValidateTotalSize(long bytes, AppSettings settings)
    {
        long limitBytes = settings.MaxTotalSizeMb * 1024L * 1024L;
        if (bytes > limitBytes)
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException($"Total source text size exceeds the configured limit of {settings.MaxTotalSizeMb} MB.");
        }
    }

    private static bool IsInExcludedFolder(string rootPath, string filePath)
    {
        string relativePath = Path.GetRelativePath(rootPath, filePath);
        string[] parts = relativePath.Split(Path.DirectorySeparatorChar, Path.AltDirectorySeparatorChar);
        return parts.Any(part => SupportedFilePolicy.ExcludedFolderNames.Contains(part));
    }

    private static bool IsZipEntryInExcludedFolder(string entryPath)
    {
        string[] parts = entryPath.Split('/', '\\');
        return parts.Any(part => SupportedFilePolicy.ExcludedFolderNames.Contains(part));
    }

    private static bool IsSupportedFile(string path)
    {
        return IsSupportedFileName(Path.GetFileName(path));
    }

    private static bool IsSupportedFileName(string fileName)
    {
        return SupportedFilePolicy.IsSupportedTextFileName(fileName);
    }

    private static string GetExtensionText(string fileName)
    {
        if (SupportedFilePolicy.SupportedSpecialFileNames.Contains(fileName) && string.IsNullOrEmpty(Path.GetExtension(fileName)))
        {
            return "[special]";
        }
        return Path.GetExtension(fileName);
    }

    private static DecodedTextResult DecodeTextWithFallback(byte[] bytes)
    {
        DecodedTextResult result = new DecodedTextResult();
        result.HadUtf8Bom = bytes.Length >= 3 && bytes[0] == 0xEF && bytes[1] == 0xBB && bytes[2] == 0xBF;
        try
        {
            result.Text = new UTF8Encoding(false, true).GetString(bytes);
            return result;
        }
        catch (DecoderFallbackException)
        {
            result.Text = Encoding.Default.GetString(bytes);
            result.UsedFallbackEncoding = true;
            return result;
        }
    }

    private static string NormalizeNewLines(string text)
    {
        return TextContentUtility.NormalizeNewLines(text);
    }

    private static int CountLines(string content)
    {
        return TextContentUtility.CountLines(content);
    }

    private static string DetectNewLineStyle(string text)
    {
        return TextContentUtility.DetectNewLineStyle(text);
    }

private static string GetRootName(string sourcePath, InputSourceKind sourceKind)
    {
        if (sourceKind == InputSourceKind.ZipArchive)
        {
            return Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(sourcePath);
        }
        return new DirectoryInfo(sourcePath).Name;
    }

    private static string FormatBytes(long bytes)
    {
        double mb = bytes / 1024d / 1024d;
        return mb.ToString("0.00") + " MB";
    }
}

BEGIN FILE
BEGIN FILE METADATA

using System.Text;

using System.Text.Json;

using System.Text.RegularExpressions;



namespace TextFileCombiner.Core;



internal static class ProjectFileExtractor

{

    private const string Cptf2MagicHeader = AppConstants.Cptf2MagicHeader;

    private const string MetadataPrefix = "' RltvPath: ";

    private const string FullPathMarker = ", FullPath: ";

    private static readonly Regex FileHeaderRegex = new Regex(@"^' .+?-+ \[(\d{3})\]\[([^\]]*)\]\[Lines:\s*(\d+)\]$", RegexOptions.Compiled);

    private static readonly char[] WindowsInvalidFileNameChars =

    {

        '<', '>', ':', '"', '|', '?', '*',

        '\0', '\u0001', '\u0002', '\u0003', '\u0004', '\u0005', '\u0006', '\u0007',

        '\u0008', '\u0009', '\u000A', '\u000B', '\u000C', '\u000D', '\u000E', '\u000F',

        '\u0010', '\u0011', '\u0012', '\u0013', '\u0014', '\u0015', '\u0016', '\u0017',

        '\u0018', '\u0019', '\u001A', '\u001B', '\u001C', '\u001D', '\u001E', '\u001F'

    };

    internal static RestoreResult ExtractProjectFiles(string combinedTextFilePath, string outputDirectory, RestoreOptions options)

    {

        return ExtractProjectFiles(combinedTextFilePath, outputDirectory, options, null);

    }



    internal static RestoreResult ExtractProjectFiles(string combinedTextFilePath, string outputDirectory, RestoreOptions options, IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones)

    {

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(combinedTextFilePath)) throw new ArgumentException("Combined text file path is required.", nameof(combinedTextFilePath));

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(outputDirectory)) throw new ArgumentException("Output directory is required.", nameof(outputDirectory));

        if (options is null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(options));

        if (!File.Exists(combinedTextFilePath)) throw new FileNotFoundException("Combined text file was not found.", combinedTextFilePath);

        if (!options.EnableValidationChecks)

        {

            ReportWarning(milestones, "Validation checks are disabled.", "Minimal output-folder containment is still enforced.");

        }

        ReportStarted(milestones, "Reading combined text file", combinedTextFilePath);

        byte[] combinedBytes = File.ReadAllBytes(combinedTextFilePath);

        string detectedNewLine = Environment.NewLine;

        string detectedProtocolName = string.Empty;

        ReportOk(milestones, "Reading combined text file", $"Read {combinedBytes.Length:N0} byte(s).");

        ReportStarted(milestones, "Parsing file entries");

        ICombinedProjectReader reader = CombinedProjectProtocolRegistry.SelectReader(combinedBytes);

        detectedProtocolName = reader.ProtocolName;

        ReportOk(milestones, "Protocol detection", $"Detected {detectedProtocolName}.");

        List<CombinedFileEntry> entries = reader.Read(combinedBytes, options, milestones, out detectedNewLine).ToList();

        if (entries.Count == 0)

        {

            throw new ExtractValidationException("Parsing", "No file entries were found in the combined text file.");

        }

        ReportOk(milestones, "Parsing file entries", $"Parsed {entries.Count} file entries.");

        RestoreResult result = new RestoreResult();

        result.ProtocolName = detectedProtocolName;

        result.TotalFileCount = entries.Count;

        result.BinaryFileCount = entries.Count(x => string.Equals(x.FileKind, "binary", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) || x.IsBinaryContent);

        result.TextFileCount = entries.Count - result.BinaryFileCount;

        result.Sha256VerificationCount = entries.Count(x => x.IsByteContent);

        string outputRoot = Path.GetFullPath(outputDirectory);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(outputRoot);

        if (options.ValidateOnly || (options.EnableValidationChecks && options.PreflightBeforeWriting))

        {

            ReportStarted(milestones, "Building write plan", "Validating all target paths before writing files.");

            List<RestoreWritePlan> writePlan = BuildWritePlan(entries, outputRoot, options, result, milestones);

            result.FilesPlanned = writePlan.Count(x => !x.SkipExistingFile);

            ReportOk(milestones, "Building write plan", $"Write plan contains {result.FilesPlanned} file(s) to create and {writePlan.Count(x => x.SkipExistingFile)} file(s) to skip.");

            if (options.ValidateOnly)

            {

                ReportDone(milestones, "Validation completed successfully", "No files were written.");

                return result;

            }

            WritePlannedFiles(writePlan, options, detectedNewLine, result, milestones);

            ReportDone(milestones, "Extraction completed successfully", $"Created {result.FilesCreated} file(s), skipped {result.FilesSkipped} file(s).");

            return result;

        }

        if (options.EnableValidationChecks)

        {

            ReportWarning(milestones, "Preflight extraction is disabled.", "Files will be written sequentially after per-file validation.");

        }

        WriteSequentially(entries, outputRoot, options, detectedNewLine, result, milestones);

        ReportDone(milestones, "Extraction completed successfully", $"Created {result.FilesCreated} file(s), skipped {result.FilesSkipped} file(s).");

        return result;

    }



    private static bool StartsWithCptf2MagicHeader(byte[] bytes)

    {

        byte[] magic = Encoding.ASCII.GetBytes(Cptf2MagicHeader);

        if (bytes.Length < magic.Length) return false;

        for (int index = 0; index < magic.Length; index++)

        {

            if (bytes[index] != magic[index]) return false;

        }

        return true;

    }



    internal static List<CombinedFileEntry> ParseCptf2LengthDelimited(byte[] bytes, RestoreOptions options, IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones)

    {

        List<CombinedFileEntry> entries = new List<CombinedFileEntry>();

        HashSet<string> seenRelativePaths = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        int position = 0;

        RequireLine(bytes, ref position, Cptf2MagicHeader);

        SkipBlankLines(bytes, ref position);

        RequireLine(bytes, ref position, "BEGIN PARSER RULES");

        SkipBlock(bytes, ref position, "END PARSER RULES");

        SkipBlankLines(bytes, ref position);

        RequireLine(bytes, ref position, "BEGIN MANIFEST");

        SkipBlock(bytes, ref position, "END MANIFEST");

        SkipBlankLines(bytes, ref position);

        RequireLine(bytes, ref position, "BEGIN PROJECT STRUCTURE");

        SkipBlock(bytes, ref position, "END PROJECT STRUCTURE");

        SkipBlankLines(bytes, ref position);

        RequireLine(bytes, ref position, "BEGIN FILES");

        if (options.EnableValidationChecks && options.DetectDuplicatePaths)

        {

            ReportStarted(milestones, "Checking duplicate relative paths");

        }

        while (true)

        {

            SkipBlankLines(bytes, ref position);

            string? line = ReadLine(bytes, ref position);

            if (line is null) throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 parsing", "Unexpected end of file while reading file blocks.");

            if (line == "END FILES") break;

            if (line != "BEGIN FILE") throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 parsing", $"Expected BEGIN FILE or END FILES, but found: {line}");

            RequireLine(bytes, ref position, "BEGIN FILE METADATA");

            string metadataJson = ReadBlockText(bytes, ref position, "END FILE METADATA");

            CombinedFileEntry entry = ParseCptf2Metadata(metadataJson);

            if (options.EnableValidationChecks && options.DetectDuplicatePaths && !seenRelativePaths.Add(NormalizeRelativePathForComparison(entry.RelativePath)))

            {

                throw new ExtractValidationException("Duplicate relative path", $"Duplicate relative path detected: {entry.RelativePath}", entry.RelativePath);

            }

            RequireLine(bytes, ref position, "BEGIN CONTENT");

            if (entry.ByteLength < 0 || entry.ByteLength > int.MaxValue || position + entry.ByteLength > bytes.Length)

            {

                throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 byteLength", $"Invalid byteLength for {entry.RelativePath}.", entry.RelativePath);

            }

            int contentByteLength = checked((int)entry.ByteLength);

            entry.ContentBytes = new byte[contentByteLength];

            Buffer.BlockCopy(bytes, position, entry.ContentBytes, 0, contentByteLength);

            position += contentByteLength;

            if (string.Equals(entry.FileKind, "binary", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))

            {

                if (!string.Equals(entry.ContentEncoding, "base64", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))

                {

                    throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 binary encoding", $"Unsupported binary content encoding for {entry.RelativePath}: {entry.ContentEncoding}", entry.RelativePath);

                }

                string base64Content = Encoding.ASCII.GetString(entry.ContentBytes);

                byte[] decodedBytes;

                try

                {

                    decodedBytes = Convert.FromBase64String(base64Content);

                }

                catch (FormatException ex)

                {

                    throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 base64", $"Invalid Base64 content for {entry.RelativePath}: {ex.Message}", entry.RelativePath);

                }

                if (entry.OriginalByteLength >= 0 && decodedBytes.LongLength != entry.OriginalByteLength)

                {

                    throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 binary length", $"Decoded binary length mismatch for {entry.RelativePath}.", entry.RelativePath);

                }

                string binarySha256 = HashService.ComputeSha256Hex(decodedBytes);

                if (!string.Equals(binarySha256, entry.Sha256, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))

                {

                    throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 sha256", $"SHA-256 mismatch for {entry.RelativePath}.", entry.RelativePath);

                }

                entry.ContentBytes = decodedBytes;

                entry.IsBinaryContent = true;

            }

            else

            {

                string actualSha256 = HashService.ComputeSha256Hex(entry.ContentBytes);

                if (!string.Equals(actualSha256, entry.Sha256, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))

                {

                    throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 sha256", $"SHA-256 mismatch for {entry.RelativePath}.", entry.RelativePath);

                }

            }

            entry.IsByteContent = true;

            ConsumeOptionalSingleNewLine(bytes, ref position);

            RequireLine(bytes, ref position, "END FILE");

            entries.Add(entry);

        }
        SkipBlankLines(bytes, ref position);
        RequireLine(bytes, ref position, "END CPTF");
        SkipBlankLines(bytes, ref position);
        if (position < bytes.Length)
        {
            throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 parsing", "Unexpected trailing bytes after END CPTF.");
        }
        return entries;
    }



    private static CombinedFileEntry ParseCptf2Metadata(string metadataJson)

    {

        using JsonDocument document = JsonDocument.Parse(metadataJson);

        JsonElement root = document.RootElement;

        CombinedFileEntry entry = new CombinedFileEntry();

        entry.Index = root.GetProperty("index").GetInt32();

        entry.RelativePath = root.GetProperty("relativePath").GetString() ?? string.Empty;

        entry.ExtensionText = root.TryGetProperty("extension", out JsonElement extensionElement) ? extensionElement.GetString() ?? string.Empty : string.Empty;

        entry.DeclaredLineCount = root.TryGetProperty("lineCount", out JsonElement lineCountElement) ? lineCountElement.GetInt32() : 0;

        entry.FileKind = root.TryGetProperty("fileKind", out JsonElement fileKindElement) ? fileKindElement.GetString() ?? "text" : "text";

        entry.ContentEncoding = root.TryGetProperty("contentEncoding", out JsonElement contentEncodingElement) ? contentEncodingElement.GetString() ?? "utf-8-plain-text" : "utf-8-plain-text";

        entry.OriginalByteLength = root.TryGetProperty("originalByteLength", out JsonElement originalByteLengthElement) ? originalByteLengthElement.GetInt64() : 0;

        entry.EncodedByteLength = root.TryGetProperty("encodedByteLength", out JsonElement encodedByteLengthElement) ? encodedByteLengthElement.GetInt64() : 0;

        entry.ByteLength = root.GetProperty("byteLength").GetInt64();

        if (string.Equals(entry.FileKind, "binary", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) && entry.EncodedByteLength > 0)

        {

            entry.ByteLength = entry.EncodedByteLength;

        }

        entry.Sha256 = root.GetProperty("sha256").GetString() ?? string.Empty;

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(entry.RelativePath)) throw new ExtractValidationException("Relative path", "A CPTF/2 file entry has an empty relative path.");

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(entry.Sha256)) throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 sha256", $"Missing SHA-256 hash for {entry.RelativePath}.", entry.RelativePath);

        return entry;

    }



    internal static List<CombinedFileEntry> ParseCombinedText(string combinedText, RestoreOptions options, IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones)

    {

        string normalizedText = combinedText.Replace("\r\n", "\n", StringComparison.Ordinal).Replace("\r", "\n", StringComparison.Ordinal);

        string[] lines = normalizedText.Split('\n');

        List<CombinedFileEntry> entries = new List<CombinedFileEntry>();

        HashSet<string> seenRelativePaths = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        if (options.EnableValidationChecks && options.DetectDuplicatePaths)

        {

            ReportStarted(milestones, "Checking duplicate relative paths");

        }

        int lineIndex = 0;

        while (lineIndex < lines.Length)

        {

            Match headerMatch = FileHeaderRegex.Match(lines[lineIndex]);

            if (!headerMatch.Success || lineIndex + 1 >= lines.Length || !lines[lineIndex + 1].StartsWith(MetadataPrefix, StringComparison.Ordinal))

            {

                lineIndex++;

                continue;

            }

            int entryIndex = int.Parse(headerMatch.Groups[1].Value);

            string extensionText = headerMatch.Groups[2].Value;

            int declaredLineCount = int.Parse(headerMatch.Groups[3].Value);

            string relativePath = ParseRelativePath(lines[lineIndex + 1]);

            if (options.EnableValidationChecks && options.DetectDuplicatePaths && !seenRelativePaths.Add(NormalizeRelativePathForComparison(relativePath)))

            {

                throw new ExtractValidationException("Duplicate relative path", $"Duplicate relative path detected: {relativePath}", relativePath);

            }

            lineIndex += 2;

            if (lineIndex < lines.Length && lines[lineIndex].Length == 0) lineIndex++;

            if (declaredLineCount < 0 || lineIndex + declaredLineCount > lines.Length)

            {

                throw new ExtractValidationException("Line-count validation", $"Invalid or out-of-range line count for {relativePath}.", relativePath);

            }

            string[] contentLines = new string[declaredLineCount];

            Array.Copy(lines, lineIndex, contentLines, 0, declaredLineCount);

            lineIndex += declaredLineCount;

            if (options.EnableValidationChecks && options.ValidateBlockBoundaries)

            {

                ValidateBlockBoundary(lines, lineIndex, relativePath);

            }

            entries.Add(new CombinedFileEntry

            {

                Index = entryIndex,

                RelativePath = relativePath,

                ExtensionText = extensionText,

                DeclaredLineCount = declaredLineCount,

                ContentLines = contentLines

            });

        }

        if (options.EnableValidationChecks && options.DetectDuplicatePaths)

        {

            ReportOk(milestones, "Checking duplicate relative paths", "No duplicate RltvPath entries found.");

        }

        if (options.EnableValidationChecks && options.ValidateBlockBoundaries)

        {

            ReportOk(milestones, "Validating declared line counts / block boundaries", "Block boundaries look valid.");

        }

        return entries;

    }



    private static List<RestoreWritePlan> BuildWritePlan(IReadOnlyList<CombinedFileEntry> entries, string outputRoot, RestoreOptions options, RestoreResult result, IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones)

    {

        List<RestoreWritePlan> writePlan = new List<RestoreWritePlan>();

        HashSet<string> seenTargetPaths = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        ReportValidationMilestonesStarted(options, milestones);

        foreach (CombinedFileEntry entry in entries.OrderBy(x => x.Index))

        {

            RestoreWritePlan? plan = CreateWritePlanForEntry(entry, outputRoot, options, result, seenTargetPaths);

            if (plan is not null) writePlan.Add(plan);

        }

        ReportValidationMilestonesOk(options, milestones);

        return writePlan;

    }



    private static RestoreWritePlan? CreateWritePlanForEntry(CombinedFileEntry entry, string outputRoot, RestoreOptions options, RestoreResult result, HashSet<string> seenTargetPaths)

    {

        string relativePath = options.PreserveRootFolder ? entry.RelativePath : RemoveRootFolder(entry.RelativePath);

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(relativePath))

        {

            result.FilesSkipped++;

            result.Warnings.Add($"Skipped entry with empty relative path: {entry.RelativePath}");

            return null;

        }

        string targetPath = GetSafeTargetPath(outputRoot, relativePath, options);

        if (options.EnableValidationChecks && options.DetectDuplicatePaths && !seenTargetPaths.Add(targetPath))

        {

            throw new ExtractValidationException("Duplicate target path", $"Duplicate target path detected: {relativePath}", relativePath);

        }

        RestoreWritePlan plan = new RestoreWritePlan();

        plan.Entry = entry;

        plan.RelativePath = relativePath;

        plan.TargetPath = targetPath;

        if (File.Exists(targetPath) && !options.OverwriteExistingFiles)

        {

            plan.SkipExistingFile = true;

            result.FilesSkipped++;

            result.Warnings.Add($"Skipped existing file: {relativePath}");

        }

        return plan;

    }



    private static void WritePlannedFiles(IReadOnlyList<RestoreWritePlan> writePlan, RestoreOptions options, string detectedNewLine, RestoreResult result, IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones)

    {

        ReportStarted(milestones, "Writing files", $"Writing {writePlan.Count(x => !x.SkipExistingFile)} file(s).");

        foreach (RestoreWritePlan plan in writePlan)

        {

            if (!plan.SkipExistingFile) WriteSingleFile(plan, options, detectedNewLine, result);

        }

        ReportOk(milestones, "Writing files", $"Created {result.FilesCreated} file(s), skipped {result.FilesSkipped} file(s).");

    }



    private static void WriteSequentially(IReadOnlyList<CombinedFileEntry> entries, string outputRoot, RestoreOptions options, string detectedNewLine, RestoreResult result, IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones)

    {

        ReportStarted(milestones, "Writing files", $"Writing {entries.Count} file entry/entries sequentially.");

        HashSet<string> seenTargetPaths = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        foreach (CombinedFileEntry entry in entries.OrderBy(x => x.Index))

        {

            RestoreWritePlan? plan = CreateWritePlanForEntry(entry, outputRoot, options, result, seenTargetPaths);

            if (plan is not null && !plan.SkipExistingFile) WriteSingleFile(plan, options, detectedNewLine, result);

        }

        ReportOk(milestones, "Writing files", $"Created {result.FilesCreated} file(s), skipped {result.FilesSkipped} file(s).");

    }



    private static void WriteSingleFile(RestoreWritePlan plan, RestoreOptions options, string detectedNewLine, RestoreResult result)

    {

        string? targetDirectory = Path.GetDirectoryName(plan.TargetPath);

        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(targetDirectory) && !Directory.Exists(targetDirectory))

        {

            Directory.CreateDirectory(targetDirectory);

            result.DirectoriesCreated++;

        }

        if (plan.Entry.IsByteContent)

        {

            File.WriteAllBytes(plan.TargetPath, plan.Entry.ContentBytes);

            string writtenSha256 = HashService.ComputeSha256Hex(File.ReadAllBytes(plan.TargetPath));

            if (!string.Equals(writtenSha256, plan.Entry.Sha256, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))

            {

                throw new ExtractValidationException("Written file hash", $"Written file hash mismatch: {plan.RelativePath}", plan.RelativePath);

            }

        }

        else

        {

            File.WriteAllText(plan.TargetPath, JoinContentLines(plan.Entry.ContentLines, options.NewLineMode, detectedNewLine), new UTF8Encoding(false));

        }

        result.FilesCreated++;

    }



    private static void ReportValidationMilestonesStarted(RestoreOptions options, IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones)

    {

        if (!options.EnableValidationChecks) return;

        if (options.ValidatePathSafety) ReportStarted(milestones, "Validating path safety", "Checking absolute paths, path navigation, and output-folder containment.");

        if (options.ValidateWindowsFileNameChars) ReportStarted(milestones, "Validating Windows filename characters");

        if (options.RejectEmptyPathSegments) ReportStarted(milestones, "Checking empty path segments");

        if (options.RejectTrailingSpacesOrDots) ReportStarted(milestones, "Checking trailing spaces or dots");

        if (options.DetectDuplicatePaths) ReportStarted(milestones, "Checking duplicate target paths");

    }



    private static void ReportValidationMilestonesOk(RestoreOptions options, IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones)

    {

        if (!options.EnableValidationChecks) return;

        if (options.ValidatePathSafety) ReportOk(milestones, "Validating path safety", "All target paths remain inside the selected output folder.");

        if (options.ValidateWindowsFileNameChars) ReportOk(milestones, "Validating Windows filename characters", "No invalid Windows filename characters found.");

        if (options.RejectEmptyPathSegments) ReportOk(milestones, "Checking empty path segments", "No empty path segments found.");

        if (options.RejectTrailingSpacesOrDots) ReportOk(milestones, "Checking trailing spaces or dots", "No path segments end with spaces or dots.");

        if (options.DetectDuplicatePaths) ReportOk(milestones, "Checking duplicate target paths", "No duplicate target paths found.");

    }



    private static void ValidateBlockBoundary(string[] lines, int lineIndex, string relativePath)

    {

        int nextIndex = lineIndex;

        while (nextIndex < lines.Length && lines[nextIndex].Length == 0) nextIndex++;

        if (nextIndex >= lines.Length) return;

        Match nextHeaderMatch = FileHeaderRegex.Match(lines[nextIndex]);

        if (nextHeaderMatch.Success)

        {

            if (nextIndex + 1 >= lines.Length || !lines[nextIndex + 1].StartsWith(MetadataPrefix, StringComparison.Ordinal))

            {

                throw new ExtractValidationException("Line-count / block-boundary validation", $"File header after {relativePath} is not followed by metadata.", relativePath);

            }

            return;

        }

        if (lines[nextIndex].StartsWith("' ", StringComparison.Ordinal)) return;

        throw new ExtractValidationException("Line-count / block-boundary validation", $"Unexpected content after {relativePath}. The declared line count may be too small.", relativePath);

    }



    private static string ParseRelativePath(string metadataLine)

    {

        string metadata = metadataLine.Substring(MetadataPrefix.Length);

        int fullPathMarkerIndex = metadata.IndexOf(FullPathMarker, StringComparison.Ordinal);

        string relativePath = fullPathMarkerIndex >= 0 ? metadata.Substring(0, fullPathMarkerIndex) : metadata;

        relativePath = relativePath.Trim();

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(relativePath)) throw new ExtractValidationException("Relative path", "A file entry has an empty relative path.");

        return relativePath;

    }



    private static string RemoveRootFolder(string relativePath)

    {

        string normalizedPath = relativePath.Replace('/', '\\');

        int separatorIndex = normalizedPath.IndexOf('\\');

        return separatorIndex < 0 || separatorIndex == normalizedPath.Length - 1 ? Path.GetFileName(normalizedPath) : normalizedPath.Substring(separatorIndex + 1);

    }



    private static string GetSafeTargetPath(string outputRoot, string relativePath, RestoreOptions options)

    {

        if (options.EnableValidationChecks) ValidateRelativePathSegments(relativePath, options);

        string normalizedRelativePath = relativePath.Replace('/', Path.DirectorySeparatorChar).Replace('\\', Path.DirectorySeparatorChar);

        string targetPath = Path.GetFullPath(Path.Combine(outputRoot, normalizedRelativePath));

        string outputRootWithSeparator = outputRoot.TrimEnd(Path.DirectorySeparatorChar, Path.AltDirectorySeparatorChar) + Path.DirectorySeparatorChar;

        if (!targetPath.Equals(outputRoot, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) && !targetPath.StartsWith(outputRootWithSeparator, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))

        {

            throw new ExtractValidationException("Output-folder containment", $"The target path is outside the output directory: {relativePath}", relativePath);

        }

        return targetPath;

    }



    private static void ValidateRelativePathSegments(string relativePath, RestoreOptions options)

    {

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(relativePath)) throw new ExtractValidationException("Relative path", "Relative path cannot be empty.", relativePath);

        string normalizedPath = relativePath.Replace('/', '\\');

        if (options.ValidatePathSafety && Path.IsPathRooted(normalizedPath)) throw new ExtractValidationException("Path safety", $"Absolute paths are not allowed: {relativePath}", relativePath);

        foreach (string segment in normalizedPath.Split('\\')) ValidatePathSegment(segment, relativePath, options);

    }



    private static void ValidatePathSegment(string segment, string originalPath, RestoreOptions options)

    {

        if (options.RejectEmptyPathSegments && string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(segment)) throw new ExtractValidationException("Empty path segment", $"Invalid empty path segment: {originalPath}", originalPath);

        if (options.ValidatePathSafety && (string.Equals(segment, ".", StringComparison.Ordinal) || string.Equals(segment, "..", StringComparison.Ordinal))) throw new ExtractValidationException("Path safety", $"Relative path navigation is not allowed: {originalPath}", originalPath);

        if (options.RejectTrailingSpacesOrDots && (segment.EndsWith(" ", StringComparison.Ordinal) || segment.EndsWith(".", StringComparison.Ordinal))) throw new ExtractValidationException("Trailing space or dot", $"Path segments cannot end with a space or dot: {originalPath}", originalPath);

        if (options.ValidateWindowsFileNameChars && segment.IndexOfAny(WindowsInvalidFileNameChars) >= 0) throw new ExtractValidationException("Invalid Windows filename character", $"Invalid Windows filename character in path: {originalPath}", originalPath);

    }



    private static string NormalizeRelativePathForComparison(string relativePath) => relativePath.Replace('/', '\\').Trim();

    private static string JoinContentLines(IReadOnlyList<string> contentLines, RestoreNewLineMode newLineMode, string detectedNewLine)

    {

        string newLine = newLineMode switch

        {

            RestoreNewLineMode.UnixLf => "\n",

            RestoreNewLineMode.PreserveCombinedFileNewLines => detectedNewLine,

            _ => "\r\n"

        };

        return string.Join(newLine, contentLines);

    }



    private static string DetectNewLine(string text)

    {

        return TextContentUtility.DetectNewLine(text);

    }



    internal static DecodedTextResult DecodeTextWithFallback(byte[] bytes)

    {

        DecodedTextResult result = new DecodedTextResult();

        try

        {

            result.Text = new UTF8Encoding(false, true).GetString(bytes);

            return result;

        }

        catch (DecoderFallbackException)

        {

            result.Text = Encoding.Default.GetString(bytes);

            result.UsedFallbackEncoding = true;

            return result;

        }

    }



    private static string? ReadLine(byte[] bytes, ref int position)

    {

        if (position >= bytes.Length) return null;

        int start = position;

        while (position < bytes.Length && bytes[position] != (byte)'\n')

        {

            position++;

        }

        int end = position;

        if (end > start && bytes[end - 1] == (byte)'\r')

        {

            end--;

        }

        if (position < bytes.Length && bytes[position] == (byte)'\n')

        {

            position++;

        }

        return new UTF8Encoding(false, true).GetString(bytes, start, end - start);

    }



    private static void RequireLine(byte[] bytes, ref int position, string expectedLine)

    {

        string? actualLine = ReadLine(bytes, ref position);

        if (!string.Equals(actualLine, expectedLine, StringComparison.Ordinal))

        {

            throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 parsing", $"Expected '{expectedLine}', but found '{actualLine ?? "<end-of-file>"}'.");

        }

    }



    private static void SkipBlankLines(byte[] bytes, ref int position)

    {

        while (position < bytes.Length)

        {

            int originalPosition = position;

            string? line = ReadLine(bytes, ref position);

            if (line is null) return;

            if (line.Length != 0)

            {

                position = originalPosition;

                return;

            }

        }

    }



    private static void SkipBlock(byte[] bytes, ref int position, string endMarker)

    {

        while (true)

        {

            string? line = ReadLine(bytes, ref position);

            if (line is null) throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 parsing", $"Unexpected end of file while looking for {endMarker}.");

            if (line == endMarker) return;

        }

    }



    private static string ReadBlockText(byte[] bytes, ref int position, string endMarker)

    {

        StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();

        while (true)

        {

            string? line = ReadLine(bytes, ref position);

            if (line is null) throw new ExtractValidationException("CPTF/2 parsing", $"Unexpected end of file while looking for {endMarker}.");

            if (line == endMarker) return builder.ToString();

            builder.AppendLine(line);

        }

    }



    private static void ConsumeOptionalSingleNewLine(byte[] bytes, ref int position)

    {

        if (position >= bytes.Length) return;

        if (bytes[position] == (byte)'\r' && position + 1 < bytes.Length && bytes[position + 1] == (byte)'\n')

        {

            position += 2;

            return;

        }

        if (bytes[position] == (byte)'\n')

        {

            position++;

        }

    }



private static void ReportStarted(IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones, string message, string detail = "") => Report(milestones, ExtractMilestoneStatus.Started, message, detail);

    private static void ReportOk(IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones, string message, string detail = "") => Report(milestones, ExtractMilestoneStatus.Completed, message, detail);

    private static void ReportWarning(IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones, string message, string detail = "") => Report(milestones, ExtractMilestoneStatus.Warning, message, detail);

    private static void ReportDone(IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones, string message, string detail = "") => Report(milestones, ExtractMilestoneStatus.Done, message, detail);

    private static void Report(IProgress<ExtractMilestone>? milestones, ExtractMilestoneStatus status, string message, string detail)

    {

        if (milestones is null) return;

        ExtractMilestone milestone = new ExtractMilestone();

        milestone.Status = status;

        milestone.Message = message;

        milestone.Detail = detail;

        milestones.Report(milestone);

    }

}

using System.Text;
using System.Text.Json;

namespace TextFileCombiner.Core;

internal static class HandledErrorService
{
    internal static HandledErrorInfo FromException(Exception exception, string operationName)
    {
        if (exception is null)
        {
            return new HandledErrorInfo
            {
                Title = operationName + " failed",
                Message = "An unknown error occurred.",
                Category = "unknown",
                IsHandled = false
            };
        }
        if (exception is AggregateException aggregateException && aggregateException.InnerExceptions.Count == 1)
        {
            exception = aggregateException.InnerExceptions[0];
        }
        HandledErrorInfo info = new HandledErrorInfo();
        info.Title = operationName + " failed";
        info.Message = GetUserMessage(exception);
        info.Detail = GetDetail(exception);
        info.Category = GetCategory(exception);
        info.IsHandled = IsHandledException(exception);
        return info;
    }

    internal static bool IsHandledException(Exception exception)
    {
        return exception is ExtractValidationException
            || exception is CliOperationException
            || exception is ArgumentException
            || exception is InvalidOperationException
            || exception is IOException
            || exception is UnauthorizedAccessException
            || exception is NotSupportedException
            || exception is FormatException
            || exception is JsonException
            || exception is DecoderFallbackException
            || exception is System.Security.SecurityException;
    }

    private static string GetUserMessage(Exception exception)
    {
        if (exception is ExtractValidationException validationException)
        {
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(validationException.RelativePath))
            {
                return validationException.CheckName + " failed for " + validationException.RelativePath + ": " + validationException.Message;
            }
            return validationException.CheckName + " failed: " + validationException.Message;
        }
        if (exception is CliOperationException cliOperationException) return cliOperationException.Message;
        if (exception is FileNotFoundException fileNotFoundException)
        {
            return !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fileNotFoundException.FileName) ? "The file was not found: " + fileNotFoundException.FileName : fileNotFoundException.Message;
        }
        if (exception is DirectoryNotFoundException) return "The folder was not found or is no longer accessible. " + exception.Message;
        if (exception is UnauthorizedAccessException) return "Access was denied. Check file/folder permissions or choose another location. " + exception.Message;
        if (exception is PathTooLongException) return "The file or folder path is too long. Choose a shorter path. " + exception.Message;
        if (exception is IOException) return "A file I/O error occurred. The file may be locked, missing, or inaccessible. " + exception.Message;
        if (exception is ArgumentException) return "One of the supplied values is invalid. " + exception.Message;
        if (exception is InvalidOperationException) return exception.Message;
        if (exception is JsonException) return "The file contains invalid or unsupported JSON metadata. " + exception.Message;
        if (exception is FormatException) return "The file format is invalid or unsupported. " + exception.Message;
        if (exception is DecoderFallbackException) return "The file contains text that could not be decoded as valid UTF-8.";
        return "An unexpected error occurred. " + exception.Message;
    }

    private static string GetCategory(Exception exception)
    {
        if (exception is ExtractValidationException) return "validation";
        if (exception is CliOperationException) return "cli";
        if (exception is ArgumentException) return "input";
        if (exception is FileNotFoundException || exception is DirectoryNotFoundException) return "not-found";
        if (exception is UnauthorizedAccessException || exception is System.Security.SecurityException) return "access-denied";
        if (exception is IOException) return "io";
        if (exception is JsonException || exception is FormatException) return "format";
        if (exception is DecoderFallbackException) return "encoding";
        if (exception is InvalidOperationException) return "operation";
        return "unexpected";
    }

    private static string GetDetail(Exception exception)
    {
        StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
        builder.AppendLine("Exception type: " + exception.GetType().Name);
        if (exception is ExtractValidationException validationException)
        {
            builder.AppendLine("Check: " + validationException.CheckName);
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(validationException.RelativePath)) builder.AppendLine("Relative path: " + validationException.RelativePath);
        }
        if (exception.InnerException is not null) builder.AppendLine("Inner exception: " + exception.InnerException.GetType().Name + ": " + exception.InnerException.Message);
        return builder.ToString().TrimEnd();
    }
}

using System.Security.Cryptography;

namespace TextFileCombiner.Core;

internal static class HashService
{
    internal static string ComputeSha256Hex(byte[] bytes)
    {
        byte[] hash = SHA256.HashData(bytes);
        return Convert.ToHexString(hash).ToLowerInvariant();
    }
}

namespace TextFileCombiner.Core;

internal static class SupportedFilePolicy
{
    internal static readonly HashSet<string> SupportedTextFileExtensions = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
    {
        ".txt", ".cs", ".csproj", ".sln", ".slnf", ".config", ".json", ".xml", ".xaml", ".resx",
        ".targets", ".props", ".md", ".editorconfig", ".yml", ".yaml", ".csv", ".log", ".sql", ".tsql",
        ".cshtml", ".razor", ".js", ".ts", ".css", ".scss", ".html", ".htm", ".cmd", ".bat", ".ps1",
        ".nuspec", ".pubxml", ".ruleset"
    };
    internal static readonly HashSet<string> SupportedSpecialFileNames = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
    {
        ".gitignore", ".gitattributes", ".editorconfig", "global.json", "nuget.config",
        "Directory.Build.props", "Directory.Build.targets", "Directory.Packages.props"
    };
    internal static readonly HashSet<string> SupportedBinaryFileExtensions = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
    {
        ".ico", ".png"
    };
    internal static readonly HashSet<string> ExcludedFolderNames = new HashSet<string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
    {
        "bin", "obj", ".vs", "packages", "node_modules"
    };
    internal static bool IsSupportedTextFileName(string fileName)
    {
        return SupportedSpecialFileNames.Contains(fileName)
            || SupportedTextFileExtensions.Contains(Path.GetExtension(fileName));
    }

    internal static bool IsSupportedBinaryAssetName(string fileName)
    {
        return SupportedBinaryFileExtensions.Contains(Path.GetExtension(fileName));
    }

    internal static bool ShouldIncludeBinaryAsset(string fileName, AppSettings settings)
    {
        return settings.OutputProtocol == CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol.Cptf2LengthDelimited
            && settings.IncludeImageAssetsInCptf2
            && IsSupportedBinaryAssetName(fileName);
    }

    internal static string GetSupportedTextFileSummary() => string.Join(", ", SupportedTextFileExtensions.OrderBy(x => x));
    internal static string GetSpecialFileSummary() => string.Join(", ", SupportedSpecialFileNames.OrderBy(x => x));
    internal static string GetBinaryFileSummary() => string.Join(", ", SupportedBinaryFileExtensions.OrderBy(x => x));
    internal static string GetExcludedFolderSummary() => string.Join(", ", ExcludedFolderNames.OrderBy(x => x));
}
