namespace TextFileCombiner.Core;

internal static class TextContentUtility
{
    internal static string NormalizeNewLines(string text)
    {
        return text
            .Replace("\r\n", "\n", StringComparison.Ordinal)
            .Replace("\r", "\n", StringComparison.Ordinal)
            .Replace("\n", "\r\n", StringComparison.Ordinal);
    }

    internal static int CountLines(string content)
    {
        if (content.Length == 0)
        {
            return 0;
        }
        return content.Split(
            new[] { "\r\n" },
            StringSplitOptions.None
        ).Length;
    }

    internal static string DetectNewLineStyle(string text)
    {
        if (text.Contains("\r\n", StringComparison.Ordinal)) return "crlf";
        if (text.Contains("\n", StringComparison.Ordinal)) return "lf";
        if (text.Contains("\r", StringComparison.Ordinal)) return "cr";
        return "none";
    }

    internal static string DetectNewLine(string text)
    {
        if (text.Contains("\r\n", StringComparison.Ordinal)) return "\r\n";
        if (text.Contains("\n", StringComparison.Ordinal)) return "\n";
        if (text.Contains("\r", StringComparison.Ordinal)) return "\r";
        return Environment.NewLine;
    }
}

using System.Text;
using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed class AboutForm : Form
{
    private readonly TabControl tabControl = new TabControl();
    private readonly TextBox txtAbout = new TextBox();
    private readonly TextBox txtReleaseNotes = new TextBox();
    private readonly TextBox txtLicense = new TextBox();
    private readonly Button btnClose = new Button();

    internal AboutForm()
    {
        Text = "About Text File Combiner";
        StartPosition = FormStartPosition.CenterParent;
        Size = new Size(900, 700);
        MinimumSize = new Size(760, 520);
        BuildLayout();
        Shown += (_, _) =>
        {
            tabControl.SelectedIndex = 0;
            btnClose.Focus();
            ClearTextSelection(txtAbout);
            ClearTextSelection(txtReleaseNotes);
            ClearTextSelection(txtLicense);
        };
    }

    private void BuildLayout()
    {
        TableLayoutPanel root = new TableLayoutPanel
        {
            Dock = DockStyle.Fill,
            ColumnCount = 1,
            RowCount = 2,
            Padding = new Padding(14)
        };
        root.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.Percent, 100));
        root.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        Controls.Add(root);

        tabControl.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        root.Controls.Add(tabControl, 0, 0);

        TabPage aboutPage = new TabPage("About");
        TabPage releaseNotesPage = new TabPage("Release notes");
        TabPage licensePage = new TabPage("License");
        tabControl.TabPages.Add(aboutPage);
        tabControl.TabPages.Add(releaseNotesPage);
        tabControl.TabPages.Add(licensePage);

        ConfigureReadOnlyTextBox(txtAbout, BuildAboutText());
        ConfigureReadOnlyTextBox(txtReleaseNotes, LoadDocumentationText("RELEASE_NOTES.md", BuildMissingDocumentMessage("RELEASE_NOTES.md")));
        ConfigureReadOnlyTextBox(txtLicense, LoadDocumentationText("LICENSE.md", LoadDocumentationText("LICENSE", BuildMissingDocumentMessage("LICENSE.md or LICENSE"))));
        aboutPage.Controls.Add(txtAbout);
        releaseNotesPage.Controls.Add(txtReleaseNotes);
        licensePage.Controls.Add(txtLicense);

        FlowLayoutPanel buttons = new FlowLayoutPanel
        {
            Dock = DockStyle.Fill,
            FlowDirection = FlowDirection.RightToLeft,
            AutoSize = true
        };
        btnClose.Text = "Close";
        btnClose.DialogResult = DialogResult.OK;
        btnClose.Width = 100;
        buttons.Controls.Add(btnClose);
        root.Controls.Add(buttons, 0, 1);
        AcceptButton = btnClose;
    }

    private static void ConfigureReadOnlyTextBox(TextBox textBox, string text)
    {
        textBox.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        textBox.Multiline = true;
        textBox.ReadOnly = true;
        textBox.ScrollBars = ScrollBars.Both;
        textBox.WordWrap = false;
        textBox.Font = new Font(FontFamily.GenericMonospace, 9F);
        textBox.Text = text;
        ClearTextSelection(textBox);
    }

    private static void ClearTextSelection(TextBox textBox)
    {
        textBox.SelectionStart = 0;
        textBox.SelectionLength = 0;
    }

    private static string BuildAboutText()
    {
        StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
        builder.AppendLine(AppVersion.ProductName + " " + AppVersion.Version);
        builder.AppendLine("==============================");
        builder.AppendLine();
        builder.AppendLine("CPTF/2 protocol version: " + AppConstants.Cptf2ProtocolVersion);
        builder.AppendLine("Parser profile: " + AppConstants.Cptf2ParserProfile);
        builder.AppendLine("Protocol name: " + AppConstants.Cptf2LengthDelimitedName);
        builder.AppendLine();
        builder.AppendLine("Text File Combiner creates, validates, and restores combined project files.");
        builder.AppendLine("Version 1.2.0 focuses on CPTF/2 v3.4.1 length-delimited output, SHA-256 verification, embedded-index metadata, CLI reporting, and selected-path extraction.");
        builder.AppendLine();
        builder.AppendLine("Main capabilities");
        builder.AppendLine("- Combine a folder or ZIP source into CPTF/1 or CPTF/2 output.");
        builder.AppendLine("- Restore a full combined project.");
        builder.AppendLine("- Validate CPTF/2 structure, metadata, payload byte lengths, paths, Base64 payloads, and SHA-256 values.");
        builder.AppendLine("- Extract one selected file or all files under a selected folder from a CPTF/2 combined file.");
        builder.AppendLine("- Use the WinForms CPTF/2 picker to select files/folders from the combined file metadata tree.");
        builder.AppendLine();
        builder.AppendLine("Release notes, CLI commands, and license text are loaded from the docs folder next to the executable.");
        return builder.ToString();
    }

    private static string LoadDocumentationText(string fileName, string fallback)
    {
        foreach (string candidatePath in EnumerateDocumentationCandidatePaths(fileName))
        {
            if (File.Exists(candidatePath))
            {
                return File.ReadAllText(candidatePath, Encoding.UTF8);
            }
        }
        return fallback;
    }

    private static IEnumerable<string> EnumerateDocumentationCandidatePaths(string fileName)
    {
        string baseDirectory = AppContext.BaseDirectory;
        yield return Path.Combine(baseDirectory, "docs", fileName);
        yield return Path.Combine(baseDirectory, fileName);
        yield return Path.Combine(Environment.CurrentDirectory, "docs", fileName);
        yield return Path.Combine(Environment.CurrentDirectory, fileName);
    }

    private static string BuildMissingDocumentMessage(string fileName)
    {
        return "Documentation file was not found: " + fileName + Environment.NewLine
            + Environment.NewLine
            + "Expected location: docs folder next to the executable." + Environment.NewLine
            + "Verify that the docs files are copied to the output directory during build.";
    }
}

  <!--
    Microsoft ResX Schema
    Version 2.0
    The primary goals of this format is to allow a simple XML format
    that is mostly human readable. The generation and parsing of the
    various data types are done through the TypeConverter classes
    associated with the data types.
    Example:
    ... ado.net/XML headers & schema ...
    <resheader name="resmimetype">text/microsoft-resx</resheader>
    <resheader name="version">2.0</resheader>
    <resheader name="reader">System.Resources.ResXResourceReader, System.Windows.Forms, ...</resheader>
    <resheader name="writer">System.Resources.ResXResourceWriter, System.Windows.Forms, ...</resheader>
    <data name="Name1"><value>this is my long string</value><comment>this is a comment</comment></data>
    <data name="Color1" type="System.Drawing.Color, System.Drawing">Blue</data>
    <data name="Bitmap1" mimetype="application/x-microsoft.net.object.binary.base64">
        <value>[base64 mime encoded serialized .NET Framework object]</value>
    </data>
    <data name="Icon1" type="System.Drawing.Icon, System.Drawing" mimetype="application/x-microsoft.net.object.bytearray.base64">
        <value>[base64 mime encoded string representing a byte array form of the .NET Framework object]</value>
        <comment>This is a comment</comment>
    </data>
    There are any number of "resheader" rows that contain simple
    name/value pairs.
    Each data row contains a name, and value. The row also contains a
    type or mimetype. Type corresponds to a .NET class that support
    text/value conversion through the TypeConverter architecture.
    Classes that don't support this are serialized and stored with the
    mimetype set.
    The mimetype is used for serialized objects, and tells the
    ResXResourceReader how to depersist the object. This is currently not
    extensible. For a given mimetype the value must be set accordingly:
    Note - application/x-microsoft.net.object.binary.base64 is the format
    that the ResXResourceWriter will generate, however the reader can
    read any of the formats listed below.
    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.binary.base64
    value   : The object must be serialized with
            : System.Runtime.Serialization.Formatters.Binary.BinaryFormatter
            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.
    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.soap.base64
    value   : The object must be serialized with
            : System.Runtime.Serialization.Formatters.Soap.SoapFormatter
            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.
    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.bytearray.base64
    value   : The object must be serialized into a byte array
            : using a System.ComponentModel.TypeConverter
            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.
    -->

using System.Text;
using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed class CliCommandsForm : Form
{
    private readonly TextBox txtCommands = new TextBox();
    private readonly Button btnClose = new Button();

    internal CliCommandsForm()
    {
        Text = "CLI commands";
        StartPosition = FormStartPosition.CenterParent;
        Size = new Size(980, 720);
        MinimumSize = new Size(820, 560);
        BuildLayout();
        Shown += (_, _) =>
        {
            btnClose.Focus();
            txtCommands.SelectionStart = 0;
            txtCommands.SelectionLength = 0;
        };
    }

    private void BuildLayout()
    {
        TableLayoutPanel root = new TableLayoutPanel
        {
            Dock = DockStyle.Fill,
            ColumnCount = 1,
            RowCount = 3,
            Padding = new Padding(14)
        };
        root.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        root.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.Percent, 100));
        root.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        Controls.Add(root);

        Label title = new Label
        {
            AutoSize = true,
            Font = new Font(Font.FontFamily, 12F, FontStyle.Bold),
            Text = "TextFileCombiner.Cli commands - " + AppVersion.Version
        };
        root.Controls.Add(title, 0, 0);

        txtCommands.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        txtCommands.Multiline = true;
        txtCommands.ReadOnly = true;
        txtCommands.ScrollBars = ScrollBars.Both;
        txtCommands.WordWrap = false;
        txtCommands.Font = new Font(FontFamily.GenericMonospace, 9F);
        txtCommands.Text = LoadCliCommandsText();
        txtCommands.SelectionStart = 0;
        txtCommands.SelectionLength = 0;
        root.Controls.Add(txtCommands, 0, 1);

        FlowLayoutPanel buttons = new FlowLayoutPanel
        {
            Dock = DockStyle.Fill,
            FlowDirection = FlowDirection.RightToLeft,
            AutoSize = true
        };
        btnClose.Text = "Close";
        btnClose.DialogResult = DialogResult.OK;
        btnClose.Width = 100;
        buttons.Controls.Add(btnClose);
        root.Controls.Add(buttons, 0, 2);
        AcceptButton = btnClose;
    }

    private static string LoadCliCommandsText()
    {
        foreach (string candidatePath in EnumerateDocumentationCandidatePaths("CLI_COMMANDS.md"))
        {
            if (File.Exists(candidatePath))
            {
                return File.ReadAllText(candidatePath, Encoding.UTF8);
            }
        }

        return "CLI command documentation was not found." + Environment.NewLine
            + Environment.NewLine
            + @"Expected location: docs\CLI_COMMANDS.md next to the executable." + Environment.NewLine
            + "Verify that the docs files are copied to the output directory during build.";
    }

    private static IEnumerable<string> EnumerateDocumentationCandidatePaths(string fileName)
    {
        string baseDirectory = AppContext.BaseDirectory;
        yield return Path.Combine(baseDirectory, "docs", fileName);
        yield return Path.Combine(baseDirectory, fileName);
        yield return Path.Combine(Environment.CurrentDirectory, "docs", fileName);
        yield return Path.Combine(Environment.CurrentDirectory, fileName);
    }
}

END FILE

<root>
  <!-- 
    Microsoft ResX Schema 
    
    Version 2.0
    
    The primary goals of this format is to allow a simple XML format 
    that is mostly human readable. The generation and parsing of the 
    various data types are done through the TypeConverter classes 
    associated with the data types.
    
    Example:
    
    ... ado.net/XML headers & schema ...
    <resheader name="resmimetype">text/microsoft-resx</resheader>
    <resheader name="version">2.0</resheader>
    <resheader name="reader">System.Resources.ResXResourceReader, System.Windows.Forms, ...</resheader>
    <resheader name="writer">System.Resources.ResXResourceWriter, System.Windows.Forms, ...</resheader>
    <data name="Name1"><value>this is my long string</value><comment>this is a comment</comment></data>
    <data name="Color1" type="System.Drawing.Color, System.Drawing">Blue</data>
    <data name="Bitmap1" mimetype="application/x-microsoft.net.object.binary.base64">
        <value>[base64 mime encoded serialized .NET Framework object]</value>
    </data>
    <data name="Icon1" type="System.Drawing.Icon, System.Drawing" mimetype="application/x-microsoft.net.object.bytearray.base64">
        <value>[base64 mime encoded string representing a byte array form of the .NET Framework object]</value>
        <comment>This is a comment</comment>
    </data>
                
    There are any number of "resheader" rows that contain simple 
    name/value pairs.
    
    Each data row contains a name, and value. The row also contains a 
    type or mimetype. Type corresponds to a .NET class that support 
    text/value conversion through the TypeConverter architecture. 
    Classes that don't support this are serialized and stored with the 
    mimetype set.
    
    The mimetype is used for serialized objects, and tells the 
    ResXResourceReader how to depersist the object. This is currently not 
    extensible. For a given mimetype the value must be set accordingly:
    
    Note - application/x-microsoft.net.object.binary.base64 is the format 
    that the ResXResourceWriter will generate, however the reader can 
    read any of the formats listed below.
    
    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.binary.base64
    value   : The object must be serialized with 
            : System.Runtime.Serialization.Formatters.Binary.BinaryFormatter
            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.
    
    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.soap.base64
    value   : The object must be serialized with 
            : System.Runtime.Serialization.Formatters.Soap.SoapFormatter
            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.

    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.bytearray.base64
    value   : The object must be serialized into a byte array 
            : using a System.ComponentModel.TypeConverter
            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.
    -->

              <xsd:attribute ref="xml:space" />

          </xsd:element>
          <xsd:element name="resheader">
            <xsd:complexType>
              <xsd:sequence>
                <xsd:element name="value" type="xsd:string" minOccurs="0" msdata:Ordinal="1" />
              </xsd:sequence>
              <xsd:attribute name="name" type="xsd:string" use="required" />
            </xsd:complexType>
          </xsd:element>
        </xsd:choice>
      </xsd:complexType>
    </xsd:element>
  </xsd:schema>
  <resheader name="resmimetype">
    <value>text/microsoft-resx</value>

using System.Text;
using System.Text.Json;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed class Cptf2StructurePickerForm : Form
{
    private readonly TreeView treeProject = new TreeView();
    private readonly TextBox txtSelectedPath = new TextBox();
    private readonly Button btnSelect = new Button();
    private readonly Button btnCancel = new Button();
    private readonly string combinedFilePath;

    internal Cptf2StructurePickerForm(string combinedFilePath)
    {
        this.combinedFilePath = combinedFilePath;
        Text = "Select file or folder inside CPTF/2 file";
        StartPosition = FormStartPosition.CenterParent;
        Size = new Size(820, 620);
        BuildLayout();
        LoadStructure();
    }

    internal string SelectedRelativePath { get; private set; } = string.Empty;

    private void BuildLayout()
    {
        TableLayoutPanel root = new TableLayoutPanel { Dock = DockStyle.Fill, ColumnCount = 1, RowCount = 4, Padding = new Padding(12) };
        root.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        root.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.Percent, 100));
        root.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        root.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        Controls.Add(root);

        Label lblInfo = new Label
        {
            AutoSize = true,
            Text = "Select a file or folder from the combined file. Selecting a folder extracts all files below that folder."
        };
        root.Controls.Add(lblInfo, 0, 0);

        treeProject.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        treeProject.HideSelection = false;
        treeProject.AfterSelect += (_, _) => UpdateSelectedPath();
        treeProject.NodeMouseDoubleClick += (_, _) => AcceptSelection();
        root.Controls.Add(treeProject, 0, 1);

        txtSelectedPath.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        txtSelectedPath.ReadOnly = true;
        root.Controls.Add(txtSelectedPath, 0, 2);

        FlowLayoutPanel buttons = new FlowLayoutPanel { Dock = DockStyle.Fill, FlowDirection = FlowDirection.RightToLeft, AutoSize = true };
        btnSelect.Text = "Select";
        btnSelect.Width = 100;
        btnSelect.Enabled = false;
        btnSelect.Click += (_, _) => AcceptSelection();
        btnCancel.Text = "Cancel";
        btnCancel.Width = 100;
        btnCancel.DialogResult = DialogResult.Cancel;
        buttons.Controls.Add(btnSelect);
        buttons.Controls.Add(btnCancel);
        root.Controls.Add(buttons, 0, 3);

        AcceptButton = btnSelect;
        CancelButton = btnCancel;
    }

    private void LoadStructure()
    {
        List<string> paths = ReadRelativePaths(combinedFilePath);
        if (paths.Count == 0)
        {
            MessageBox.Show(this, "No project files were found in the selected combined file.", "No files", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Information);
            return;
        }

        treeProject.BeginUpdate();
        try
        {
            treeProject.Nodes.Clear();
            foreach (string path in paths.OrderBy(x => x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                AddPath(path);
            }
            foreach (TreeNode node in treeProject.Nodes)
            {
                node.Expand();
            }
        }
        finally
        {
            treeProject.EndUpdate();
        }
    }

    private void AddPath(string relativePath)
    {
        string normalized = relativePath.Replace('\\', '/').Trim('/');
        string[] segments = normalized.Split('/', StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);
        TreeNodeCollection collection = treeProject.Nodes;
        string currentPath = string.Empty;
        for (int index = 0; index < segments.Length; index++)
        {
            string segment = segments[index];
            currentPath = currentPath.Length == 0 ? segment : currentPath + "\\" + segment;
            TreeNode? node = FindNode(collection, segment);
            if (node is null)
            {
                node = new TreeNode(segment) { Tag = currentPath };
                collection.Add(node);
            }
            else
            {
                node.Tag = currentPath;
            }
            collection = node.Nodes;
        }
    }

    private static TreeNode? FindNode(TreeNodeCollection collection, string text)
    {
        foreach (TreeNode node in collection)
        {
            if (string.Equals(node.Text, text, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                return node;
            }
        }
        return null;
    }

    private void UpdateSelectedPath()
    {
        string selectedPath = treeProject.SelectedNode?.Tag as string ?? string.Empty;
        txtSelectedPath.Text = selectedPath;
        btnSelect.Enabled = selectedPath.Length > 0;
    }

    private void AcceptSelection()
    {
        string selectedPath = treeProject.SelectedNode?.Tag as string ?? string.Empty;
        if (selectedPath.Length == 0)
        {
            return;
        }
        SelectedRelativePath = selectedPath;
        DialogResult = DialogResult.OK;
        Close();
    }

    private static List<string> ReadRelativePaths(string combinedFilePath)
    {
        byte[] bytes = File.ReadAllBytes(combinedFilePath);
        ReaderState state = new ReaderState(bytes);
        RequireLine(state, "CPTF/2");
        SkipBlankLines(state);
        RequireSection(state, "BEGIN PARSER RULES", "END PARSER RULES");
        SkipBlankLines(state);
        RequireSection(state, "BEGIN MANIFEST", "END MANIFEST");
        SkipBlankLines(state);
        RequireSection(state, "BEGIN PROJECT STRUCTURE", "END PROJECT STRUCTURE");
        SkipBlankLines(state);
        RequireLine(state, "BEGIN FILES");

        List<string> paths = new List<string>();
        while (true)
        {
            SkipBlankLines(state);
            string marker = ReadLine(state);
            if (string.Equals(marker, "END FILES", StringComparison.Ordinal))
            {
                break;
            }
            if (!string.Equals(marker, "BEGIN FILE", StringComparison.Ordinal))
            {
                throw new InvalidDataException("Expected BEGIN FILE or END FILES.");
            }

            RequireLine(state, "BEGIN FILE METADATA");
            string metadataJson = ReadBlock(state, "END FILE METADATA");
            using JsonDocument document = JsonDocument.Parse(metadataJson);
            JsonElement metadata = document.RootElement;
            string relativePath = metadata.TryGetProperty("relativePath", out JsonElement relativePathElement)
                ? relativePathElement.GetString() ?? string.Empty
                : string.Empty;
            bool isInternal = metadata.TryGetProperty("internal", out JsonElement internalElement) && internalElement.ValueKind == JsonValueKind.True;
            string normalized = relativePath.Replace('\\', '/');
            RequireLine(state, "BEGIN CONTENT");
            long byteLength = metadata.TryGetProperty("byteLength", out JsonElement byteLengthElement) && byteLengthElement.TryGetInt64(out long parsed)
                ? parsed
                : -1;
            if (byteLength < 0 || byteLength > int.MaxValue)
            {
                throw new InvalidDataException("Invalid byteLength in CPTF/2 metadata.");
            }
            state.SkipBytes((int)byteLength);
            ConsumeOptionalNewLine(state);
            RequireLine(state, "END FILE");

            if (!isInternal && !normalized.StartsWith("__cptf__/", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) && relativePath.Length > 0)
            {
                paths.Add(relativePath);
            }
        }

        return paths;
    }

    private static void RequireSection(ReaderState state, string begin, string end)
    {
        RequireLine(state, begin);
        ReadBlock(state, end);
    }

    private static void RequireLine(ReaderState state, string expected)
    {
        string actual = ReadLine(state);
        if (!string.Equals(actual, expected, StringComparison.Ordinal))
        {
            throw new InvalidDataException($"Expected '{expected}', got '{actual}'.");
        }
    }

    private static string ReadBlock(ReaderState state, string endMarker)
    {
        StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
        while (!state.EndOfFile)
        {
            string line = ReadLine(state);
            if (string.Equals(line, endMarker, StringComparison.Ordinal))
            {
                return builder.ToString();
            }
            builder.AppendLine(line);
        }
        throw new InvalidDataException("Unexpected end of file while reading CPTF/2 block.");
    }

    private static void SkipBlankLines(ReaderState state)
    {
        while (!state.EndOfFile)
        {
            int saved = state.Position;
            string line = ReadLine(state);
            if (line.Length != 0)
            {
                state.Position = saved;
                return;
            }
        }
    }

    private static string ReadLine(ReaderState state)
    {
        int start = state.Position;
        while (state.Position < state.Bytes.Length && state.Bytes[state.Position] != (byte)'\n')
        {
            state.Position++;
        }
        int length = state.Position - start;
        if (state.Position < state.Bytes.Length && state.Bytes[state.Position] == (byte)'\n')
        {
            state.Position++;
        }
        if (length > 0 && state.Bytes[start + length - 1] == (byte)'\r')
        {
            length--;
        }
        return Encoding.UTF8.GetString(state.Bytes, start, length);
    }

    private static void ConsumeOptionalNewLine(ReaderState state)
    {
        if (state.Position < state.Bytes.Length && state.Bytes[state.Position] == (byte)'\r')
        {
            state.Position++;
        }
        if (state.Position < state.Bytes.Length && state.Bytes[state.Position] == (byte)'\n')
        {
            state.Position++;
        }
    }

    private sealed class ReaderState
    {
        internal ReaderState(byte[] bytes)
        {
            Bytes = bytes;
        }
        internal byte[] Bytes { get; }
        internal int Position { get; set; }
        internal bool EndOfFile => Position >= Bytes.Length;
        internal void SkipBytes(int length)
        {
            if (Position + length > Bytes.Length)
            {
                throw new InvalidDataException("CPTF/2 content payload is shorter than declared byteLength.");
            }
            Position += length;
        }
    }
}

using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed class IndexedExtractOneForm : Form
{
    private readonly TextBox txtCombinedFile = new TextBox();
    private readonly TextBox txtRelativePath = new TextBox();
    private readonly TextBox txtOutputFolder = new TextBox();

    private readonly CheckBox chkValidateOnly = new CheckBox();

    internal IndexedExtractOneForm()
    {
        Text = "CPTF/2 indexed extract selected path";
        StartPosition = FormStartPosition.CenterParent;
        Size = new Size(900, 380);
        BuildLayout();
        ConfigureToolTips();
        UpdateSelectRelativePathButtonState();

    internal string CombinedFilePath => txtCombinedFile.Text.Trim();
    internal string RelativePath => txtRelativePath.Text.Trim();
    internal string OutputFolderPath => txtOutputFolder.Text.Trim();
    internal RestoreIndexMode IndexMode => cboIndexMode.SelectedIndex switch
    {
        0 => RestoreIndexMode.Sequential,
        2 => RestoreIndexMode.IndexedOnly,
        _ => RestoreIndexMode.AutoIndexed

    private void BuildLayout()

        AddPathInsideCombinedRow(root, 1);
        AddPathRow(root, 2, "Output folder", txtOutputFolder, BrowseOutput);

        cboIndexMode.DropDownStyle = ComboBoxStyle.DropDownList;
        cboIndexMode.Items.AddRange(new object[] { "Sequential", "Auto-indexed", "Indexed-only" });
        cboIndexMode.SelectedIndex = 1;
        AddControlRow(root, 3, "Index mode", cboIndexMode);

        chkOverwrite.Text = "Overwrite";
        chkValidateOnly.Text = "Validate only; do not write files";
        AddControlRow(root, 4, string.Empty, chkOverwrite);
        AddControlRow(root, 5, string.Empty, chkValidateOnly);

        Label lblHint = new Label
        {
            AutoSize = true,
            Text = "Tip: use Select... to choose a file or folder from the combined file. Selecting a folder extracts all files below it."
        };
        root.Controls.Add(lblHint, 1, 6);
        root.SetColumnSpan(lblHint, 2);

        FlowLayoutPanel buttons = new FlowLayoutPanel { FlowDirection = FlowDirection.RightToLeft, Dock = DockStyle.Fill };
        Button ok = new Button { Text = "Extract", DialogResult = DialogResult.None, Width = 100 };
        Button cancel = new Button { Text = "Cancel", DialogResult = DialogResult.Cancel, Width = 100 };
        ok.Click += (_, _) => AcceptIfValid();
        buttons.Controls.Add(ok);
        buttons.Controls.Add(cancel);
        root.Controls.Add(buttons, 1, 7);
        root.SetColumnSpan(buttons, 2);

        txtCombinedFile.TextChanged += (_, _) =>
        {
            UpdateSelectRelativePathButtonState();
            AutoFillOutputFolderFromCombinedFile();
        };

        AcceptButton = ok;
        CancelButton = cancel;
    }

        toolTip.SetToolTip(txtOutputFolder, "Destination folder where the selected file or folder will be extracted.");
        toolTip.SetToolTip(cboIndexMode, "Sequential: scan entries. Auto-indexed: use index when available/fall back safely. Indexed-only: require embedded index.");
        toolTip.SetToolTip(chkOverwrite, "Overwrite existing files in the output folder.");
        toolTip.SetToolTip(chkValidateOnly, "Validate the selected file/folder extraction without writing files.");
    }

    private static void AddLabel(TableLayoutPanel root, int row, string text)

        root.Controls.Add(new Label { Text = text, AutoSize = true, Anchor = AnchorStyles.Left }, 0, row);

    private static void AddTextRow(TableLayoutPanel root, int row, string label, TextBox textBox)

    {
        AddLabel(root, row, label);
        textBox.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        root.Controls.Add(textBox, 1, row);
        Button browse = new Button { Text = "Browse...", Dock = DockStyle.Fill };
        browse.Click += browseHandler;
        root.Controls.Add(browse, 2, row);
    }

    private void AddPathInsideCombinedRow(TableLayoutPanel root, int row)
    {
        AddLabel(root, row, "Path inside combined file");
        txtRelativePath.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        root.Controls.Add(txtRelativePath, 1, row);
        btnSelectRelativePath.Text = "Select...";
        btnSelectRelativePath.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        btnSelectRelativePath.Click += SelectRelativePath;
        root.Controls.Add(btnSelectRelativePath, 2, row);
    }

    private static void AddControlRow(TableLayoutPanel root, int row, string label, Control control)
    {
        AddLabel(root, row, label);
        control.Dock = DockStyle.Left;
        root.Controls.Add(control, 1, row);
        root.SetColumnSpan(control, 2);
    }

    private void BrowseInput(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        using OpenFileDialog dialog = new OpenFileDialog { Filter = "Combined files (*.txt;*.cptf2)|*.txt;*.cptf2|All files (*.*)|*.*" };
        if (dialog.ShowDialog(this) == DialogResult.OK)
        {
            txtCombinedFile.Text = dialog.FileName;
            AutoFillOutputFolderFromCombinedFile();
        }
    }

    private void BrowseOutput(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        using FolderBrowserDialog dialog = new FolderBrowserDialog();
        if (dialog.ShowDialog(this) == DialogResult.OK)
        {
            txtOutputFolder.Text = dialog.SelectedPath;
        }
    }

    private void SelectRelativePath(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        if (!File.Exists(CombinedFilePath))
        {
            MessageBox.Show(this, "Select an existing Combined file first.", "Combined file required", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Information);
            return;
        }

        try
        {
            using Cptf2StructurePickerForm picker = new Cptf2StructurePickerForm(CombinedFilePath);
            if (picker.ShowDialog(this) == DialogResult.OK)
            {
                txtRelativePath.Text = picker.SelectedRelativePath;
            }
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            MessageBox.Show(this, ex.Message, "Unable to read combined file structure", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
        }
    }

    private void UpdateSelectRelativePathButtonState()
    {
        bool enabled = File.Exists(CombinedFilePath);
        btnSelectRelativePath.Enabled = enabled;
        toolTip.SetToolTip(btnSelectRelativePath, enabled
            ? "Open the combined file structure and select a file or folder to extract."
            : "Select a Combined file first.");
    }

    private void AutoFillOutputFolderFromCombinedFile()
    {
        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtOutputFolder.Text))
        {
            return;
        }
        if (!File.Exists(CombinedFilePath))
        {
            return;
        }
        string? directory = Path.GetDirectoryName(CombinedFilePath);
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(directory))
        {
            return;
        }
        string name = Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(CombinedFilePath);
        txtOutputFolder.Text = Path.Combine(directory, name + "_Extracted");
    }

    private void AcceptIfValid()
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(CombinedFilePath) || !File.Exists(CombinedFilePath))
        {
            MessageBox.Show(this, "Select an existing combined file.", "Missing input", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
            return;
        }
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(RelativePath))
        {
            MessageBox.Show(this, "Enter or select a file/folder path inside the combined file.", "Missing selected path", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
            return;
        }
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(OutputFolderPath))
        {
            MessageBox.Show(this, "Select an output folder.", "Missing output folder", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
            return;
        }
        DialogResult = DialogResult.OK;
        Close();
    }
}

using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed partial class MainForm
{
    private bool ConfirmGeneratedOutputWarning(string sourcePath, string outputFilePath)
    {
        if (!Directory.Exists(sourcePath))
        {
            return true;
        }
        string sourceRoot = Path.GetFullPath(sourcePath).TrimEnd(Path.DirectorySeparatorChar, Path.AltDirectorySeparatorChar) + Path.DirectorySeparatorChar;
        string outputPath = Path.GetFullPath(outputFilePath);
        if (!outputPath.StartsWith(sourceRoot, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            return true;
        }
        DialogResult result = MessageBox.Show(this,
            "The output file is inside the selected source folder." + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine +
            "The current output file will be excluded, but older generated combined output files in the same source tree may still be included." + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine +
            "Continue?",
            "Output file inside source folder",
            MessageBoxButtons.YesNo,
            MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
        return result == DialogResult.Yes;
    }

    private void BtnBrowseSource_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        InputSourceKind kind = GetSelectedInputSourceKind();
        if (kind == InputSourceKind.Auto)
        {
            autoBrowseMenu.Show(btnBrowseSource, new Point(0, btnBrowseSource.Height));
            return;
        }
        if (kind == InputSourceKind.Folder)
        {
            BrowseForFolder();
            return;
        }
        BrowseForZipArchive();
    }

    private void BtnBrowseOutputFile_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        using SaveFileDialog saveFileDialog = new SaveFileDialog
        {
            Title = "Select the output file",
            Filter = "Text files (*.txt)|*.txt|All files (*.*)|*.*",
            DefaultExt = "txt",
            AddExtension = true
        };
        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtOutputFile.Text))
        {
            saveFileDialog.FileName = txtOutputFile.Text;
        }
        if (saveFileDialog.ShowDialog(this) == DialogResult.OK)
        {
            txtOutputFile.Text = saveFileDialog.FileName;
            UpdateOutputButtons();
        }
    }

    private async void BtnCombine_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        string sourcePath = txtSourcePath.Text.Trim();
        string outputFilePath = txtOutputFile.Text.Trim();
        InputSourceKind kind = GetSelectedInputSourceKind();
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(sourcePath) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(outputFilePath))
        {
            MessageBox.Show(this, "Select a source path and output file.", "Input Validation", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
            return;
        }
        if (!ConfirmGeneratedOutputWarning(sourcePath, outputFilePath))
        {
            return;
        }
        SetCombineUiEnabled(false);
        UpdateStatus("Combining files...");
        try
        {
            CombineResult result = await Task.Run(() => ProjectFileCombiner.CombineProjectTextFiles(kind, sourcePath, outputFilePath, currentSettings));
            txtOutputFile.Text = result.OutputFilePath;
            RememberRecentSourcePath(sourcePath);
            RememberRecentOutputFile(result.OutputFilePath);
            UpdateOutputButtons();
            string combineStatus = BuildCombineDiagnosticsStatus(result);
            if (chkVerifyOutputAfterCombining.Checked)
            {
                UpdateStatus(combineStatus + " Verifying generated combined file...");
                string validationRoot = Path.GetDirectoryName(result.OutputFilePath) ?? Environment.CurrentDirectory;
                CombinedFileValidationResult validationResult = await Task.Run(() => CombinedProjectValidator.ValidateCombinedFile(result.OutputFilePath, BuildCombinedFileValidationOptions(validationRoot)));
                combineStatus += " " + BuildCompactValidationStatus(validationResult);
                if (!validationResult.IsValid)
                {
                    MessageBox.Show(this, BuildValidationFailureMessage(validationResult), "Verification Failed", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
                }
            }
            lblCombineResultSummary.Text = combineStatus;
            UpdateStatus(combineStatus);
            if (chkOpenOutputWhenFinished.Checked)
            {
                OpenOutputFile();
            }
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowHandledError("Combine", ex);
        }
        finally
        {
            SetCombineUiEnabled(true);
        }
    }

    private void BrowseForFolder()
    {
        using FolderBrowserDialog folderBrowserDialog = new FolderBrowserDialog { Description = "Select source folder" };
        if (Directory.Exists(txtSourcePath.Text))
        {
            folderBrowserDialog.SelectedPath = txtSourcePath.Text;
        }
        if (folderBrowserDialog.ShowDialog(this) == DialogResult.OK)
        {
            txtSourcePath.Text = folderBrowserDialog.SelectedPath;
            rdoFolder.Checked = true;
            TrySuggestOutputPath(overwriteExisting: true);
        }
    }

    private void BrowseForZipArchive()
    {
        using OpenFileDialog openFileDialog = new OpenFileDialog { Title = "Select ZIP archive", Filter = "ZIP archives (*.zip)|*.zip|All files (*.*)|*.*" };
        if (File.Exists(txtSourcePath.Text))
        {
            openFileDialog.FileName = txtSourcePath.Text;
        }
        if (openFileDialog.ShowDialog(this) == DialogResult.OK)
        {
            txtSourcePath.Text = openFileDialog.FileName;
            rdoZipArchive.Checked = true;
            TrySuggestOutputPath(overwriteExisting: true);
        }
    }

    private InputSourceKind GetSelectedInputSourceKind()
    {
        return rdoFolder.Checked ? InputSourceKind.Folder : rdoZipArchive.Checked ? InputSourceKind.ZipArchive : InputSourceKind.Auto;
    }

    private void UpdateSourceMode()
    {
        InputSourceKind kind = GetSelectedInputSourceKind();
        lblSourcePath.Text = kind == InputSourceKind.Folder ? "Source folder" : kind == InputSourceKind.ZipArchive ? "Source ZIP archive" : "Source path (folder or ZIP)";
        UpdateStatus(kind == InputSourceKind.Auto ? "Auto mode accepts a folder or a ZIP archive." : $"Selected source mode: {ProjectFileCombiner.GetSourceTypeText(kind)}.");
    }

    private void TrySuggestOutputPath(bool overwriteExisting = false)
    {
        if (!overwriteExisting && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtOutputFile.Text))
        {
            return;
        }
        string sourcePath = txtSourcePath.Text.Trim();
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(sourcePath))
        {
            return;
        }
        string baseDirectory = Directory.Exists(sourcePath) ? sourcePath : Path.GetDirectoryName(sourcePath) ?? Environment.CurrentDirectory;
        string sourceName = Directory.Exists(sourcePath) ? new DirectoryInfo(sourcePath).Name : Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(sourcePath);
        string safeSourceName = SanitizeOutputFileNamePart(sourceName);
        txtOutputFile.Text = Path.Combine(baseDirectory, $"CombinedProjectFiles_{safeSourceName}.txt");
    }

    private static string SanitizeOutputFileNamePart(string? value)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
        {
            return "Project";
        }
        char[] invalidCharacters = Path.GetInvalidFileNameChars();
        string safeValue = new string(value.Trim().Select(character => invalidCharacters.Contains(character) ? '_' : character).ToArray());
        safeValue = safeValue.Trim(' ', '.');
        return string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(safeValue) ? "Project" : safeValue;
    }

    private void SetCombineUiEnabled(bool enabled)
    {
        btnBrowseSource.Enabled = enabled;
        btnRecentSource.Enabled = enabled;
        btnBrowseOutputFile.Enabled = enabled;
        btnRecentOutputFile.Enabled = enabled;
        btnOpenOutputFile.Enabled = enabled && File.Exists(txtOutputFile.Text.Trim());
        btnOpenOutputFolder.Enabled = enabled;
        mnuSettingsDialog.Enabled = enabled;
        mnuAboutDialog.Enabled = enabled;
        mnuExit.Enabled = enabled;
        btnCombine.Enabled = enabled;
        chkOpenOutputWhenFinished.Enabled = enabled;
        chkVerifyOutputAfterCombining.Enabled = enabled;
        chkAlwaysOnTop.Enabled = enabled;
        rdoAuto.Enabled = enabled;
        rdoFolder.Enabled = enabled;
        rdoZipArchive.Enabled = enabled;
        UpdateOutputButtons();
    }

    private void OpenOutputFile()
    {
        if (File.Exists(txtOutputFile.Text.Trim()))
        {
            OpenFile(txtOutputFile.Text.Trim());
        }
    }

    private void OpenOutputFolder()
    {
        string? directory = Path.GetDirectoryName(txtOutputFile.Text.Trim());
        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(directory) && Directory.Exists(directory))
        {
            OpenFolder(directory);
        }
    }

    private void UpdateOutputButtons()
    {
        string output = txtOutputFile.Text.Trim();
        bool outputFileExists = File.Exists(output);
        btnOpenOutputFile.Enabled = outputFileExists;
        string? directory = Path.GetDirectoryName(output);
        btnOpenOutputFolder.Enabled = !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(directory) && Directory.Exists(directory);
        UpdateCombineReadySummary();
    }

    private void RdoSource_CheckedChanged(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        UpdateSourceMode();
        UpdateCombineReadySummary();
    }

    private void CombineInput_TextChanged(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        UpdateOutputButtons();
        UpdateCombineReadySummary();
    }

    private void UpdateCombineReadySummary()
    {
        if (lblCombineReadySummary.IsDisposed)
        {
            return;
        }
        string source = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtSourcePath.Text) ? "<not selected>" : txtSourcePath.Text.Trim();
        string output = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtOutputFile.Text) ? "<not selected>" : txtOutputFile.Text.Trim();
        lblCombineReadySummary.Text = "Ready to combine:" + Environment.NewLine +
            $"Source: {source}" + Environment.NewLine +
            $"Output: {output}" + Environment.NewLine +
            $"Verify after combine: {(chkVerifyOutputAfterCombining.Checked ? "Yes" : "No")}";
    }

    private void BtnRecentSource_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e) => recentSourceMenu.Show(btnRecentSource, new Point(0, btnRecentSource.Height));
    private void BtnRecentOutputFile_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e) => recentOutputFileMenu.Show(btnRecentOutputFile, new Point(0, btnRecentOutputFile.Height));

    private void BtnAutoBrowseSource_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        if (autoBrowseMenu.Items.Count > 0)
        {
            autoBrowseMenu.Show(btnAutoBrowseSource, new Point(0, btnAutoBrowseSource.Height));
        }
    }

    private void SelectFolderMenuItem_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        BrowseForFolder();
    }

    private void SelectZipMenuItem_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        BrowseForZipArchive();
    }

}

    private Control CreateExtractOptionsGroup()
    {
        TableLayoutPanel layout = new TableLayoutPanel
        {
            Dock = DockStyle.Top,
            AutoSize = true,
            ColumnCount = 1,
            Padding = new Padding(0),
            Margin = new Padding(0)
        };
        FlowLayoutPanel common = new FlowLayoutPanel { Dock = DockStyle.Top, AutoSize = true, WrapContents = true, Padding = new Padding(0), Margin = new Padding(0) };
        chkPreserveRootFolder.Text = "Preserve root folder from combined file";
        chkPreserveRootFolder.AutoSize = true;
        chkPreserveRootFolder.CheckedChanged += ExtractInput_TextChanged;
        chkOverwriteExistingFiles.Text = "Overwrite existing files";
        chkOverwriteExistingFiles.AutoSize = true;
        chkOverwriteExistingFiles.CheckedChanged += ExtractInput_TextChanged;
        chkEnableExtractValidation.Text = "Enable validation checks";
        chkEnableExtractValidation.AutoSize = true;
        chkEnableExtractValidation.CheckedChanged += ChkEnableExtractValidation_CheckedChanged;
        chkShowAdvancedValidationOptions.Text = "Show advanced validation options";
        chkShowAdvancedValidationOptions.AutoSize = true;
        chkShowAdvancedValidationOptions.CheckedChanged += ChkShowAdvancedValidationOptions_CheckedChanged;
        common.Controls.Add(chkPreserveRootFolder);
        common.Controls.Add(chkOverwriteExistingFiles);
        common.Controls.Add(chkEnableExtractValidation);
        common.Controls.Add(chkShowAdvancedValidationOptions);
        layout.Controls.Add(common, 0, 0);
        pnlAdvancedValidationOptions.Dock = DockStyle.Top;
        pnlAdvancedValidationOptions.AutoSize = true;
        pnlAdvancedValidationOptions.Margin = new Padding(0, 4, 0, 0);
        pnlAdvancedValidationOptions.Visible = chkShowAdvancedValidationOptions.Checked;
        pnlAdvancedValidationOptions.Controls.Add(CreateAdvancedValidationPanel());
        layout.Controls.Add(pnlAdvancedValidationOptions, 0, 1);
        return layout;
    }

    private Control CreateAdvancedValidationPanel()

        TableLayoutPanel layout = new TableLayoutPanel { Dock = DockStyle.Top, AutoSize = true, ColumnCount = 2, RowCount = 4, Padding = new Padding(0, 4, 0, 0), Margin = new Padding(0) };

        ConfigureValidationCheckBox(chkRejectTrailingSpacesOrDots, "Reject trailing spaces or dots");

        layout.Controls.Add(chkValidateBlockBoundaries, 1, 2);
        layout.Controls.Add(chkPreflightBeforeWriting, 0, 3);
        return layout;
    }

    private GroupBox CreateExtractValidationGroup()

        ConfigureValidationCheckBox(chkDetectDuplicatePaths, "Detect duplicate paths");
        ConfigureValidationCheckBox(chkValidatePathSafety, "Validate path safety");
        ConfigureValidationCheckBox(chkValidateWindowsFileNameChars, "Validate Windows filename characters");
        ConfigureValidationCheckBox(chkRejectEmptyPathSegments, "Reject empty path segments");
        ConfigureValidationCheckBox(chkRejectTrailingSpacesOrDots, "Reject trailing spaces or dots");
        ConfigureValidationCheckBox(chkValidateBlockBoundaries, "Validate declared line counts / block boundaries");
        ConfigureValidationCheckBox(chkPreflightBeforeWriting, "Preflight extraction before writing files");
        layout.Controls.Add(chkDetectDuplicatePaths, 0, 1);
        layout.Controls.Add(chkValidatePathSafety, 1, 1);
        layout.Controls.Add(chkValidateWindowsFileNameChars, 0, 2);

    private void BuildApplicationMenu()
    {
        mnuFile.DropDownItems.Clear();
        mnuTools.DropDownItems.Clear();
        mnuHelp.DropDownItems.Clear();
        mainMenu.Items.Clear();
        ConfigureMenuItem(mnuExit, BtnClose_Click);
        ConfigureMenuItem(mnuSettingsDialog, BtnSettings_Click);
        ConfigureMenuItem(mnuAboutDialog, BtnAbout_Click);
        mnuFile.DropDownItems.AddRange(new ToolStripItem[]
        {
            mnuRecentSources,
            mnuRecentCombinedFiles,
            mnuRecentOutputFiles,
            mnuRecentOutputFolders,
            new ToolStripSeparator(),
            mnuExit
        });
        mnuTools.DropDownItems.Add(mnuSettingsDialog);
        mnuHelp.DropDownItems.Add(mnuAboutDialog);
        mainMenu.Items.AddRange(new ToolStripItem[] { mnuFile, mnuTools, mnuHelp });
    }

    private static void ConfigureMenuItem(ToolStripMenuItem menuItem, EventHandler handler)
    {
        menuItem.Click -= handler;
        menuItem.Click += handler;
    }

    private static void ConfigureValidationCheckBox(CheckBox checkBox, string text)
    {
        checkBox.Text = text;
        checkBox.AutoSize = true;
        checkBox.Margin = new Padding(3, 4, 10, 4);
    }

    private static void ConfigureButton(Button button, string text, EventHandler handler)
    {
        button.Text = text;
        button.AutoSize = true;
        button.Click -= handler;
        button.Click += handler;
    }

    private static void ConfigurePrimaryButton(Button button, string text, EventHandler handler)
    {
        ConfigureButton(button, text, handler);
        button.Font = new Font(button.Font, FontStyle.Bold);
        button.MinimumSize = new Size(126, 32);
        button.BackColor = SystemColors.Highlight;
        button.ForeColor = SystemColors.HighlightText;
        button.UseVisualStyleBackColor = false;
    }

    private void ConfigureRadio(RadioButton radioButton, string text)
    {
        radioButton.Text = text;
        radioButton.AutoSize = true;
        radioButton.CheckedChanged += RdoSource_CheckedChanged;
    }

    private static void ConfigureStatusLabel(Label label, string text)
    {
        label.Text = text;
        label.BorderStyle = BorderStyle.FixedSingle;
        label.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        label.Padding = new Padding(6);
    }

    private static TableLayoutPanel CreateWorkflowLayout()
    {
        TableLayoutPanel layout = new TableLayoutPanel { ColumnCount = 1, Dock = DockStyle.Fill, Padding = new Padding(2), AutoScroll = true, AutoSize = true };
        layout.ColumnStyles.Add(new ColumnStyle(SizeType.Percent, 100F));
        for (int i = 0; i < 9; i++)
        {
            layout.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        }
        return layout;
    }

    private static TableLayoutPanel CreateTwoRowSectionContent()
    {
        TableLayoutPanel panel = new TableLayoutPanel { ColumnCount = 1, RowCount = 2, Dock = DockStyle.Top, AutoSize = true, Padding = new Padding(0), Margin = new Padding(0) };
        panel.ColumnStyles.Add(new ColumnStyle(SizeType.Percent, 100F));
        panel.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        panel.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        return panel;
    }

    private bool IsDarkUi()
    {
        return BackColor.GetBrightness() < 0.45F;
    }

    private Color GetWorkflowSectionBackColor()
    {
        return IsDarkUi()
            ? Color.FromArgb(31, 31, 31)
            : Color.FromArgb(248, 248, 248);
    }

    private Color GetWorkflowSectionBorderColor()
    {
        return IsDarkUi()
            ? Color.FromArgb(42, 42, 42)
            : Color.FromArgb(218, 218, 218);
    }

    private Color GetWorkflowSubtleBackColor()
    {
        return IsDarkUi()
            ? Color.FromArgb(36, 36, 36)
            : Color.FromArgb(245, 245, 245);
    }

    private Color GetWorkflowSubtleBorderColor()
    {
        return IsDarkUi()
            ? Color.FromArgb(48, 48, 48)
            : Color.FromArgb(210, 210, 210);
    }

    private void PaintSubtleBorder(object? sender, PaintEventArgs e)
    {
        if (sender is not Control control)
        {
            return;
        }
        using Pen borderPen = new Pen(GetWorkflowSectionBorderColor());
        Rectangle rectangle = new Rectangle(0, 0, control.Width - 1, control.Height - 1);
        e.Graphics.DrawRectangle(borderPen, rectangle);
    }

    private void PaintVerySubtleBorder(object? sender, PaintEventArgs e)
    {
        if (sender is not Control control)
        {
            return;
        }
        using Pen borderPen = new Pen(GetWorkflowSubtleBorderColor());
        Rectangle rectangle = new Rectangle(0, 0, control.Width - 1, control.Height - 1);
        e.Graphics.DrawRectangle(borderPen, rectangle);
    }

    private Control CreateWorkflowSection(string title, string description, Control content)
    {
        TableLayoutPanel section = new TableLayoutPanel { ColumnCount = 1, Dock = DockStyle.Top, AutoSize = true, Padding = new Padding(7, 4, 7, 4), Margin = new Padding(0, 1, 0, 3), BackColor = GetWorkflowSectionBackColor() };
        section.ColumnStyles.Add(new ColumnStyle(SizeType.Percent, 100F));
        section.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        section.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        section.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        section.Paint -= PaintSubtleBorder;
        section.Paint += PaintSubtleBorder;
        Label titleLabel = new Label { Text = title, AutoSize = true, Dock = DockStyle.Top, Font = new Font(Font, FontStyle.Bold), Margin = new Padding(0) };
        Label descriptionLabel = new Label { Text = description, AutoSize = true, Dock = DockStyle.Top, Margin = new Padding(0, 0, 0, 3) };
        content.Dock = DockStyle.Top;
        content.Margin = new Padding(0);
        section.Controls.Add(titleLabel, 0, 0);
        section.Controls.Add(descriptionLabel, 0, 1);
        section.Controls.Add(content, 0, 2);
        return section;
    }

    private Control CreateCollapsibleDetailsSection(string title, string toggleText, CheckBox toggle, Panel detailsPanel, Control detailsContent)
    {
        TableLayoutPanel section = new TableLayoutPanel { ColumnCount = 1, Dock = DockStyle.Top, AutoSize = true, Padding = new Padding(7, 4, 7, 4), Margin = new Padding(0, 1, 0, 3), BackColor = GetWorkflowSectionBackColor() };
        section.ColumnStyles.Add(new ColumnStyle(SizeType.Percent, 100F));
        section.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        section.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        section.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        section.Paint -= PaintSubtleBorder;
        section.Paint += PaintSubtleBorder;
        Label titleLabel = new Label { Text = title, AutoSize = true, Dock = DockStyle.Top, Font = new Font(Font, FontStyle.Bold), Margin = new Padding(0) };
        toggle.Text = toggleText;
        toggle.AutoSize = true;
        toggle.Dock = DockStyle.Top;
        toggle.Margin = new Padding(0, 0, 0, 2);
        detailsPanel.Dock = DockStyle.Top;
        detailsPanel.AutoSize = true;
        detailsPanel.Margin = new Padding(0);
        detailsPanel.Padding = new Padding(0);
        detailsPanel.Visible = toggle.Checked;
        detailsPanel.Controls.Clear();
        detailsContent.Dock = DockStyle.Top;
        detailsContent.Margin = new Padding(0);
        detailsPanel.Controls.Add(detailsContent);
        toggle.CheckedChanged += (sender, args) => detailsPanel.Visible = toggle.Checked;
        section.Controls.Add(titleLabel, 0, 0);
        section.Controls.Add(toggle, 0, 1);
        section.Controls.Add(detailsPanel, 0, 2);
        return section;
    }

    private Panel CreateSummaryLabelPanel(Label label, string text)
    {
        Panel panel = new Panel { Dock = DockStyle.Top, AutoSize = true, Padding = new Padding(7), Margin = new Padding(0), BorderStyle = BorderStyle.None, BackColor = GetWorkflowSubtleBackColor() };
        panel.Paint -= PaintVerySubtleBorder;
        panel.Paint += PaintVerySubtleBorder;
        label.Text = text;
        label.AutoSize = true;
        label.Dock = DockStyle.Top;
        label.Padding = new Padding(0);
        label.Margin = new Padding(0);
        label.BorderStyle = BorderStyle.None;
        panel.Resize += (sender, args) => label.MaximumSize = new Size(Math.Max(80, panel.ClientSize.Width - panel.Padding.Horizontal), 0);
        panel.Controls.Add(label);
        return panel;
    }

    private Panel CreateDropHintPanel(Panel panel, string text)
    {
        panel.Dock = DockStyle.Top;
        panel.Height = 24;
        panel.Padding = new Padding(8, 3, 8, 3);
        panel.Margin = new Padding(0, 1, 0, 3);
        panel.BorderStyle = BorderStyle.None;
        panel.BackColor = GetWorkflowSubtleBackColor();
        panel.Paint -= PaintVerySubtleBorder;
        panel.Paint += PaintVerySubtleBorder;
        panel.Controls.Clear();
        Label label = new Label { Text = text, Dock = DockStyle.Fill, TextAlign = ContentAlignment.MiddleCenter, AutoSize = false };
        panel.Controls.Add(label);
        return panel;
    }

    private static Label CreateTitleLabel(string text)
    {
        return new Label { Text = text, AutoSize = true, Font = new Font("Segoe UI", 12F, FontStyle.Bold, GraphicsUnit.Point), Margin = new Padding(0, 0, 0, 6) };
    }

    private static Panel CreatePathRow(Label label, TextBox textBox, Button browseButton, EventHandler browseHandler)
    {
        return CreatePathRow(label, textBox, browseButton, null, browseHandler, null);
    }

    private static Panel CreatePathRow(Label label, TextBox textBox, Button browseButton, Button? recentButton, EventHandler browseHandler, EventHandler? recentHandler)
    {
        Panel panel = new Panel { Dock = DockStyle.Top, Height = 36, Margin = new Padding(0) };
        label.AutoSize = true;
        label.Location = new Point(0, 0);
        textBox.Anchor = AnchorStyles.Left | AnchorStyles.Right | AnchorStyles.Top;
        textBox.Location = new Point(0, 17);
        browseButton.Text = "Browse...";
        browseButton.Anchor = AnchorStyles.Top | AnchorStyles.Right;
        browseButton.Width = 88;
        browseButton.Click -= browseHandler;
        browseButton.Click += browseHandler;
        if (recentButton is not null)
        {
            recentButton.Text = "Recent";
            recentButton.Anchor = AnchorStyles.Top | AnchorStyles.Right;
            recentButton.Width = 76;
            if (recentHandler is not null)
            {
                recentButton.Click -= recentHandler;
                recentButton.Click += recentHandler;
            }
            panel.Controls.Add(recentButton);
        }
        panel.Resize += (sender, args) =>
        {
            int buttonY = 15;
            browseButton.Location = new Point(Math.Max(0, panel.Width - 88), buttonY);
            int reservedWidth = 96;
            if (recentButton is not null)
            {
                recentButton.Location = new Point(Math.Max(0, panel.Width - 170), buttonY);
                reservedWidth = 178;
            }
            textBox.Width = Math.Max(60, panel.Width - reservedWidth);
        };
        panel.Controls.Add(label);
        panel.Controls.Add(textBox);
        panel.Controls.Add(browseButton);
        return panel;
    }

    private TableLayoutPanel CreateSummaryGrid()
    {
        TableLayoutPanel details = new TableLayoutPanel { ColumnCount = 1, RowCount = 3, Dock = DockStyle.Top, AutoSize = true, Padding = new Padding(0), Margin = new Padding(0) };
        details.ColumnStyles.Add(new ColumnStyle(SizeType.Percent, 100F));
        details.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        details.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        details.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        details.Controls.Add(CreateChipGroup("Supported extensions", SplitSummaryValues(ProjectFileCombiner.GetSupportedFileSummary())), 0, 0);
        details.Controls.Add(CreateChipGroup("Special files", SplitSummaryValues(ProjectFileCombiner.GetSpecialFileSummary())), 0, 1);
        details.Controls.Add(CreateChipGroup("Excluded folders", SplitSummaryValues(ProjectFileCombiner.GetExcludedFolderSummary())), 0, 2);
        return details;
    }

    private Control CreateChipGroup(string title, IEnumerable<string> values)
    {
        TableLayoutPanel group = new TableLayoutPanel { ColumnCount = 1, RowCount = 2, Dock = DockStyle.Top, AutoSize = true, Padding = new Padding(0), Margin = new Padding(0, 0, 0, 6) };
        group.ColumnStyles.Add(new ColumnStyle(SizeType.Percent, 100F));
        group.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        group.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        Label titleLabel = new Label { Text = title, AutoSize = true, Dock = DockStyle.Top, Font = new Font(Font, FontStyle.Bold), Margin = new Padding(0, 0, 0, 3) };
        FlowLayoutPanel chips = new FlowLayoutPanel { Dock = DockStyle.Top, AutoSize = true, WrapContents = true, FlowDirection = FlowDirection.LeftToRight, Padding = new Padding(0), Margin = new Padding(0) };
        foreach (string value in values)
        {
            chips.Controls.Add(CreateInfoChip(value));
        }
        if (chips.Controls.Count == 0)
        {
            chips.Controls.Add(CreateInfoChip("None"));
        }
        group.Controls.Add(titleLabel, 0, 0);
        group.Controls.Add(chips, 0, 1);
        return group;
    }

    private Label CreateInfoChip(string text)
    {
        Label chip = new Label { Text = text, AutoSize = true, Padding = new Padding(6, 2, 6, 2), Margin = new Padding(0, 0, 5, 4), BackColor = GetWorkflowSubtleBackColor(), BorderStyle = BorderStyle.FixedSingle };
        return chip;
    }

    private static IEnumerable<string> SplitSummaryValues(string? summary)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(summary))
        {
            return Enumerable.Empty<string>();
        }

        return summary
            .Split(new[] { ',', ';', '\r', '\n' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries | StringSplitOptions.TrimEntries)
            .Where(value => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value));
    }

    private static FlowLayoutPanel CreateRightAlignedButtonLayout()
    {
        return new FlowLayoutPanel
        {
            Dock = DockStyle.Top,
            FlowDirection = FlowDirection.RightToLeft,
            WrapContents = true,
            AutoSize = true,
            Padding = new Padding(0, 2, 0, 0),
            Margin = new Padding(0)
        };
    }
}

using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed partial class MainForm
{
    private void RegisterDragDropRecursive(Control control)
    {
        control.AllowDrop = true;
        control.DragEnter += HandleDragEnter;
        control.DragDrop += HandleDragDrop;
        foreach (Control childControl in control.Controls)
        {
            RegisterDragDropRecursive(childControl);
        }
    }

    private void HandleDragEnter(object? sender, DragEventArgs e)
    {
        string? path = GetSingleDroppedPath(e);
        e.Effect = IsSupportedDropTarget(path) ? DragDropEffects.Copy : DragDropEffects.None;
    }

    private void HandleDragDrop(object? sender, DragEventArgs e)
    {
        string? path = GetSingleDroppedPath(e);
        if (!IsSupportedDropTarget(path))
        {
            UpdateStatusForActiveTab("Unsupported drop target.");
            return;
        }
        if (tabControl.SelectedTab == tabExtract)
        {
            if (Directory.Exists(path!))
            {
                txtExtractOutputFolder.Text = path!;
                RememberRecentOutputFolder(path!);
            }
            else
            {
                txtCombinedTextFile.Text = path!;
                RememberRecentCombinedFile(path!);
                SuggestExtractOutputFolder(path!, overwriteExisting: true);
            }
            lblExtractStatus.Text = "Selected item by drag && drop.";
            return;
        }
        txtSourcePath.Text = path!;
        RememberRecentSourcePath(path!);
        rdoAuto.Checked = true;
        TrySuggestOutputPath(overwriteExisting: true);
        UpdateStatus(Directory.Exists(path) ? "Selected folder by drag && drop." : "Selected ZIP archive by drag && drop.");
    }

    private static string? GetSingleDroppedPath(DragEventArgs e)
    {
        if (!e.Data?.GetDataPresent(DataFormats.FileDrop) ?? true)
        {
            return null;
        }
        string[]? files = e.Data?.GetData(DataFormats.FileDrop) as string[];
        return files is { Length: 1 } ? files[0] : null;
    }

    private bool IsSupportedDropTarget(string? path)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(path))
        {
            return false;
        }
        if (tabControl.SelectedTab == tabExtract)
        {
            return Directory.Exists(path) || (File.Exists(path) && string.Equals(Path.GetExtension(path), ".txt", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
        }
        return Directory.Exists(path) || (File.Exists(path) && string.Equals(Path.GetExtension(path), ".zip", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
    }

    protected override void OnFormClosed(FormClosedEventArgs e)
    {
        autoBrowseMenu.Dispose();
        extractValidationToolTip.Dispose();
        base.OnFormClosed(e);
    }
}

END FILE
