using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed partial class MainForm
{
    private void ChkEnableExtractValidation_CheckedChanged(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        UpdateExtractValidationUiState();
        UpdateExtractReadySummary();
    }

    private void ChkShowAdvancedValidationOptions_CheckedChanged(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        pnlAdvancedValidationOptions.Visible = chkShowAdvancedValidationOptions.Checked;
    }

    private void UpdateExtractValidationUiState()
    {
        bool enabled = chkEnableExtractValidation.Checked;
        chkDetectDuplicatePaths.Enabled = enabled;
        chkValidatePathSafety.Enabled = enabled;
        chkValidateWindowsFileNameChars.Enabled = enabled;
        chkRejectEmptyPathSegments.Enabled = enabled;
        chkRejectTrailingSpacesOrDots.Enabled = enabled;
        chkValidateBlockBoundaries.Enabled = enabled;
        chkPreflightBeforeWriting.Enabled = enabled;
        chkShowAdvancedValidationOptions.Enabled = enabled;
        if (!enabled)
        {
            lblExtractStatus.Text = "Validation checks are disabled. Output-folder containment is still enforced.";
        }
    }

    private void ApplyExtractValidationToolTips()
    {
        extractValidationToolTip.SetToolTip(chkEnableExtractValidation, "Master switch for optional extract validation checks. When disabled, extraction is more permissive, but output-folder containment is still enforced.");
        extractValidationToolTip.SetToolTip(chkDetectDuplicatePaths, "Detects duplicate RltvPath entries and duplicate final target paths after path normalization.");
        extractValidationToolTip.SetToolTip(chkValidatePathSafety, "Rejects absolute paths, '.' and '..' path navigation, and any path that would escape the selected restore folder.");
        extractValidationToolTip.SetToolTip(chkValidateWindowsFileNameChars, "Rejects characters invalid in Windows filenames, such as < > : \" | ? *. Reserved device names are intentionally not checked.");
        extractValidationToolTip.SetToolTip(chkRejectEmptyPathSegments, "Rejects malformed paths with empty or whitespace-only segments, such as Project\\File.cs.");
        extractValidationToolTip.SetToolTip(chkRejectTrailingSpacesOrDots, "Rejects path segments ending with a space or dot because Windows can normalize or handle those paths unexpectedly.");
        extractValidationToolTip.SetToolTip(chkValidateBlockBoundaries, "Checks that the next combined-file block boundary looks valid after the declared [Lines: N] content is read.");
        extractValidationToolTip.SetToolTip(chkPreflightBeforeWriting, "Builds and validates the full write plan before files are written, so validation failures can stop extraction before output is created.");
        extractValidationToolTip.SetToolTip(btnValidateOnly, "Parses the selected combined file, validates protocol structure, byte lengths, SHA-256 hashes, duplicate paths, and path safety without writing files.");
    }

    private void BtnBrowseCombinedTextFile_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        using OpenFileDialog openFileDialog = new OpenFileDialog { Title = "Select combined text file", Filter = "Text files (*.txt)|*.txt|All files (*.*)|*.*" };
        if (File.Exists(txtCombinedTextFile.Text))
        {
            openFileDialog.FileName = txtCombinedTextFile.Text;
        }
        if (openFileDialog.ShowDialog(this) == DialogResult.OK)
        {
            txtCombinedTextFile.Text = openFileDialog.FileName;
            SuggestExtractOutputFolder(openFileDialog.FileName, overwriteExisting: true);
        }
    }

    private void BtnBrowseExtractOutputFolder_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        using FolderBrowserDialog folderBrowserDialog = new FolderBrowserDialog { Description = "Select output folder for restored project" };
        if (Directory.Exists(txtExtractOutputFolder.Text))
        {
            folderBrowserDialog.SelectedPath = txtExtractOutputFolder.Text;
        }
        if (folderBrowserDialog.ShowDialog(this) == DialogResult.OK)
        {
            txtExtractOutputFolder.Text = folderBrowserDialog.SelectedPath;
        }
    }

    private void BtnOpenCombinedTextFile_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        if (File.Exists(txtCombinedTextFile.Text.Trim()))
        {
            OpenFile(txtCombinedTextFile.Text.Trim());
        }
    }

    private void BtnOpenExtractOutputFolder_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        if (Directory.Exists(txtExtractOutputFolder.Text.Trim()))
        {
            OpenFolder(txtExtractOutputFolder.Text.Trim());
        }
    }

    private void BtnCopyExtractLog_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtExtractLog.Text))
        {
            try
            {
                Clipboard.SetText(txtExtractLog.Text);
                lblExtractStatus.Text = "Extract log copied to clipboard.";
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                ShowHandledError("Copy extract log", ex);
            }
        }
    }

    private async void RunExtractAsync(bool validateOnly)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtCombinedTextFile.Text) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtExtractOutputFolder.Text))
        {
            MessageBox.Show(this, "Select a combined text file and restore folder.", "Input Validation", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
            return;
        }
        txtExtractLog.Clear();
        AppendExtractLogText(validateOnly ? "[INFO ] Validating combined text file..." : "[INFO ] Extracting project files...");
        SetExtractUiEnabled(false);
        try
        {
            Progress<ExtractMilestone> milestones = new Progress<ExtractMilestone>(AppendExtractMilestone);
            if (validateOnly)
            {
                CombinedFileValidationResult validationResult = await Task.Run(() => CombinedProjectValidator.ValidateCombinedFile(txtCombinedTextFile.Text.Trim(), BuildCombinedFileValidationOptions(txtExtractOutputFolder.Text.Trim()), milestones));
                RememberRecentCombinedFile(txtCombinedTextFile.Text.Trim());
                RememberRecentOutputFolder(txtExtractOutputFolder.Text.Trim());
                string validationStatus = BuildCompactValidationStatus(validationResult);
                lblExtractStatus.Text = validationStatus;
                lblExtractResultSummary.Text = validationStatus;
                AppendExtractLogText(validationStatus);
                AppendValidationIssuesToExtractLog(validationResult);
                MessageBox.Show(this,
                    validationResult.IsValid ? validationStatus : BuildValidationFailureMessage(validationResult),
                    validationResult.IsValid ? "Validation Complete" : "Validation Failed",
                    MessageBoxButtons.OK,
                    validationResult.IsValid ? MessageBoxIcon.Information : MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
                return;
            }

            RestoreOptions options = BuildRestoreOptionsFromUi();
            options.ValidateOnly = false;
            RestoreResult result = await Task.Run(() => ProjectFileExtractor.ExtractProjectFiles(txtCombinedTextFile.Text.Trim(), txtExtractOutputFolder.Text.Trim(), options, milestones));
            RememberRecentCombinedFile(txtCombinedTextFile.Text.Trim());
            RememberRecentOutputFolder(txtExtractOutputFolder.Text.Trim());
            string extractStatus = BuildExtractDiagnosticsStatus(result, false);
            lblExtractStatus.Text = extractStatus;
            lblExtractResultSummary.Text = extractStatus;
            AppendExtractLogText(extractStatus);
            MessageBox.Show(this,
                BuildExtractDiagnosticsMessage(result, false),
                "Extract Complete",
                MessageBoxButtons.OK,
                MessageBoxIcon.Information);
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowHandledError(validateOnly ? "Validate Combined File" : "Extract", ex);
            AppendExtractLogText("[ERROR] " + ex.Message);
        }
        finally
        {
            SetExtractUiEnabled(true);
        }
    }

    private RestoreOptions BuildRestoreOptionsFromUi()
    {
        return new RestoreOptions
        {
            PreserveRootFolder = chkPreserveRootFolder.Checked,
            OverwriteExistingFiles = chkOverwriteExistingFiles.Checked,
            EnableValidationChecks = chkEnableExtractValidation.Checked,
            DetectDuplicatePaths = chkDetectDuplicatePaths.Checked,
            ValidatePathSafety = chkValidatePathSafety.Checked,
            ValidateWindowsFileNameChars = chkValidateWindowsFileNameChars.Checked,
            RejectEmptyPathSegments = chkRejectEmptyPathSegments.Checked,
            RejectTrailingSpacesOrDots = chkRejectTrailingSpacesOrDots.Checked,
            ValidateBlockBoundaries = chkValidateBlockBoundaries.Checked,
            PreflightBeforeWriting = chkPreflightBeforeWriting.Checked,
            NewLineMode = RestoreNewLineMode.WindowsCrLf
        };
    }

    private static string BuildValidationFailureMessage(ExtractValidationException ex)
    {
        string message = "Validation failed." + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine +
            "Check:" + Environment.NewLine + ex.CheckName + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine;
        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(ex.RelativePath))
        {
            message += "Path:" + Environment.NewLine + ex.RelativePath + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine;
        }
        return message + "Details:" + Environment.NewLine + ex.Message;
    }

    private void AppendExtractMilestone(ExtractMilestone milestone)
    {
        string prefix = milestone.Status switch
        {
            ExtractMilestoneStatus.Started => "[START]",
            ExtractMilestoneStatus.Completed => "[ OK  ]",
            ExtractMilestoneStatus.Warning => "[WARN ]",
            ExtractMilestoneStatus.Failed => "[FAIL ]",
            ExtractMilestoneStatus.Done => "[DONE ]",
            _ => "[INFO ]"
        };
        AppendExtractLogText(prefix + " " + milestone.Message);
        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(milestone.Detail))
        {
            AppendExtractLogText("       " + milestone.Detail);
        }
        AppendExtractLogText(string.Empty);
    }

    private void SuggestExtractOutputFolder(string combinedTextFilePath, bool overwriteExisting = false)
    {
        if (!overwriteExisting && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtExtractOutputFolder.Text))
        {
            return;
        }
        string baseDirectory = Path.GetDirectoryName(combinedTextFilePath) ?? Environment.CurrentDirectory;
        txtExtractOutputFolder.Text = Path.Combine(baseDirectory, Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(combinedTextFilePath) + "_Restored");
    }

    private void UpdateExtractButtons()
    {
        string combined = txtCombinedTextFile.Text.Trim();
        string output = txtExtractOutputFolder.Text.Trim();
        btnOpenCombinedTextFile.Enabled = File.Exists(combined);
        btnOpenExtractOutputFolder.Enabled = Directory.Exists(output);
        btnValidateOnly.Enabled = !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(combined) && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(output);
        btnExtractProject.Enabled = btnValidateOnly.Enabled;
        UpdateExtractReadySummary();
    }

    private void SetExtractUiEnabled(bool enabled)
    {
        btnBrowseCombinedTextFile.Enabled = enabled;
        btnRecentCombinedTextFile.Enabled = enabled;
        btnBrowseExtractOutputFolder.Enabled = enabled;
        btnRecentExtractOutputFolder.Enabled = enabled;
        btnOpenCombinedTextFile.Enabled = enabled && File.Exists(txtCombinedTextFile.Text.Trim());
        btnOpenExtractOutputFolder.Enabled = enabled && Directory.Exists(txtExtractOutputFolder.Text.Trim());
        btnCopyExtractLog.Enabled = enabled;
        btnValidateOnly.Enabled = enabled;
        btnExtractProject.Enabled = enabled;
        mnuSettingsDialog.Enabled = enabled;
        mnuAboutDialog.Enabled = enabled;
        mnuExit.Enabled = enabled;
        chkPreserveRootFolder.Enabled = enabled;
        chkOverwriteExistingFiles.Enabled = enabled;
        chkEnableExtractValidation.Enabled = enabled;
        UpdateExtractValidationUiState();
        UpdateExtractButtons();
    }

    private void ExtractInput_TextChanged(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        UpdateExtractButtons();
        UpdateExtractReadySummary();
    }

    private void UpdateExtractReadySummary()
    {
        if (lblExtractReadySummary.IsDisposed)
        {
            return;
        }
        string input = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtCombinedTextFile.Text) ? "<not selected>" : txtCombinedTextFile.Text.Trim();
        string destination = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(txtExtractOutputFolder.Text) ? "<not selected>" : txtExtractOutputFolder.Text.Trim();
        lblExtractReadySummary.Text = "Ready to extract:" + Environment.NewLine +
            $"Input: {input}" + Environment.NewLine +
            $"Destination: {destination}" + Environment.NewLine +
            $"Validation checks: {(chkEnableExtractValidation.Checked ? "Enabled" : "Disabled")}" + Environment.NewLine +
            $"Overwrite existing files: {(chkOverwriteExistingFiles.Checked ? "Yes" : "No")}";
    }

    private void BtnRecentCombinedTextFile_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e) => recentCombinedFileMenu.Show(btnRecentCombinedTextFile, new Point(0, btnRecentCombinedTextFile.Height));
    private void BtnRecentExtractOutputFolder_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e) => recentOutputFolderMenu.Show(btnRecentExtractOutputFolder, new Point(0, btnRecentExtractOutputFolder.Height));

    private void BtnValidateOnly_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        RunExtractAsync(validateOnly: true);
    }

    private void BtnExtractProject_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        RunExtractAsync(validateOnly: false);
    }

}

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed partial class MainForm
{
    private bool cliCommandsHelpMenuInitialized;

    protected override void OnHandleCreated(EventArgs e)
    {
        base.OnHandleCreated(e);
        InitializeCliCommandsHelpMenu();
    }

    private void InitializeCliCommandsHelpMenu()
    {
        if (cliCommandsHelpMenuInitialized)
        {
            return;
        }
        cliCommandsHelpMenuInitialized = true;

        MenuStrip? menuStrip = Controls.OfType<MenuStrip>().FirstOrDefault();
        if (menuStrip is null)
        {
            return;
        }

        ToolStripMenuItem? helpMenu = menuStrip.Items
            .OfType<ToolStripMenuItem>()
            .FirstOrDefault(item => string.Equals(item.Text?.Replace("&", string.Empty), "Help", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
        if (helpMenu is null)
        {
            helpMenu = new ToolStripMenuItem("Help");
            menuStrip.Items.Add(helpMenu);
        }

        if (!helpMenu.DropDownItems.OfType<ToolStripMenuItem>().Any(item => string.Equals(item.Text, "CLI commands", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)))
        {
            ToolStripMenuItem cliCommands = new ToolStripMenuItem("CLI commands");
            cliCommands.Click += (_, _) =>
            {
                using CliCommandsForm dialog = new CliCommandsForm();
                dialog.ShowDialog(this);
            };
            InsertBeforeAbout(helpMenu, cliCommands);
        }

        if (!helpMenu.DropDownItems.OfType<ToolStripMenuItem>().Any(item => string.Equals(item.Text, "Open docs folder", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)))
        {
            ToolStripMenuItem openDocsFolder = new ToolStripMenuItem("Open docs folder");
            openDocsFolder.Click += (_, _) => OpenDocsFolder();
            InsertBeforeAbout(helpMenu, openDocsFolder);
        }
    }

    private static void InsertBeforeAbout(ToolStripMenuItem helpMenu, ToolStripMenuItem menuItem)
    {
        int aboutIndex = -1;
        for (int index = 0; index < helpMenu.DropDownItems.Count; index++)
        {
            if (helpMenu.DropDownItems[index] is ToolStripMenuItem item
                && item.Text is not null
                && item.Text.Replace("&", string.Empty).StartsWith("About", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                aboutIndex = index;
                break;
            }
        }

        if (aboutIndex >= 0)
        {
            helpMenu.DropDownItems.Insert(aboutIndex, menuItem);
        }
        else
        {
            helpMenu.DropDownItems.Add(menuItem);
        }
    }

    private void OpenDocsFolder()
    {
        string docsFolder = Path.Combine(AppContext.BaseDirectory, "docs");
        try
        {
            if (!Directory.Exists(docsFolder))
            {
                Directory.CreateDirectory(docsFolder);
            }

            System.Diagnostics.Process.Start(new System.Diagnostics.ProcessStartInfo
            {
                FileName = docsFolder,
                UseShellExecute = true
            });
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            MessageBox.Show(this, ex.Message, "Unable to open docs folder", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
        }
    }
}

using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed partial class MainForm
{
    private ToolStripMenuItem? mnuCptf2IndexedExtractOne;
    private bool cptf2IndexedExtractionUiInitialized;

    protected override void OnShown(EventArgs e)
    {
        base.OnShown(e);
        InitializeCptf2IndexedExtractionUi();
    }

    private void InitializeCptf2IndexedExtractionUi()
    {
        if (cptf2IndexedExtractionUiInitialized)
        {
            return;
        }
        cptf2IndexedExtractionUiInitialized = true;
        MenuStrip? menuStrip = Controls.OfType<MenuStrip>().FirstOrDefault();
        if (menuStrip is null)
        {
            return;
        }
        ToolStripMenuItem cptf2Menu = new ToolStripMenuItem("CPTF/2");
        mnuCptf2IndexedExtractOne = new ToolStripMenuItem("Indexed extract selected path...");
        mnuCptf2IndexedExtractOne.Click += (_, _) => ShowCptf2IndexedExtractOneDialog();
        cptf2Menu.DropDownItems.Add(mnuCptf2IndexedExtractOne);
        menuStrip.Items.Add(cptf2Menu);
    }

    private void ShowCptf2IndexedExtractOneDialog()
    {
        using IndexedExtractOneForm dialog = new IndexedExtractOneForm();
        if (dialog.ShowDialog(this) != DialogResult.OK)
        {
            return;
        }
        RestoreOptions options = new RestoreOptions
        {
            PreserveRootFolder = true,
            OverwriteExistingFiles = dialog.OverwriteExistingFile,
            ValidateOnly = dialog.ValidateOnly,
            IndexMode = dialog.IndexMode
        };
        try
        {
            RestoreResult result = Cptf2IndexedExtractor.ExtractOne(dialog.CombinedFilePath, dialog.RelativePath, dialog.OutputFolderPath, options);
            string action = dialog.ValidateOnly ? "Validation" : "Extraction";
            MessageBox.Show(
                this,
                $"{action} completed for selected path '{dialog.RelativePath}'. Planned {result.FilesPlanned:N0}, created {result.FilesCreated:N0}, skipped {result.FilesSkipped:N0}.",
                "CPTF/2 selected path extraction",
                MessageBoxButtons.OK,
                MessageBoxIcon.Information);
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            MessageBox.Show(this, ex.Message, "CPTF/2 selected path extraction failed", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
        }
    }
}

using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed partial class MainForm
{
    private void RememberRecentSourcePath(string path) => RememberRecentPath(currentSettings.RecentSourcePaths, path);
    private void RememberRecentCombinedFile(string path) => RememberRecentPath(currentSettings.RecentCombinedFiles, path);
    private void RememberRecentOutputFolder(string path) => RememberRecentPath(currentSettings.RecentOutputFolders, path);
    private void RememberRecentOutputFile(string path) => RememberRecentPath(currentSettings.RecentOutputFiles, path);

    private void RememberRecentPath(List<string> list, string path)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(path))
        {
            return;
        }
        string fullPath = path.Trim();
        list.RemoveAll(value => string.Equals(value, fullPath, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
        list.Insert(0, fullPath);
        while (list.Count > 10)
        {
            list.RemoveAt(list.Count - 1);
        }
        SettingsService.SaveWithResult(currentSettings);
        UpdateRecentMenus();
    }

    private void UpdateRecentMenus()
    {
        PopulateRecentMenu(recentSourceMenu, currentSettings.RecentSourcePaths, path =>
        {
            txtSourcePath.Text = path;
            TrySuggestOutputPath(overwriteExisting: true);
        });
        PopulateRecentMenu(recentOutputFileMenu, currentSettings.RecentOutputFiles, path => txtOutputFile.Text = path);
        PopulateRecentMenu(recentCombinedFileMenu, currentSettings.RecentCombinedFiles, path =>
        {
            txtCombinedTextFile.Text = path;
            SuggestExtractOutputFolder(path, overwriteExisting: true);
        });
        PopulateRecentMenu(recentOutputFolderMenu, currentSettings.RecentOutputFolders, path => txtExtractOutputFolder.Text = path);

        PopulateRecentToolStripMenu(mnuRecentSources, currentSettings.RecentSourcePaths, path =>
        {
            tabControl.SelectedTab = tabCombine;
            txtSourcePath.Text = path;
            TrySuggestOutputPath(overwriteExisting: true);
        });
        PopulateRecentToolStripMenu(mnuRecentCombinedFiles, currentSettings.RecentCombinedFiles, path =>
        {
            tabControl.SelectedTab = tabExtract;
            txtCombinedTextFile.Text = path;
            SuggestExtractOutputFolder(path, overwriteExisting: true);
        });
        PopulateRecentToolStripMenu(mnuRecentOutputFiles, currentSettings.RecentOutputFiles, path =>
        {
            tabControl.SelectedTab = tabCombine;
            txtOutputFile.Text = path;
        });
        PopulateRecentToolStripMenu(mnuRecentOutputFolders, currentSettings.RecentOutputFolders, path =>
        {
            tabControl.SelectedTab = tabExtract;
            txtExtractOutputFolder.Text = path;
        });

        btnRecentSource.Enabled = currentSettings.RecentSourcePaths.Count > 0;
        btnRecentOutputFile.Enabled = currentSettings.RecentOutputFiles.Count > 0;
        btnRecentCombinedTextFile.Enabled = currentSettings.RecentCombinedFiles.Count > 0;
        btnRecentExtractOutputFolder.Enabled = currentSettings.RecentOutputFolders.Count > 0;
    }

    private static void PopulateRecentMenu(ContextMenuStrip menu, List<string> paths, Action<string> onSelect)
    {
        menu.Items.Clear();
        if (paths.Count == 0)
        {
            menu.Items.Add(new ToolStripMenuItem("No recent items") { Enabled = false });
            return;
        }
        foreach (string path in paths)
        {
            ToolStripMenuItem item = new ToolStripMenuItem(path);
            item.Click += (sender, args) => onSelect(path);
            menu.Items.Add(item);
        }
    }

    private static void PopulateRecentToolStripMenu(ToolStripMenuItem menu, List<string> paths, Action<string> onSelect)
    {
        menu.DropDownItems.Clear();
        if (paths.Count == 0)
        {
            menu.DropDownItems.Add(new ToolStripMenuItem("No recent items") { Enabled = false });
            return;
        }
        foreach (string path in paths)
        {
            ToolStripMenuItem item = new ToolStripMenuItem(path);
            item.Click += (sender, args) => onSelect(path);
            menu.DropDownItems.Add(item);
        }
    }
}

  <!-- 
    Microsoft ResX Schema 
    
    Version 2.0
    
    The primary goals of this format is to allow a simple XML format 
    that is mostly human readable. The generation and parsing of the 
    various data types are done through the TypeConverter classes 
    associated with the data types.
    
    Example:
    
    ... ado.net/XML headers & schema ...
    <resheader name="resmimetype">text/microsoft-resx</resheader>
    <resheader name="version">2.0</resheader>
    <resheader name="reader">System.Resources.ResXResourceReader, System.Windows.Forms, ...</resheader>
    <resheader name="writer">System.Resources.ResXResourceWriter, System.Windows.Forms, ...</resheader>
    <data name="Name1"><value>this is my long string</value><comment>this is a comment</comment></data>
    <data name="Color1" type="System.Drawing.Color, System.Drawing">Blue</data>
    <data name="Bitmap1" mimetype="application/x-microsoft.net.object.binary.base64">
        <value>[base64 mime encoded serialized .NET Framework object]</value>
    </data>
    <data name="Icon1" type="System.Drawing.Icon, System.Drawing" mimetype="application/x-microsoft.net.object.bytearray.base64">
        <value>[base64 mime encoded string representing a byte array form of the .NET Framework object]</value>
        <comment>This is a comment</comment>
    </data>
                
    There are any number of "resheader" rows that contain simple 
    name/value pairs.
    
    Each data row contains a name, and value. The row also contains a 
    type or mimetype. Type corresponds to a .NET class that support 
    text/value conversion through the TypeConverter architecture. 
    Classes that don't support this are serialized and stored with the 
    mimetype set.
    
    The mimetype is used for serialized objects, and tells the 
    ResXResourceReader how to depersist the object. This is currently not 
    extensible. For a given mimetype the value must be set accordingly:
    
    Note - application/x-microsoft.net.object.binary.base64 is the format 
    that the ResXResourceWriter will generate, however the reader can 
    read any of the formats listed below.
    
    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.binary.base64
    value   : The object must be serialized with 
            : System.Runtime.Serialization.Formatters.Binary.BinaryFormatter
            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.
    
    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.soap.base64
    value   : The object must be serialized with 
            : System.Runtime.Serialization.Formatters.Soap.SoapFormatter
            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.

    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.bytearray.base64
    value   : The object must be serialized into a byte array 
            : using a System.ComponentModel.TypeConverter
            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.
    -->
  <xsd:schema id="root" xmlns="" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:msdata="urn:schemas-microsoft-com:xml-msdata">
    <xsd:import namespace="http://www.w3.org/XML/1998/namespace" />
    <xsd:element name="root" msdata:IsDataSet="true">
      <xsd:complexType>
        <xsd:choice maxOccurs="unbounded">
          <xsd:element name="metadata">
            <xsd:complexType>
              <xsd:sequence>
                <xsd:element name="value" type="xsd:string" minOccurs="0" />
              </xsd:sequence>
              <xsd:attribute name="name" use="required" type="xsd:string" />
              <xsd:attribute name="type" type="xsd:string" />

using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed partial class MainForm
{
    private void BtnAbout_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        using AboutForm aboutForm = new AboutForm();
        ShowOwnedDialog(aboutForm);
    }

    private void BtnSettings_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        try
        {
            AppThemeMode previousThemeMode = currentSettings.ThemeMode;
            using SettingsForm settingsForm = new SettingsForm(currentSettings);
            if (ShowOwnedDialog(settingsForm) == DialogResult.OK)
            {
                currentSettings = settingsForm.Settings;
                SettingsOperationResult result = SettingsService.SaveWithResult(currentSettings);
                UpdateSafetySummary();
                UpdateStatusForActiveTab("Settings saved.");
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(result.WarningMessage))
                {
                    MessageBox.Show(this, result.WarningMessage + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine + result.SettingsFilePath, "Settings warning", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
                }
                if (previousThemeMode != currentSettings.ThemeMode)
                {
                    DialogResult restartResult = MessageBox.Show(this,
                        "Theme changes require restarting the application." + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine + "Restart now?",
                        "Restart required",
                        MessageBoxButtons.YesNo,
                        MessageBoxIcon.Question);
                    if (restartResult == DialogResult.Yes)
                    {
                        Application.Restart();
                        Close();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowHandledError("Settings", ex);
        }
    }


    private DialogResult ShowOwnedDialog(Form dialog)
    {
        bool restoreTopMost = TopMost;
        try
        {
            dialog.StartPosition = FormStartPosition.CenterParent;
            dialog.ShowInTaskbar = false;
            if (restoreTopMost)
            {
                // Temporarily lower the main topmost window and make the modal dialog topmost.
                // This prevents Settings/About from opening behind the main window when Always on top is enabled.
                TopMost = false;
                dialog.TopMost = true;
            }
            return dialog.ShowDialog(this);
        }
        finally
        {
            if (!IsDisposed)
            {
                TopMost = restoreTopMost;
            }
        }
    }

    private void UpdateSafetySummary()
    {
        string binaryAssetMode = currentSettings.OutputProtocol == CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol.Cptf2LengthDelimited && currentSettings.IncludeImageAssetsInCptf2 ? "included" : "not included";
        lblSafetySummary.Text = $"Safety limits: max {currentSettings.MaxFileCount} files, max {currentSettings.MaxTotalSizeMb} MB total text/binary size, max {currentSettings.MaxSingleFileSizeMb} MB per file. Output protocol: {ProjectFileCombiner.GetOutputProtocolText(currentSettings.OutputProtocol)}. .ico/.png files: {binaryAssetMode}. Theme: {currentSettings.ThemeMode}.";
    }

    private void ChkAlwaysOnTop_CheckedChanged(object? sender, EventArgs e) => TopMost = chkAlwaysOnTop.Checked;
    private void BtnClose_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e) => Close();
}

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<root>
  <!--
    Microsoft ResX Schema
    Version 2.0
    The primary goals of this format is to allow a simple XML format
    that is mostly human readable. The generation and parsing of the
    various data types are done through the TypeConverter classes
    associated with the data types.
    Example:
    ... ado.net/XML headers & schema ...
    <resheader name="resmimetype">text/microsoft-resx</resheader>
    <resheader name="version">2.0</resheader>
    <resheader name="reader">System.Resources.ResXResourceReader, System.Windows.Forms, ...</resheader>
    <resheader name="writer">System.Resources.ResXResourceWriter, System.Windows.Forms, ...</resheader>
    <data name="Name1"><value>this is my long string</value><comment>this is a comment</comment></data>
    <data name="Color1" type="System.Drawing.Color, System.Drawing">Blue</data>
    <data name="Bitmap1" mimetype="application/x-microsoft.net.object.binary.base64">
        <value>[base64 mime encoded serialized .NET Framework object]</value>
    </data>
    <data name="Icon1" type="System.Drawing.Icon, System.Drawing" mimetype="application/x-microsoft.net.object.bytearray.base64">
        <value>[base64 mime encoded string representing a byte array form of the .NET Framework object]</value>
        <comment>This is a comment</comment>
    </data>
    There are any number of "resheader" rows that contain simple
    name/value pairs.
    Each data row contains a name, and value. The row also contains a
    type or mimetype. Type corresponds to a .NET class that support
    text/value conversion through the TypeConverter architecture.
    Classes that don't support this are serialized and stored with the
    mimetype set.
    The mimetype is used for serialized objects, and tells the
    ResXResourceReader how to depersist the object. This is currently not
    extensible. For a given mimetype the value must be set accordingly:
    Note - application/x-microsoft.net.object.binary.base64 is the format
    that the ResXResourceWriter will generate, however the reader can
    read any of the formats listed below.
    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.binary.base64
    value   : The object must be serialized with
            : System.Runtime.Serialization.Formatters.Binary.BinaryFormatter
            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.
    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.soap.base64
    value   : The object must be serialized with
            : System.Runtime.Serialization.Formatters.Soap.SoapFormatter
            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.
    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.bytearray.base64
    value   : The object must be serialized into a byte array
            : using a System.ComponentModel.TypeConverter
            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.
    -->
  <xsd:schema id="root" xmlns="" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:msdata="urn:schemas-microsoft-com:xml-msdata">

using System.Diagnostics;
using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed partial class MainForm
{
    private void OpenFile(string filePath)
    {
        try
        {
            ProcessStartInfo processStartInfo = new ProcessStartInfo { FileName = filePath, UseShellExecute = true };
            Process.Start(processStartInfo);
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowHandledError("Open file", ex);
        }
    }

    private void OpenFolder(string folderPath)
    {
        try
        {
            ProcessStartInfo processStartInfo = new ProcessStartInfo { FileName = folderPath, UseShellExecute = true };
            Process.Start(processStartInfo);
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowHandledError("Open folder", ex);
        }
    }

    private void UpdateStatusForActiveTab(string text)
    {
        if (tabControl.SelectedTab == tabExtract)
        {
            lblExtractStatus.Text = text;
        }
        else
        {
            UpdateStatus(text);
        }
    }

    private void UpdateStatus(string text) => lblStatus.Text = text;
    private void AppendExtractLogText(string text) => txtExtractLog.AppendText(text + Environment.NewLine);
    private void ShowHandledError(string operationName, Exception exception)
    {
        HandledErrorInfo error = HandledErrorService.FromException(exception, operationName);
        UpdateStatusForActiveTab(error.Message);
        if (tabControl.SelectedTab == tabExtract)
        {
            AppendExtractLogText("[ERROR] " + error.Message);
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(error.Detail))
            {
                AppendExtractLogText("        " + error.Detail.Replace(Environment.NewLine, Environment.NewLine + "        "));
            }
        }
        MessageBox.Show(this, error.Message, error.Title, MessageBoxButtons.OK, error.IsHandled ? MessageBoxIcon.Warning : MessageBoxIcon.Error);
    }

    private static string BuildCombineDiagnosticsStatus(CombineResult result)
    {
        string protocol = ProjectFileCombiner.GetOutputProtocolText(result.OutputProtocol);
        string hash = ShortHash(result.OutputFileSha256);
        string status = $"Done in {result.Duration.TotalSeconds:0.000} s. Protocol: {protocol}. Files: {result.CombinedFileCount} ({result.TextFileCount} text, {result.BinaryFileCount} binary). Output: {FormatByteSize(result.OutputFileByteLength)}. SHA-256: {hash}.";
        if (result.EncodingWarningCount > 0)
        {
            status += $" Warning: {result.EncodingWarningCount} file(s) required fallback decoding from strict UTF-8.";
        }
        return status;
    }

    private static string BuildExtractDiagnosticsStatus(RestoreResult result, bool validateOnly)
    {
        string action = validateOnly ? "Validation completed" : "Extraction completed";
        string protocol = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(result.ProtocolName) ? "unknown protocol" : result.ProtocolName;
        string hashSummary = result.Sha256VerificationCount > 0 ? $", SHA-256 checks: {result.Sha256VerificationCount}" : string.Empty;
        return validateOnly
            ? $"{action}. Protocol: {protocol}. Files: {result.TotalFileCount} ({result.TextFileCount} text, {result.BinaryFileCount} binary), planned: {result.FilesPlanned}, skipped: {result.FilesSkipped}{hashSummary}. No files were written."
            : $"{action}. Protocol: {protocol}. Created {result.FilesCreated}, skipped {result.FilesSkipped}. Files: {result.TotalFileCount} ({result.TextFileCount} text, {result.BinaryFileCount} binary){hashSummary}.";
    }

    private static string BuildExtractDiagnosticsMessage(RestoreResult result, bool validateOnly)
    {
        string status = BuildExtractDiagnosticsStatus(result, validateOnly);
        return validateOnly
            ? status + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine + "No files were written."
            : status;
    }

    private static string FormatByteSize(long byteCount)
    {
        const double kb = 1024;
        const double mb = kb * 1024;
        const double gb = mb * 1024;
        if (byteCount >= gb) return (byteCount / gb).ToString("0.00") + " GB";
        if (byteCount >= mb) return (byteCount / mb).ToString("0.00") + " MB";
        if (byteCount >= kb) return (byteCount / kb).ToString("0.00") + " KB";
        return byteCount.ToString("N0") + " bytes";
    }

    private static string ShortHash(string sha256)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(sha256)) return "n/a";
        return sha256.Length <= 12 ? sha256 : sha256.Substring(0, 12);
    }
}

using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed partial class MainForm
{
    private CombinedFileValidationOptions BuildCombinedFileValidationOptions(string intendedOutputRoot)
    {
        return new CombinedFileValidationOptions
        {
            IntendedOutputRoot = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(intendedOutputRoot) ? Environment.CurrentDirectory : intendedOutputRoot,
            ValidateSafePaths = true,
            ValidateHashes = true,
            ValidateBinaryBase64 = true,
            DetectDuplicatePaths = true,
            ValidateWindowsFileNameChars = true,
            RejectEmptyPathSegments = true,
            RejectTrailingSpacesOrDots = true,
            PreflightTargetContainment = true
        };
    }

    private static string BuildCompactValidationStatus(CombinedFileValidationResult validationResult)
    {
        string protocolSuffix = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(validationResult.ProtocolVersion)
            ? validationResult.Protocol
            : $"{validationResult.Protocol} v{validationResult.ProtocolVersion}";
        string embeddedIndexStatus = validationResult.EmbeddedIndexPresent
            ? $"embedded index present, valid {validationResult.EmbeddedIndexValid}, used {validationResult.EmbeddedIndexUsed}"
            : "embedded index absent";
        return validationResult.IsValid
            ? $"Verification passed: {protocolSuffix}, files {validationResult.ParsedFileCount:N0} (content {validationResult.ContentFileCount:N0}, internal {validationResult.InternalFileCount:N0}), text {validationResult.TextFileCount:N0}, binary {validationResult.BinaryFileCount:N0}, SHA-256 failures {validationResult.Sha256FailureCount:N0}, Base64 failures {validationResult.Base64FailureCount:N0}, path failures {validationResult.PathFailureCount:N0}, duplicate paths {validationResult.DuplicateRelativePathCount + validationResult.DuplicateTargetPathCount:N0}, {embeddedIndexStatus}."
            : $"Verification failed: {protocolSuffix}, errors {validationResult.ErrorCount:N0}, metadata failures {validationResult.MetadataFailureCount:N0}, payload failures {validationResult.PayloadFailureCount:N0}, SHA-256 failures {validationResult.Sha256FailureCount:N0}, Base64 failures {validationResult.Base64FailureCount:N0}, path failures {validationResult.PathFailureCount:N0}, duplicate paths {validationResult.DuplicateRelativePathCount + validationResult.DuplicateTargetPathCount:N0}, {embeddedIndexStatus}.";
    }

    private static string BuildValidationFailureMessage(CombinedFileValidationResult validationResult)
    {
        IEnumerable<string> issueLines = validationResult.Issues
            .Where(issue => issue.Severity == CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity.Error)
            .Take(8)
            .Select(issue => string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(issue.RelativePath) ? $"- {issue.Message}" : $"- {issue.RelativePath}: {issue.Message}");
        string details = string.Join(Environment.NewLine, issueLines);
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(details))
        {
            details = "- Validation failed without detailed issue text.";
        }
        return "The combined file did not pass validation." + Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine + details;
    }

    private void AppendValidationIssuesToExtractLog(CombinedFileValidationResult validationResult)
    {
        foreach (CombinedFileValidationIssue issue in validationResult.Issues.Take(10))
        {
            string prefix = issue.Severity == CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity.Error ? "[ERROR]" : issue.Severity == CombinedFileValidationIssueSeverity.Warning ? "[WARN ]" : "[INFO ]";
            string pathText = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(issue.RelativePath) ? string.Empty : issue.RelativePath + ": ";
            AppendExtractLogText(prefix + " " + pathText + issue.Message);
        }
    }
}

using System.Threading;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal static class Program
{
    [STAThread]
    private static void Main()
    {
        Application.SetUnhandledExceptionMode(UnhandledExceptionMode.CatchException);
        Application.ThreadException += Application_ThreadException;
        AppDomain.CurrentDomain.UnhandledException += CurrentDomain_UnhandledException;
        TaskScheduler.UnobservedTaskException += TaskScheduler_UnobservedTaskException;
        try
        {
            AppSettings settings = SettingsService.Load();
#pragma warning disable WFO5001
            Application.SetColorMode(MapThemeMode(settings.ThemeMode));
#pragma warning restore WFO5001
            ApplicationConfiguration.Initialize();
            MainForm mainForm = new MainForm();
            ApplyApplicationIcon(mainForm);
            Application.Run(mainForm);
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            ShowStartupError(ex);
        }
    }

    private static void Application_ThreadException(object sender, ThreadExceptionEventArgs e)
    {
        ShowStartupError(e.Exception);
    }

    private static void CurrentDomain_UnhandledException(object sender, UnhandledExceptionEventArgs e)
    {
        if (e.ExceptionObject is Exception exception)
        {
            ShowStartupError(exception);
        }
    }

    private static void TaskScheduler_UnobservedTaskException(object? sender, UnobservedTaskExceptionEventArgs e)
    {
        e.SetObserved();
        ShowStartupError(e.Exception);
    }

    private static void ShowStartupError(Exception exception)
    {
        HandledErrorInfo error = HandledErrorService.FromException(exception, "Application");
        MessageBox.Show(error.Message, error.Title, MessageBoxButtons.OK, error.IsHandled ? MessageBoxIcon.Warning : MessageBoxIcon.Error);
    }
#pragma warning disable WFO5001
    private static SystemColorMode MapThemeMode(AppThemeMode themeMode)
    {
        return themeMode switch
        {
            AppThemeMode.Light => SystemColorMode.Classic,
            AppThemeMode.Dark => SystemColorMode.Dark,
            _ => SystemColorMode.System
        };
    }
#pragma warning restore WFO5001
    internal static void ApplyApplicationIcon(Form form)
    {
        try
        {
            string[] candidateIconPaths =
            {
                Path.Combine(AppContext.BaseDirectory, "app.ico"),
                Path.Combine(AppContext.BaseDirectory, "Resources", "app.ico"),
                Path.Combine(AppDomain.CurrentDomain.BaseDirectory, "app.ico")
            };
            string? iconPath = candidateIconPaths.FirstOrDefault(File.Exists);
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(iconPath))
            {
                form.Icon = new Icon(iconPath);
            }
        }
        catch
        {
            // Icon loading is cosmetic and should never block application startup.
        }
    }
}

using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed class SettingsForm : Form
{
    private readonly NumericUpDown nudMaxFileCount;
    private readonly NumericUpDown nudMaxTotalSizeMb;
    private readonly NumericUpDown nudMaxSingleFileSizeMb;
    private readonly ComboBox cboOutputProtocol;
    private readonly CheckBox chkIncludeImageAssetsInCptf2;
    private readonly ComboBox cboThemeMode;
    internal AppSettings Settings { get; }
    internal SettingsForm(AppSettings settings)
    {
        Settings = new AppSettings();
        Settings.MaxFileCount = settings.MaxFileCount;
        Settings.MaxTotalSizeMb = settings.MaxTotalSizeMb;
        Settings.MaxSingleFileSizeMb = settings.MaxSingleFileSizeMb;
        Settings.ThemeMode = settings.ThemeMode;
        Settings.OutputProtocol = settings.OutputProtocol;
        Settings.IncludeImageAssetsInCptf2 = settings.IncludeImageAssetsInCptf2;
        Text = "Settings";
        StartPosition = FormStartPosition.CenterParent;
        FormBorderStyle = FormBorderStyle.FixedDialog;
        MaximizeBox = false;
        MinimizeBox = false;
        ShowInTaskbar = false;
        ClientSize = new Size(640, 400);
        TableLayoutPanel layout = new TableLayoutPanel();
        layout.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        layout.Padding = new Padding(12);
        layout.ColumnCount = 2;
        layout.RowCount = 10;
        layout.ColumnStyles.Add(new ColumnStyle(SizeType.Percent, 58F));
        layout.ColumnStyles.Add(new ColumnStyle(SizeType.Percent, 42F));
        for (int rowIndex = 0; rowIndex < 9; rowIndex++)
        {
            layout.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.AutoSize));
        }
        layout.RowStyles.Add(new RowStyle(SizeType.Percent, 100F));
        Label lblMaxFileCount = CreateLabel("Max number of files");
        nudMaxFileCount = CreateNumberBox(settings.MaxFileCount, 1, 100000);
        Label lblMaxTotalSizeMb = CreateLabel("Max total text/binary size (MB)");
        nudMaxTotalSizeMb = CreateNumberBox(settings.MaxTotalSizeMb, 1, 100000);
        Label lblMaxSingleFileSizeMb = CreateLabel("Max single file size (MB)");
        nudMaxSingleFileSizeMb = CreateNumberBox(settings.MaxSingleFileSizeMb, 1, 100000);
        Label lblOutputProtocol = CreateLabel("Combine output protocol");
        cboOutputProtocol = new ComboBox();
        cboOutputProtocol.DropDownStyle = ComboBoxStyle.DropDownList;
        cboOutputProtocol.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        cboOutputProtocol.Items.Add(AppConstants.Cptf1HumanReadableName + " - classic readable text format");
        cboOutputProtocol.Items.Add(AppConstants.Cptf2LengthDelimitedName + " - byteLength + SHA-256");
        cboOutputProtocol.SelectedIndex = settings.OutputProtocol == CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol.Cptf2LengthDelimited ? 1 : 0;
        cboOutputProtocol.SelectedIndexChanged += CboOutputProtocol_SelectedIndexChanged;
        chkIncludeImageAssetsInCptf2 = new CheckBox();
        chkIncludeImageAssetsInCptf2.Text = "Include .ico and .png files in CPTF/2 exports";
        chkIncludeImageAssetsInCptf2.AutoSize = true;
        chkIncludeImageAssetsInCptf2.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        chkIncludeImageAssetsInCptf2.Checked = settings.IncludeImageAssetsInCptf2;
        layout.SetColumnSpan(chkIncludeImageAssetsInCptf2, 2);
        Label lblProtocolNote = new Label();
        lblProtocolNote.Text = "Image assets are included only with CPTF/2 LengthDelimited and are restored as binary files. Extract auto-detects the protocol.";
        lblProtocolNote.AutoSize = true;
        lblProtocolNote.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        lblProtocolNote.Margin = new Padding(0, 4, 0, 8);
        layout.SetColumnSpan(lblProtocolNote, 2);
        Label lblThemeMode = CreateLabel("Theme");
        cboThemeMode = new ComboBox();
        cboThemeMode.DropDownStyle = ComboBoxStyle.DropDownList;
        cboThemeMode.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        cboThemeMode.Items.Add("System default");
        cboThemeMode.Items.Add("Light");
        cboThemeMode.Items.Add("Dark");
        cboThemeMode.SelectedIndex = settings.ThemeMode switch
        {
            AppThemeMode.Light => 1,
            AppThemeMode.Dark => 2,
            _ => 0
        };
        Label lblRestartNote = new Label();
        lblRestartNote.Text = "Theme changes are applied after restarting the application.";
        lblRestartNote.AutoSize = true;
        lblRestartNote.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        lblRestartNote.Margin = new Padding(0, 8, 0, 8);
        layout.SetColumnSpan(lblRestartNote, 2);
        FlowLayoutPanel buttonLayout = new FlowLayoutPanel();
        buttonLayout.FlowDirection = FlowDirection.RightToLeft;
        buttonLayout.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        buttonLayout.AutoSize = true;
        layout.SetColumnSpan(buttonLayout, 2);
        Button btnCancel = new Button();
        btnCancel.Text = "Cancel";
        btnCancel.AutoSize = true;
        btnCancel.Click += BtnCancel_Click;
        Button btnOk = new Button();
        btnOk.Text = "OK";
        btnOk.AutoSize = true;
        btnOk.Click += BtnOk_Click;
        buttonLayout.Controls.Add(btnCancel);
        buttonLayout.Controls.Add(btnOk);
        layout.Controls.Add(lblMaxFileCount, 0, 0);
        layout.Controls.Add(nudMaxFileCount, 1, 0);
        layout.Controls.Add(lblMaxTotalSizeMb, 0, 1);
        layout.Controls.Add(nudMaxTotalSizeMb, 1, 1);
        layout.Controls.Add(lblMaxSingleFileSizeMb, 0, 2);
        layout.Controls.Add(nudMaxSingleFileSizeMb, 1, 2);
        layout.Controls.Add(lblOutputProtocol, 0, 3);
        layout.Controls.Add(cboOutputProtocol, 1, 3);
        layout.Controls.Add(chkIncludeImageAssetsInCptf2, 0, 4);
        layout.Controls.Add(lblProtocolNote, 0, 5);
        layout.Controls.Add(lblThemeMode, 0, 6);
        layout.Controls.Add(cboThemeMode, 1, 6);
        layout.Controls.Add(lblRestartNote, 0, 7);
        layout.Controls.Add(buttonLayout, 0, 8);
        Controls.Add(layout);
        AcceptButton = btnOk;
        CancelButton = btnCancel;
        UpdateImageAssetCheckBoxState();
    }

    private static Label CreateLabel(string text)
    {
        Label label = new Label();
        label.Text = text;
        label.AutoSize = true;
        label.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        label.Margin = new Padding(0, 5, 8, 8);
        return label;
    }

    private static NumericUpDown CreateNumberBox(int value, int minimum, int maximum)
    {
        NumericUpDown numericUpDown = new NumericUpDown();
        numericUpDown.Minimum = minimum;
        numericUpDown.Maximum = maximum;
        numericUpDown.Value = Math.Clamp(value, minimum, maximum);
        numericUpDown.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
        return numericUpDown;
    }

    private void CboOutputProtocol_SelectedIndexChanged(object? sender, EventArgs e) => UpdateImageAssetCheckBoxState();
    private void UpdateImageAssetCheckBoxState()
    {
        chkIncludeImageAssetsInCptf2.Enabled = cboOutputProtocol.SelectedIndex == 1;
    }

    private void BtnOk_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        Settings.MaxFileCount = (int)nudMaxFileCount.Value;
        Settings.MaxTotalSizeMb = (int)nudMaxTotalSizeMb.Value;
        Settings.MaxSingleFileSizeMb = (int)nudMaxSingleFileSizeMb.Value;
        Settings.OutputProtocol = cboOutputProtocol.SelectedIndex == 1 ? CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol.Cptf2LengthDelimited : CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol.Cptf1HumanReadable;
        Settings.IncludeImageAssetsInCptf2 = chkIncludeImageAssetsInCptf2.Checked;
        Settings.ThemeMode = cboThemeMode.SelectedIndex switch
        {
            1 => AppThemeMode.Light,
            2 => AppThemeMode.Dark,
            _ => AppThemeMode.System
        };
        DialogResult = DialogResult.OK;
        Close();
    }

    private void BtnCancel_Click(object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        DialogResult = DialogResult.Cancel;
        Close();
    }
}

using System.Text.Json;
using System.Text.Json.Serialization;
using TextFileCombiner.Core;

namespace TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10;

internal sealed class SettingsOperationResult
{
    internal AppSettings Settings { get; set; } = new AppSettings();
    internal string SettingsFilePath { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    internal bool UsedFallbackLocation { get; set; }
    internal string WarningMessage { get; set; } = string.Empty;
}

internal static class SettingsService
{
    private const string SettingsFileName = "TextFileCombiner.settings.json";
    private static readonly JsonSerializerOptions SerializerOptions = new JsonSerializerOptions
    {
        WriteIndented = true
    };
    static SettingsService()
    {
        SerializerOptions.Converters.Add(new JsonStringEnumConverter());
    }

    internal static string PrimarySettingsFilePath
    {
        get
        {
            return Path.Combine(AppContext.BaseDirectory, SettingsFileName);
        }
    }

    internal static string FallbackSettingsFilePath
    {
        get
        {
            string appDataFolder = Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.ApplicationData);
            return Path.Combine(appDataFolder, "TextFileCombiner", SettingsFileName);
        }
    }

    internal static AppSettings Load()
    {
        return LoadWithResult().Settings;
    }

    internal static SettingsOperationResult LoadWithResult()
    {
        SettingsOperationResult primaryResult = TryLoadFromPath(PrimarySettingsFilePath, false);
        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(primaryResult.WarningMessage))
        {
            return primaryResult;
        }
        SettingsOperationResult fallbackResult = TryLoadFromPath(FallbackSettingsFilePath, true);
        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(fallbackResult.WarningMessage))
        {
            fallbackResult.WarningMessage = "Settings could not be loaded or saved next to the application. The user profile settings location is being used instead.";
            return fallbackResult;
        }
        SettingsOperationResult defaultResult = new SettingsOperationResult();
        defaultResult.Settings = new AppSettings();
        defaultResult.SettingsFilePath = FallbackSettingsFilePath;
        defaultResult.UsedFallbackLocation = true;
        defaultResult.WarningMessage = "Settings could not be loaded from either settings location. Defaults are being used.";
        return defaultResult;
    }

    internal static SettingsOperationResult SaveWithResult(AppSettings settings)
    {
        Normalize(settings);
        SettingsOperationResult primaryResult = TrySaveToPath(settings, PrimarySettingsFilePath, false);
        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(primaryResult.WarningMessage))
        {
            return primaryResult;
        }
        SettingsOperationResult fallbackResult = TrySaveToPath(settings, FallbackSettingsFilePath, true);
        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(fallbackResult.WarningMessage))
        {
            fallbackResult.WarningMessage = "Settings could not be saved next to the application. They were saved to the user profile instead.";
            return fallbackResult;
        }
        fallbackResult.WarningMessage = "Settings could not be saved to either settings location.";
        return fallbackResult;
    }

    internal static void Save(AppSettings settings)
    {
        SettingsOperationResult result = SaveWithResult(settings);
        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(result.WarningMessage) && !File.Exists(result.SettingsFilePath))
        {
            // Keep the original void API non-throwing for startup/theme usage.
        }
    }

    private static SettingsOperationResult TryLoadFromPath(string settingsFilePath, bool isFallback)
    {
        SettingsOperationResult result = new SettingsOperationResult();
        result.SettingsFilePath = settingsFilePath;
        result.UsedFallbackLocation = isFallback;
        try
        {
            if (!File.Exists(settingsFilePath))
            {
                AppSettings defaultSettings = new AppSettings();
                SettingsOperationResult saveResult = TrySaveToPath(defaultSettings, settingsFilePath, isFallback);
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(saveResult.WarningMessage))
                {
                    result.WarningMessage = saveResult.WarningMessage;
                    return result;
                }
                result.Settings = defaultSettings;
                return result;
            }
            string json = File.ReadAllText(settingsFilePath);
            AppSettings? loadedSettings = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<AppSettings>(json, SerializerOptions);
            if (loadedSettings is null)
            {
                result.WarningMessage = "The settings file is empty or invalid.";
                return result;
            }
            Normalize(loadedSettings);
            result.Settings = loadedSettings;
            return result;
        }
        catch (IOException ex)
        {
            result.WarningMessage = ex.Message;
            return result;
        }
        catch (UnauthorizedAccessException ex)
        {
            result.WarningMessage = ex.Message;
            return result;
        }
        catch (JsonException ex)
        {
            result.WarningMessage = ex.Message;
            return result;
        }
        catch (NotSupportedException ex)
        {
            result.WarningMessage = ex.Message;
            return result;
        }
    }

    private static SettingsOperationResult TrySaveToPath(AppSettings settings, string settingsFilePath, bool isFallback)
    {
        SettingsOperationResult result = new SettingsOperationResult();
        result.Settings = settings;
        result.SettingsFilePath = settingsFilePath;
        result.UsedFallbackLocation = isFallback;
        try
        {
            string? directory = Path.GetDirectoryName(settingsFilePath);
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(directory))
            {
                Directory.CreateDirectory(directory);
            }
            string json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(settings, SerializerOptions);
            File.WriteAllText(settingsFilePath, json);
            return result;
        }
        catch (IOException ex)
        {
            result.WarningMessage = ex.Message;
            return result;
        }
        catch (UnauthorizedAccessException ex)
        {
            result.WarningMessage = ex.Message;
            return result;
        }
        catch (NotSupportedException ex)
        {
            result.WarningMessage = ex.Message;
            return result;
        }
    }

    private static void Normalize(AppSettings settings)
    {
        if (settings.MaxFileCount < 1)
        {
            settings.MaxFileCount = 1;
        }
        if (settings.MaxTotalSizeMb < 1)
        {
            settings.MaxTotalSizeMb = 1;
        }
        if (settings.MaxSingleFileSizeMb < 1)
        {
            settings.MaxSingleFileSizeMb = 1;
        }
        if (!Enum.IsDefined(settings.ThemeMode))
        {
            settings.ThemeMode = AppThemeMode.System;
        }
        if (!Enum.IsDefined(settings.OutputProtocol))
        {
            settings.OutputProtocol = CombinedProjectTextFileProtocol.Cptf1HumanReadable;
        }
        settings.RecentSourcePaths = NormalizeRecentList(settings.RecentSourcePaths);
        settings.RecentCombinedFiles = NormalizeRecentList(settings.RecentCombinedFiles);
        settings.RecentOutputFolders = NormalizeRecentList(settings.RecentOutputFolders);
        settings.RecentOutputFiles = NormalizeRecentList(settings.RecentOutputFiles);
    }

    private static List<string> NormalizeRecentList(List<string>? values)
    {
        if (values is null)
        {
            return new List<string>();
        }
        return values
            .Where(value => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
            .Select(value => value.Trim())
            .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .Take(10)
            .ToList();
    }
}

END FILE

<!--

    MainForm is built mostly in code rather than by the visual WinForms designer.

    Visual Studio may create MainForm*.resx files after opening the designer.

    If embedded, those files can collide as TextFileCombiner.WinForms.Net10.MainForm.resources.

    Keep MainForm source files as code files and explicitly prevent generated MainForm resource files

    from becoming EmbeddedResource items.

  -->
